l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-01 THE PATCHWORK GIRL OF OZ BY L. FRANK BAUM AFFECTIONATELY DEDICATED TO MY YOUNG FRIEND SUMNER HAMILTON BRITTON OF CHICAGO PROLOGUE THROUGH THE KINDNESS OF DOROTHY GALE OF KANSAS AFTERWARD PRINCESS DOROTHY OF OZ AN HUMBLE WRITER IN THE UNITED STATES OF AMERICA WAS ONCE APPOINTED ROYAL HISTORIAN OF OZ WITH THE PRIVILEGE OF WRITING THE CHRONICLE OF THAT WONDERFUL FAIRYLAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-02 BUT AFTER MAKING SIX BOOKS ABOUT THE ADVENTURES OF THOSE INTERESTING BUT QUEER PEOPLE WHO LIVE IN THE LAND OF OZ THE HISTORIAN LEARNED WITH SORROW THAT BY AN EDICT OF THE SUPREME RULER OZMA OF OZ HER COUNTRY WOULD THEREAFTER BE RENDERED INVISIBLE TO ALL WHO LIVED OUTSIDE ITS BORDERS AND THAT ALL COMMUNICATION WITH OZ WOULD IN THE FUTURE BE CUT OFF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-03 THE CHILDREN WHO HAD LEARNED TO LOOK FOR THE BOOKS ABOUT OZ AND WHO LOVED THE STORIES ABOUT THE GAY AND HAPPY PEOPLE INHABITING THAT FAVORED COUNTRY WERE AS SORRY AS THEIR HISTORIAN THAT THERE WOULD BE NO MORE BOOKS OF OZ STORIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-04 THEY WROTE MANY LETTERS ASKING IF THE HISTORIAN DID NOT KNOW OF SOME ADVENTURES TO WRITE ABOUT THAT HAD HAPPENED BEFORE THE LAND OF OZ WAS SHUT OUT FROM ALL THE REST OF THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-05 BUT HE DID NOT KNOW OF ANY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-06 FINALLY ONE OF THE CHILDREN INQUIRED WHY WE COULDN'T HEAR FROM PRINCESS DOROTHY BY WIRELESS TELEGRAPH WHICH WOULD ENABLE HER TO COMMUNICATE TO THE HISTORIAN WHATEVER HAPPENED IN THE FAR OFF LAND OF OZ WITHOUT HIS SEEING HER OR EVEN KNOWING JUST WHERE OZ IS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-07 THAT SEEMED A GOOD IDEA,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-08 SO THE HISTORIAN RIGGED UP A HIGH TOWER IN HIS BACK YARD AND TOOK LESSONS IN WIRELESS TELEGRAPHY UNTIL HE UNDERSTOOD IT AND THEN BEGAN TO CALL PRINCESS DOROTHY OF OZ BY SENDING MESSAGES INTO THE AIR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-09 NOW IT WASN'T LIKELY THAT DOROTHY WOULD BE LOOKING FOR WIRELESS MESSAGES OR WOULD HEED THE CALL,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-10 BUT ONE THING THE HISTORIAN WAS SURE OF AND THAT WAS THAT THE POWERFUL SORCERESS GLINDA WOULD KNOW WHAT HE WAS DOING AND THAT HE DESIRED TO COMMUNICATE WITH DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-11 FOR GLINDA HAS A BIG BOOK IN WHICH IS RECORDED EVERY EVENT THAT TAKES PLACE ANYWHERE IN THE WORLD JUST THE MOMENT THAT IT HAPPENS AND SO OF COURSE THE BOOK WOULD TELL HER ABOUT THE WIRELESS MESSAGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-12 AND THAT WAS THE WAY DOROTHY HEARD THAT THE HISTORIAN WANTED TO SPEAK WITH HER AND THERE WAS A SHAGGY MAN IN THE LAND OF OZ WHO KNEW HOW TO TELEGRAPH A WIRELESS REPLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-13 THE RESULT WAS THAT THE HISTORIAN BEGGED SO HARD TO BE TOLD THE LATEST NEWS OF OZ SO THAT HE COULD WRITE IT DOWN FOR THE CHILDREN TO READ THAT DOROTHY ASKED PERMISSION OF OZMA AND OZMA GRACIOUSLY CONSENTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-14 THAT IS WHY AFTER TWO LONG YEARS OF WAITING ANOTHER OZ STORY IS NOW PRESENTED TO THE CHILDREN OF AMERICA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-15 THIS WOULD NOT HAVE BEEN POSSIBLE HAD NOT SOME CLEVER MAN INVENTED THE WIRELESS AND AN EQUALLY CLEVER CHILD SUGGESTED THE IDEA OF REACHING THE MYSTERIOUS LAND OF OZ BY ITS MEANS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-16 L. FRANK BAUM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-17 OZCOT AT HOLLYWOOD IN CALIFORNIA THE PATCHWORK GIRL OF OZ CHAPTER ONE OJO AND UNC NUNKIE WHERE'S THE BUTTER UNC NUNKIE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-18 ASKED OJO. UNC LOOKED OUT OF THE WINDOW AND STROKED HIS LONG BEARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-19 THEN HE TURNED TO THE MUNCHKIN BOY AND SHOOK HIS HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-20 ISN'T SAID HE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-21 ISN'T ANY BUTTER?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-22 THAT'S TOO BAD UNC. WHERE'S THE JAM THEN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-23 INQUIRED OJO STANDING ON A STOOL SO HE COULD LOOK THROUGH ALL THE SHELVES OF THE CUPBOARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-24 BUT UNC NUNKIE SHOOK HIS HEAD AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-25 GONE HE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-26 NO JAM EITHER?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-27 AND NO CAKE NO JELLY NO APPLES NOTHING BUT BREAD?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-28 ALL SAID UNC AGAIN STROKING HIS BEARD AS HE GAZED FROM THE WINDOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-29 THE LITTLE BOY BROUGHT THE STOOL AND SAT BESIDE HIS UNCLE MUNCHING THE DRY BREAD SLOWLY AND SEEMING IN DEEP THOUGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-30 NOTHING GROWS IN OUR YARD BUT THE BREAD TREE HE MUSED AND THERE ARE ONLY TWO MORE LOAVES ON THAT TREE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-31 AND THEY'RE NOT RIPE YET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-32 TELL ME UNC,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-33 WHY ARE WE SO POOR?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-34 THE OLD MUNCHKIN TURNED AND LOOKED AT OJO. HE HAD KINDLY EYES BUT HE HADN'T SMILED OR LAUGHED IN SO LONG THAT THE BOY HAD FORGOTTEN THAT UNC NUNKIE COULD LOOK ANY OTHER WAY THAN SOLEMN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-35 AND UNC NEVER SPOKE ANY MORE WORDS THAN HE WAS OBLIGED TO SO HIS LITTLE NEPHEW WHO LIVED ALONE WITH HIM HAD LEARNED TO UNDERSTAND A GREAT DEAL FROM ONE WORD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-36 WHY ARE WE SO POOR UNC?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-37 REPEATED THE BOY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-38 NOT SAID THE OLD MUNCHKIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-39 I THINK WE ARE DECLARED OJO. WHAT HAVE WE GOT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-40 I KNOW,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-41 BUT EVERYONE IN THE LAND OF OZ HAS A PLACE TO LIVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-42 WHAT ELSE UNC?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-43 BREAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-44 I'M EATING THE LAST LOAF THAT'S RIPE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-45 THERE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-46 I'VE PUT ASIDE YOUR SHARE UNC. IT'S ON THE TABLE SO YOU CAN EAT IT WHEN YOU GET HUNGRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-47 BUT WHEN THAT IS GONE WHAT SHALL WE EAT UNC?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-48 THE OLD MAN SHIFTED IN HIS CHAIR BUT MERELY SHOOK HIS HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-49 OF COURSE SAID OJO WHO WAS OBLIGED TO TALK BECAUSE HIS UNCLE WOULD NOT NO ONE STARVES IN THE LAND OF OZ EITHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-50 THERE IS PLENTY FOR EVERYONE YOU KNOW,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-51 ONLY IF IT ISN'T JUST WHERE YOU HAPPEN TO BE YOU MUST GO WHERE IT IS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-52 THE AGED MUNCHKIN WRIGGLED AGAIN AND STARED AT HIS SMALL NEPHEW AS IF DISTURBED BY HIS ARGUMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-53 BY TO MORROW MORNING THE BOY WENT ON WE MUST GO WHERE THERE IS SOMETHING TO EAT OR WE SHALL GROW VERY HUNGRY AND BECOME VERY UNHAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-54 WHERE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-55 ASKED UNC. WHERE SHALL WE GO?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-56 I DON'T KNOW I'M SURE REPLIED OJO. BUT YOU MUST KNOW UNC. YOU MUST HAVE TRAVELED IN YOUR TIME BECAUSE YOU'RE SO OLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-57 I DON'T REMEMBER IT BECAUSE EVER SINCE I COULD REMEMBER ANYTHING WE'VE LIVED RIGHT HERE IN THIS LONESOME ROUND HOUSE WITH A LITTLE GARDEN BACK OF IT AND THE THICK WOODS ALL AROUND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-58 ALL I'VE EVER SEEN OF THE GREAT LAND OF OZ UNC DEAR IS THE VIEW OF THAT MOUNTAIN OVER AT THE SOUTH WHERE THEY SAY THE HAMMERHEADS LIVE WHO WON'T LET ANYBODY GO BY THEM AND THAT MOUNTAIN AT THE NORTH WHERE THEY SAY NOBODY LIVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-59 ONE DECLARED UNC CORRECTING HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-60 OH YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-61 ONE FAMILY LIVES THERE I'VE HEARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-62 THAT'S THE CROOKED MAGICIAN WHO IS NAMED DOCTOR PIPT AND HIS WIFE MARGOLOTTE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-63 ONE YEAR YOU TOLD ME ABOUT THEM,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-64 I THINK IT TOOK YOU A WHOLE YEAR UNC TO SAY AS MUCH AS I'VE JUST SAID ABOUT THE CROOKED MAGICIAN AND HIS WIFE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-65 THEY LIVE HIGH UP ON THE MOUNTAIN AND THE GOOD MUNCHKIN COUNTRY WHERE THE FRUITS AND FLOWERS GROW IS JUST THE OTHER SIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-66 IT'S FUNNY YOU AND I SHOULD LIVE HERE ALL ALONE IN THE MIDDLE OF THE FOREST ISN'T IT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-67 YES SAID UNC. THEN LET'S GO AWAY AND VISIT THE MUNCHKIN COUNTRY AND ITS JOLLY GOOD NATURED PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-68 I'D LOVE TO GET A SIGHT OF SOMETHING BESIDES WOODS UNC NUNKIE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-69 TOO LITTLE SAID UNC. WHY I'M NOT SO LITTLE AS I USED TO BE ANSWERED THE BOY EARNESTLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-70 I THINK I CAN WALK AS FAR AND AS FAST THROUGH THE WOODS AS YOU CAN UNC. AND NOW THAT NOTHING GROWS IN OUR BACK YARD THAT IS GOOD TO EAT WE MUST GO WHERE THERE IS FOOD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-71 UNC NUNKIE MADE NO REPLY FOR A TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-72 THEN HE SHUT DOWN THE WINDOW AND TURNED HIS CHAIR TO FACE THE ROOM FOR THE SUN WAS SINKING BEHIND THE TREE TOPS AND IT WAS GROWING COOL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-73 BY AND BY OJO LIGHTED THE FIRE AND THE LOGS BLAZED FREELY IN THE BROAD FIREPLACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-74 THE TWO SAT IN THE FIRELIGHT A LONG TIME THE OLD WHITE BEARDED MUNCHKIN AND THE LITTLE BOY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-75 BOTH WERE THINKING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-76 WHEN IT GREW QUITE DARK OUTSIDE OJO SAID, EAT YOUR BREAD UNC AND THEN WE WILL GO TO BED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-77 BUT UNC NUNKIE DID NOT EAT THE BREAD,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-78 NEITHER DID HE GO DIRECTLY TO BED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-01-79 LONG AFTER HIS LITTLE NEPHEW WAS SOUND ASLEEP IN THE CORNER OF THE ROOM THE OLD MAN SAT BY THE FIRE THINKING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-01 CHAPTER TWO THE CROOKED MAGICIAN JUST AT DAWN NEXT MORNING UNC NUNKIE LAID HIS HAND TENDERLY ON OJO'S HEAD AND AWAKENED HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-02 COME HE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-03 OJO DRESSED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-04 HE WORE BLUE SILK STOCKINGS BLUE KNEE PANTS WITH GOLD BUCKLES A BLUE RUFFLED WAIST AND A JACKET OF BRIGHT BLUE BRAIDED WITH GOLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-05 HIS SHOES WERE OF BLUE LEATHER AND TURNED UP AT THE TOES WHICH WERE POINTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-06 HIS HAT HAD A PEAKED CROWN AND A FLAT BRIM AND AROUND THE BRIM WAS A ROW OF TINY GOLDEN BELLS THAT TINKLED WHEN HE MOVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-07 THIS WAS THE NATIVE COSTUME OF THOSE WHO INHABITED THE MUNCHKIN COUNTRY OF THE LAND OF OZ SO UNC NUNKIE'S DRESS WAS MUCH LIKE THAT OF HIS NEPHEW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-08 INSTEAD OF SHOES THE OLD MAN WORE BOOTS WITH TURNOVER TOPS AND HIS BLUE COAT HAD WIDE CUFFS OF GOLD BRAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-09 THE BOY NOTICED THAT HIS UNCLE HAD NOT EATEN THE BREAD AND SUPPOSED THE OLD MAN HAD NOT BEEN HUNGRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-10 OJO WAS HUNGRY THOUGH,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-11 SO HE DIVIDED THE PIECE OF BREAD UPON THE TABLE AND ATE HIS HALF FOR BREAKFAST WASHING IT DOWN WITH FRESH COOL WATER FROM THE BROOK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-12 UNC PUT THE OTHER PIECE OF BREAD IN HIS JACKET POCKET AFTER WHICH HE AGAIN SAID AS HE WALKED OUT THROUGH THE DOORWAY, COME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-13 OJO WAS WELL PLEASED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-14 HE WAS DREADFULLY TIRED OF LIVING ALL ALONE IN THE WOODS AND WANTED TO TRAVEL AND SEE PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-15 FOR A LONG TIME HE HAD WISHED TO EXPLORE THE BEAUTIFUL LAND OF OZ IN WHICH THEY LIVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-16 WHEN THEY WERE OUTSIDE UNC SIMPLY LATCHED THE DOOR AND STARTED UP THE PATH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-17 NO ONE WOULD DISTURB THEIR LITTLE HOUSE EVEN IF ANYONE CAME SO FAR INTO THE THICK FOREST WHILE THEY WERE GONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-18 AT THE FOOT OF THE MOUNTAIN THAT SEPARATED THE COUNTRY OF THE MUNCHKINS FROM THE COUNTRY OF THE GILLIKINS THE PATH DIVIDED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-19 ONE WAY LED TO THE LEFT AND THE OTHER TO THE RIGHT STRAIGHT UP THE MOUNTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-20 UNC NUNKIE TOOK THIS RIGHT HAND PATH AND OJO FOLLOWED WITHOUT ASKING WHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-21 HE KNEW IT WOULD TAKE THEM TO THE HOUSE OF THE CROOKED MAGICIAN WHOM HE HAD NEVER SEEN BUT WHO WAS THEIR NEAREST NEIGHBOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-22 ALL THE MORNING THEY TRUDGED UP THE MOUNTAIN PATH AND AT NOON UNC AND OJO SAT ON A FALLEN TREE TRUNK AND ATE THE LAST OF THE BREAD WHICH THE OLD MUNCHKIN HAD PLACED IN HIS POCKET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-23 THEN THEY STARTED ON AGAIN AND TWO HOURS LATER CAME IN SIGHT OF THE HOUSE OF DOCTOR PIPT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-24 IT WAS A BIG HOUSE ROUND AS WERE ALL THE MUNCHKIN HOUSES AND PAINTED BLUE WHICH IS THE DISTINCTIVE COLOR OF THE MUNCHKIN COUNTRY OF OZ. THERE WAS A PRETTY GARDEN AROUND THE HOUSE WHERE BLUE TREES AND BLUE FLOWERS GREW IN ABUNDANCE AND IN ONE PLACE WERE BEDS OF BLUE CABBAGES BLUE CARROTS AND BLUE LETTUCE ALL OF WHICH WERE DELICIOUS TO EAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-25 IN DOCTOR PIPT'S GARDEN GREW BUN TREES CAKE TREES CREAM PUFF BUSHES BLUE BUTTERCUPS WHICH YIELDED EXCELLENT BLUE BUTTER AND A ROW OF CHOCOLATE CARAMEL PLANTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-26 PATHS OF BLUE GRAVEL DIVIDED THE VEGETABLE AND FLOWER BEDS AND A WIDER PATH LED UP TO THE FRONT DOOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-27 THE PLACE WAS IN A CLEARING ON THE MOUNTAIN BUT A LITTLE WAY OFF WAS THE GRIM FOREST WHICH COMPLETELY SURROUNDED IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-28 UNC KNOCKED AT THE DOOR OF THE HOUSE AND A CHUBBY PLEASANT FACED WOMAN DRESSED ALL IN BLUE OPENED IT AND GREETED THE VISITORS WITH A SMILE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-29 AH SAID OJO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-30 YOU MUST BE DAME MARGOLOTTE THE GOOD WIFE OF DOCTOR PIPT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-31 I AM MY DEAR AND ALL STRANGERS ARE WELCOME TO MY HOME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-32 MAY WE SEE THE FAMOUS MAGICIAN MADAM?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-33 HE IS VERY BUSY JUST NOW SHE SAID SHAKING HER HEAD DOUBTFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-34 BUT COME IN AND LET ME GIVE YOU SOMETHING TO EAT FOR YOU MUST HAVE TRAVELED FAR IN ORDER TO GET OUR LONELY PLACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-35 WE HAVE REPLIED OJO AS HE AND UNC ENTERED THE HOUSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-36 WE HAVE COME FROM A FAR LONELIER PLACE THAN THIS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-37 PLACE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-38 AND IN THE MUNCHKIN COUNTRY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-39 SHE EXCLAIMED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-40 THEN IT MUST BE SOMEWHERE IN THE BLUE FOREST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-41 IT IS GOOD DAME MARGOLOTTE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-42 DEAR ME!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-43 SHE SAID LOOKING AT THE MAN YOU MUST BE UNC NUNKIE KNOWN AS THE SILENT ONE. THEN SHE LOOKED AT THE BOY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-44 AND YOU MUST BE OJO THE UNLUCKY SHE ADDED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-45 YES SAID UNC. I NEVER KNEW I WAS CALLED THE UNLUCKY SAID OJO SOBERLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-46 BUT IT IS REALLY A GOOD NAME FOR ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-47 WELL REMARKED THE WOMAN AS SHE BUSTLED AROUND THE ROOM AND SET THE TABLE AND BROUGHT FOOD FROM THE CUPBOARD YOU WERE UNLUCKY TO LIVE ALL ALONE IN THAT DISMAL FOREST WHICH IS MUCH WORSE THAN THE FOREST AROUND HERE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-48 BUT PERHAPS YOUR LUCK WILL CHANGE NOW YOU ARE AWAY FROM IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-49 IF DURING YOUR TRAVELS YOU CAN MANAGE TO LOSE THAT UN AT THE BEGINNING OF YOUR NAME UNLUCKY YOU WILL THEN BECOME OJO THE LUCKY WHICH WILL BE A GREAT IMPROVEMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-50 HOW CAN I LOSE THAT UN DAME MARGOLOTTE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-51 I DO NOT KNOW HOW BUT YOU MUST KEEP THE MATTER IN MIND AND PERHAPS THE CHANCE WILL COME TO YOU SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-52 OJO HAD NEVER EATEN SUCH A FINE MEAL IN ALL HIS LIFE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-53 THERE WAS A SAVORY STEW SMOKING HOT A DISH OF BLUE PEAS A BOWL OF SWEET MILK OF A DELICATE BLUE TINT AND A BLUE PUDDING WITH BLUE PLUMS IN IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-54 WHEN THE VISITORS HAD EATEN HEARTILY OF THIS FARE THE WOMAN SAID TO THEM, DO YOU WISH TO SEE DOCTOR PIPT ON BUSINESS OR FOR PLEASURE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-55 UNC SHOOK HIS HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-56 WE ARE TRAVELING REPLIED OJO AND WE STOPPED AT YOUR HOUSE JUST TO REST AND REFRESH OURSELVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-57 I DO NOT THINK UNC NUNKIE CARES VERY MUCH TO SEE THE FAMOUS CROOKED MAGICIAN,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-58 BUT FOR MY PART I AM CURIOUS TO LOOK AT SUCH A GREAT MAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-59 THE WOMAN SEEMED THOUGHTFUL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-60 I REMEMBER THAT UNC NUNKIE AND MY HUSBAND USED TO BE FRIENDS MANY YEARS AGO SHE SAID SO PERHAPS THEY WILL BE GLAD TO MEET AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-61 THE MAGICIAN IS VERY BUSY AS I SAID BUT IF YOU WILL PROMISE NOT TO DISTURB HIM YOU MAY COME INTO HIS WORKSHOP AND WATCH HIM PREPARE A WONDERFUL CHARM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-62 THANK YOU REPLIED THE BOY MUCH PLEASED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-63 I WOULD LIKE TO DO THAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-64 SHE LED THE WAY TO A GREAT DOMED HALL AT THE BACK OF THE HOUSE WHICH WAS THE MAGICIAN'S WORKSHOP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-65 THERE WAS A ROW OF WINDOWS EXTENDING NEARLY AROUND THE SIDES OF THE CIRCULAR ROOM WHICH RENDERED THE PLACE VERY LIGHT AND THERE WAS A BACK DOOR IN ADDITION TO THE ONE LEADING TO THE FRONT PART OF THE HOUSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-66 BEFORE THE ROW OF WINDOWS A BROAD SEAT WAS BUILT AND THERE WERE SOME CHAIRS AND BENCHES IN THE ROOM BESIDES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-67 AT ONE END STOOD A GREAT FIREPLACE IN WHICH A BLUE LOG WAS BLAZING WITH A BLUE FLAME AND OVER THE FIRE HUNG FOUR KETTLES IN A ROW ALL BUBBLING AND STEAMING AT A GREAT RATE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-68 THE MAGICIAN WAS STIRRING ALL FOUR OF THESE KETTLES AT THE SAME TIME TWO WITH HIS HANDS AND TWO WITH HIS FEET TO THE LATTER WOODEN LADLES BEING STRAPPED FOR THIS MAN WAS SO VERY CROOKED THAT HIS LEGS WERE AS HANDY AS HIS ARMS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-69 UNC NUNKIE CAME FORWARD TO GREET HIS OLD FRIEND BUT NOT BEING ABLE TO SHAKE EITHER HIS HANDS OR HIS FEET WHICH WERE ALL OCCUPIED IN STIRRING HE PATTED THE MAGICIAN'S BALD HEAD AND ASKED, WHAT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-70 AH IT'S THE SILENT ONE REMARKED DOCTOR PIPT WITHOUT LOOKING UP AND HE WANTS TO KNOW WHAT I'M MAKING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-71 WELL WHEN IT IS QUITE FINISHED THIS COMPOUND WILL BE THE WONDERFUL POWDER OF LIFE WHICH NO ONE KNOWS HOW TO MAKE BUT MYSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-72 WHENEVER IT IS SPRINKLED ON ANYTHING THAT THING WILL AT ONCE COME TO LIFE NO MATTER WHAT IT IS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-73 IT TAKES ME SEVERAL YEARS TO MAKE THIS MAGIC POWDER BUT AT THIS MOMENT I AM PLEASED TO SAY IT IS NEARLY DONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-74 YOU SEE I AM MAKING IT FOR MY GOOD WIFE MARGOLOTTE WHO WANTS TO USE SOME OF IT FOR A PURPOSE OF HER OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-75 YOU MUST KNOW SAID MARGOLOTTE WHEN THEY WERE ALL SEATED TOGETHER ON THE BROAD WINDOW SEAT THAT MY HUSBAND FOOLISHLY GAVE AWAY ALL THE POWDER OF LIFE HE FIRST MADE TO OLD MOMBI THE WITCH WHO USED TO LIVE IN THE COUNTRY OF THE GILLIKINS TO THE NORTH OF HERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-76 MOMBI GAVE TO DOCTOR PIPT A POWDER OF PERPETUAL YOUTH IN EXCHANGE FOR HIS POWDER OF LIFE BUT SHE CHEATED HIM WICKEDLY FOR THE POWDER OF YOUTH WAS NO GOOD AND COULD WORK NO MAGIC AT ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-77 PERHAPS THE POWDER OF LIFE COULDN'T EITHER SAID OJO. YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-78 IT IS PERFECTION SHE DECLARED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-79 THE FIRST LOT WE TESTED ON OUR GLASS CAT WHICH NOT ONLY BEGAN TO LIVE BUT HAS LIVED EVER SINCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-80 SHE'S SOMEWHERE AROUND THE HOUSE NOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-81 A GLASS CAT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-02-82 EXCLAIMED OJO ASTONISHED.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-48 OZMA HAD NEVER KNOWN THAT HER DOMINIONS CONTAINED SUCH A THING AS A WOOZY THERE BEING BUT ONE IN EXISTENCE AND THIS BEING CONFINED IN HIS FOREST FOR MANY YEARS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-50 BUT SHE ADDED THAT SHE DID NOT CARE MUCH FOR THE GLASS CAT. STILL SAID THE SHAGGY MAN THE GLASS CAT IS VERY PRETTY AND IF SHE WERE NOT SO CONCEITED OVER HER PINK BRAINS NO ONE WOULD OBJECT TO HER AS A COMPANION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-51 THE WIZARD HAD BEEN EATING SILENTLY UNTIL NOW WHEN HE LOOKED UP AND REMARKED, THAT POWDER OF LIFE WHICH IS MADE BY THE CROOKED MAGICIAN IS REALLY A WONDERFUL THING.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-53 I MUST SEE ABOUT THAT SAID OZMA GRAVELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-54 WELL WHEN I WAS A BABY GIRL I WAS STOLEN BY AN OLD WITCH NAMED MOMBI AND TRANSFORMED INTO A BOY BEGAN THE GIRL RULER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-55 I DID NOT KNOW WHO I WAS AND WHEN I GREW BIG ENOUGH TO WORK THE WITCH MADE ME WAIT UPON HER AND CARRY WOOD FOR THE FIRE AND HOE IN THE GARDEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-56 ONE DAY SHE CAME BACK FROM A JOURNEY BRINGING SOME OF THE POWDER OF LIFE WHICH DOCTOR PIPT HAD GIVEN HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-57 I HAD MADE A PUMPKIN HEADED MAN AND SET IT UP IN HER PATH TO FRIGHTEN HER FOR I WAS FOND OF FUN AND HATED THE WITCH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-58 BUT SHE KNEW WHAT THE FIGURE WAS AND TO TEST HER POWDER OF LIFE SHE SPRINKLED SOME OF IT ON THE MAN I HAD MADE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-59 IT CAME TO LIFE AND IS NOW OUR DEAR FRIEND JACK PUMPKINHEAD.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-61 DURING OUR JOURNEY WE CAME UPON A WOODEN SAWHORSE STANDING BY THE ROAD AND I USED THE MAGIC POWDER TO BRING IT TO LIFE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-62 THE SAWHORSE HAS BEEN WITH ME EVER SINCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-63 WHEN I GOT TO THE EMERALD CITY THE GOOD SORCERESS GLINDA KNEW WHO I WAS AND RESTORED ME TO MY PROPER PERSON WHEN I BECAME THE RIGHTFUL RULER OF THIS LAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-64 SO YOU SEE HAD NOT OLD MOMBI BROUGHT HOME THE POWDER OF LIFE I MIGHT NEVER HAVE RUN AWAY FROM HER AND BECOME OZMA OF OZ NOR WOULD WE HAVE HAD JACK PUMPKINHEAD AND THE SAWHORSE TO COMFORT AND AMUSE US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-65 THAT STORY INTERESTED THE SHAGGY MAN VERY MUCH AS WELL AS THE OTHERS WHO HAD OFTEN HEARD IT BEFORE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-17-66 THE DINNER BEING NOW CONCLUDED THEY ALL WENT TO OZMA'S DRAWING ROOM WHERE THEY PASSED A PLEASANT EVENING BEFORE IT CAME TIME TO RETIRE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-18-01 CHAPTER EIGHTEEN OJO IS FORGIVEN THE NEXT MORNING THE SOLDIER WITH THE GREEN WHISKERS WENT TO THE PRISON AND TOOK OJO AWAY TO THE ROYAL PALACE WHERE HE WAS SUMMONED TO APPEAR BEFORE THE GIRL RULER FOR JUDGMENT.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-18-61 YEARS AGO THERE WERE MANY WITCHES AND MAGICIANS IN THE LAND OF OZ AND ONE OF THE THINGS THEY OFTEN USED IN MAKING THEIR MAGIC CHARMS AND TRANSFORMATIONS WAS A SIX LEAVED CLOVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-18-62 THESE WITCHES AND MAGICIANS CAUSED SO MUCH TROUBLE AMONG MY PEOPLE OFTEN USING THEIR POWERS FOR EVIL RATHER THAN GOOD THAT I DECIDED TO FORBID ANYONE TO PRACTICE MAGIC OR SORCERY EXCEPT GLINDA THE GOOD AND HER ASSISTANT THE WIZARD OF OZ BOTH OF WHOM I CAN TRUST TO USE THEIR ARTS ONLY TO BENEFIT MY PEOPLE AND TO MAKE THEM HAPPIER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-18-137 I'M CALLED OJO THE UNLUCKY YOU KNOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-01 CHAPTER NINETEEN TROUBLE WITH THE TOTTENHOTS A DAY'S JOURNEY FROM THE EMERALD CITY BROUGHT THE LITTLE BAND OF ADVENTURERS TO THE HOME OF JACK PUMPKINHEAD WHICH WAS A HOUSE FORMED FROM THE SHELL OF AN IMMENSE PUMPKIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-02 JACK HAD MADE IT HIMSELF AND WAS VERY PROUD OF IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-03 THERE WAS A DOOR AND SEVERAL WINDOWS AND THROUGH THE TOP WAS STUCK A STOVEPIPE THAT LED FROM A SMALL STOVE INSIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-04 THE DOOR WAS REACHED BY A FLIGHT OF THREE STEPS AND THERE WAS A GOOD FLOOR ON WHICH WAS ARRANGED SOME FURNITURE THAT WAS QUITE COMFORTABLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-05 IT IS CERTAIN THAT JACK PUMPKINHEAD MIGHT HAVE HAD A MUCH FINER HOUSE TO LIVE IN HAD HE WANTED IT FOR OZMA LOVED THE STUPID FELLOW WHO HAD BEEN HER EARLIEST COMPANION,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-06 BUT JACK PREFERRED HIS PUMPKIN HOUSE AS IT MATCHED HIMSELF VERY WELL AND IN THIS HE WAS NOT SO STUPID AFTER ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-07 THE BODY OF THIS REMARKABLE PERSON WAS MADE OF WOOD BRANCHES OF TREES OF VARIOUS SIZES HAVING BEEN USED FOR THE PURPOSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-08 THIS WOODEN FRAMEWORK WAS COVERED BY A RED SHIRT WITH WHITE SPOTS IN IT BLUE TROUSERS A YELLOW VEST A JACKET OF GREEN AND GOLD AND STOUT LEATHER SHOES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-09 THE NECK WAS A SHARPENED STICK ON WHICH THE PUMPKIN HEAD WAS SET AND THE EYES EARS NOSE AND MOUTH WERE CARVED ON THE SKIN OF THE PUMPKIN VERY LIKE A CHILD'S JACK O LANTERN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-10 THE HOUSE OF THIS INTERESTING CREATION STOOD IN THE CENTER OF A VAST PUMPKIN FIELD WHERE THE VINES GREW IN PROFUSION AND BORE PUMPKINS OF EXTRAORDINARY SIZE AS WELL AS THOSE WHICH WERE SMALLER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-11 SOME OF THE PUMPKINS NOW RIPENING ON THE VINES WERE ALMOST AS LARGE AS JACK'S HOUSE AND HE TOLD DOROTHY HE INTENDED TO ADD ANOTHER PUMPKIN TO HIS MANSION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-12 THE TRAVELERS WERE CORDIALLY WELCOMED TO THIS QUAINT DOMICILE AND INVITED TO PASS THE NIGHT THERE WHICH THEY HAD PLANNED TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-13 THE PATCHWORK GIRL WAS GREATLY INTERESTED IN JACK AND EXAMINED HIM ADMIRINGLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-14 YOU ARE QUITE HANDSOME SHE SAID,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-15 BUT NOT AS REALLY BEAUTIFUL AS THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-16 JACK TURNED AT THIS TO EXAMINE THE SCARECROW CRITICALLY AND HIS OLD FRIEND SLYLY WINKED ONE PAINTED EYE AT HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-17 THERE IS NO ACCOUNTING FOR TASTES REMARKED THE PUMPKINHEAD WITH A SIGH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-18 AN OLD CROW ONCE TOLD ME I WAS VERY FASCINATING BUT OF COURSE THE BIRD MIGHT HAVE BEEN MISTAKEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-19 YET I HAVE NOTICED THAT THE CROWS USUALLY AVOID THE SCARECROW WHO IS A VERY HONEST FELLOW IN HIS WAY BUT STUFFED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-20 I AM NOT STUFFED YOU WILL OBSERVE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-21 MY BODY IS GOOD SOLID HICKORY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-22 I ADORE STUFFING SAID THE PATCHWORK GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-23 WELL AS FOR THAT MY HEAD IS STUFFED WITH PUMPKIN SEEDS DECLARED JACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-24 I USE THEM FOR BRAINS AND WHEN THEY ARE FRESH I AM INTELLECTUAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-25 JUST NOW I REGRET TO SAY MY SEEDS ARE RATTLING A BIT SO I MUST SOON GET ANOTHER HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-26 OH,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-27 DO YOU CHANGE YOUR HEAD?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-28 ASKED OJO. TO BE SURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-29 PUMPKINS ARE NOT PERMANENT MORE'S THE PITY AND IN TIME THEY SPOIL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-30 THAT IS WHY I GROW SUCH A GREAT FIELD OF PUMPKINS THAT I MAY SELECT A NEW HEAD WHENEVER NECESSARY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-31 WHO CARVES THE FACES ON THEM?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-32 INQUIRED THE BOY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-33 I DO THAT MYSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-34 I LIFT OFF MY OLD HEAD PLACE IT ON A TABLE BEFORE ME AND USE THE FACE FOR A PATTERN TO GO BY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-35 SOMETIMES THE FACES I CARVE ARE BETTER THAN OTHERS MORE EXPRESSIVE AND CHEERFUL YOU KNOW BUT I THINK THEY AVERAGE VERY WELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-36 BEFORE SHE HAD STARTED ON THE JOURNEY DOROTHY HAD PACKED A KNAPSACK WITH THE THINGS SHE MIGHT NEED AND THIS KNAPSACK THE SCARECROW CARRIED STRAPPED TO HIS BACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-37 THE LITTLE GIRL WORE A PLAIN GINGHAM DRESS AND A CHECKED SUNBONNET AS SHE KNEW THEY WERE BEST FITTED FOR TRAVEL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-38 OJO ALSO HAD BROUGHT ALONG HIS BASKET TO WHICH OZMA HAD ADDED A BOTTLE OF SQUARE MEAL TABLETS AND SOME FRUIT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-39 BUT JACK PUMPKINHEAD GREW A LOT OF THINGS IN HIS GARDEN BESIDES PUMPKINS SO HE COOKED FOR THEM A FINE VEGETABLE SOUP AND GAVE DOROTHY OJO AND TOTO THE ONLY ONES WHO FOUND IT NECESSARY TO EAT A PUMPKIN PIE AND SOME GREEN CHEESE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-40 FOR BEDS THEY MUST USE THE SWEET DRIED GRASSES WHICH JACK HAD STREWN ALONG ONE SIDE OF THE ROOM BUT THAT SATISFIED DOROTHY AND OJO VERY WELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-41 TOTO OF COURSE SLEPT BESIDE HIS LITTLE MISTRESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-42 THE SCARECROW SCRAPS AND THE PUMPKINHEAD WERE TIRELESS AND HAD NO NEED TO SLEEP SO THEY SAT UP AND TALKED TOGETHER ALL NIGHT,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-43 BUT THEY STAYED OUTSIDE THE HOUSE UNDER THE BRIGHT STARS AND TALKED IN LOW TONES SO AS NOT TO DISTURB THE SLEEPERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-44 DURING THE CONVERSATION THE SCARECROW EXPLAINED THEIR QUEST FOR A DARK WELL AND ASKED JACK'S ADVICE WHERE TO FIND IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-45 THE PUMPKINHEAD CONSIDERED THE MATTER GRAVELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-46 THAT IS GOING TO BE A DIFFICULT TASK SAID HE AND IF I WERE YOU I'D TAKE ANY ORDINARY WELL AND ENCLOSE IT SO AS TO MAKE IT DARK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-47 I FEAR THAT WOULDN'T DO REPLIED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-48 THE WELL MUST BE NATURALLY DARK AND THE WATER MUST NEVER HAVE SEEN THE LIGHT OF DAY FOR OTHERWISE THE MAGIC CHARM MIGHT NOT WORK AT ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-49 HOW MUCH OF THE WATER DO YOU NEED?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-50 ASKED JACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-51 A GILL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-52 HOW MUCH IS A GILL?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-53 WHY A GILL IS A GILL OF COURSE ANSWERED THE SCARECROW WHO DID NOT WISH TO DISPLAY HIS IGNORANCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-54 I KNOW!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-55 CRIED SCRAPS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-56 JACK AND JILL WENT UP THE HILL TO FETCH NO NO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-57 THAT'S WRONG INTERRUPTED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-58 THERE ARE TWO KINDS OF GILLS I THINK,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-59 ONE IS A GIRL AND THE OTHER IS A GILLYFLOWER SAID JACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-60 NO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-61 A MEASURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-62 HOW BIG A MEASURE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-63 WELL I'LL ASK DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-64 SO NEXT MORNING THEY ASKED DOROTHY AND SHE SAID, I DON'T JUST KNOW HOW MUCH A GILL IS BUT I'VE BROUGHT ALONG A GOLD FLASK THAT HOLDS A PINT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-65 THAT'S MORE THAN A GILL I'M SURE AND THE CROOKED MAGICIAN MAY MEASURE IT TO SUIT HIMSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-66 BUT THE THING THAT'S BOTHERING US MOST JACK IS TO FIND THE WELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-67 JACK GAZED AROUND THE LANDSCAPE FOR HE WAS STANDING IN THE DOORWAY OF HIS HOUSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-68 THIS IS A FLAT COUNTRY SO YOU WON'T FIND ANY DARK WELLS HERE SAID HE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-69 YOU MUST GO INTO THE MOUNTAINS WHERE ROCKS AND CAVERNS ARE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-70 AND WHERE IS THAT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-71 ASKED OJO. IN THE QUADLING COUNTRY WHICH LIES SOUTH OF HERE REPLIED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-72 I'VE KNOWN ALL ALONG THAT WE MUST GO TO THE MOUNTAINS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-73 SO HAVE I SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-74 BUT GOODNESS ME!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-75 THE QUADLING COUNTRY IS FULL OF DANGERS DECLARED JACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-76 I'VE NEVER BEEN THERE MYSELF BUT I HAVE SAID THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-77 I'VE FACED THE DREADFUL HAMMERHEADS WHICH HAVE NO ARMS AND BUTT YOU LIKE A GOAT,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-78 AND I'VE FACED THE FIGHTING TREES WHICH BEND DOWN THEIR BRANCHES TO POUND AND WHIP YOU AND HAD MANY OTHER ADVENTURES THERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-79 IT'S A WILD COUNTRY REMARKED DOROTHY SOBERLY AND IF WE GO THERE WE'RE SURE TO HAVE TROUBLES OF OUR OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-80 BUT I GUESS WE'LL HAVE TO GO IF WE WANT THAT GILL OF WATER FROM THE DARK WELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-81 SO THEY SAID GOOD BYE TO THE PUMPKINHEAD AND RESUMED THEIR TRAVELS HEADING NOW DIRECTLY TOWARD THE SOUTH COUNTRY WHERE MOUNTAINS AND ROCKS AND CAVERNS AND FORESTS OF GREAT TREES ABOUNDED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-82 THIS PART OF THE LAND OF OZ WHILE IT BELONGED TO OZMA AND OWED HER ALLEGIANCE WAS SO WILD AND SECLUDED THAT MANY QUEER PEOPLES HID IN ITS JUNGLES AND LIVED IN THEIR OWN WAY WITHOUT EVEN A KNOWLEDGE THAT THEY HAD A RULER IN THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-83 IF THEY WERE LEFT ALONE THESE CREATURES NEVER TROUBLED THE INHABITANTS OF THE REST OF OZ BUT THOSE WHO INVADED THEIR DOMAINS ENCOUNTERED MANY DANGERS FROM THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-84 IT WAS A TWO DAYS JOURNEY FROM JACK PUMKINHEAD'S HOUSE TO THE EDGE OF THE QUADLING COUNTRY FOR NEITHER DOROTHY NOR OJO COULD WALK VERY FAST AND THEY OFTEN STOPPED BY THE WAYSIDE TO REST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-85 THE FIRST NIGHT THEY SLEPT ON THE BROAD FIELDS AMONG THE BUTTERCUPS AND DAISIES AND THE SCARECROW COVERED THE CHILDREN WITH A GAUZE BLANKET TAKEN FROM HIS KNAPSACK SO THEY WOULD NOT BE CHILLED BY THE NIGHT AIR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-86 TOWARD EVENING OF THE SECOND DAY THEY REACHED A SANDY PLAIN WHERE WALKING WAS DIFFICULT,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-87 BUT SOME DISTANCE BEFORE THEM THEY SAW A GROUP OF PALM TREES WITH MANY CURIOUS BLACK DOTS UNDER THEM,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-88 SO THEY TRUDGED BRAVELY ON TO REACH THAT PLACE BY DARK AND SPEND THE NIGHT UNDER THE SHELTER OF THE TREES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-89 THE BLACK DOTS GREW LARGER AS THEY ADVANCED AND ALTHOUGH THE LIGHT WAS DIM DOROTHY THOUGHT THEY LOOKED LIKE BIG KETTLES TURNED UPSIDE DOWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-90 JUST BEYOND THIS PLACE A JUMBLE OF HUGE JAGGED ROCKS LAY SCATTERED RISING TO THE MOUNTAINS BEHIND THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-91 OUR TRAVELERS PREFERRED TO ATTEMPT TO CLIMB THESE ROCKS BY DAYLIGHT AND THEY REALIZED THAT FOR A TIME THIS WOULD BE THEIR LAST NIGHT ON THE PLAINS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-92 TWILIGHT HAD FALLEN BY THE TIME THEY CAME TO THE TREES BENEATH WHICH WERE THE BLACK CIRCULAR OBJECTS THEY HAD MARKED FROM A DISTANCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-93 DOZENS OF THEM WERE SCATTERED AROUND AND DOROTHY BENT NEAR TO ONE WHICH WAS ABOUT AS TALL AS SHE WAS TO EXAMINE IT MORE CLOSELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-94 AS SHE DID SO THE TOP FLEW OPEN AND OUT POPPED A DUSKY CREATURE RISING ITS LENGTH INTO THE AIR AND THEN PLUMPING DOWN UPON THE GROUND JUST BESIDE THE LITTLE GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-95 ANOTHER AND ANOTHER POPPED OUT OF THE CIRCULAR POT LIKE DWELLING WHILE FROM ALL THE OTHER BLACK OBJECTS CAME POPPING MORE CREATURES VERY LIKE JUMPING JACKS WHEN THEIR BOXES ARE UNHOOKED UNTIL FULLY A HUNDRED STOOD GATHERED AROUND OUR LITTLE GROUP OF TRAVELERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-96 BY THIS TIME DOROTHY HAD DISCOVERED THEY WERE PEOPLE TINY AND CURIOUSLY FORMED BUT STILL PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-97 THEIR SKINS WERE DUSKY AND THEIR HAIR STOOD STRAIGHT UP LIKE WIRES AND WAS BRILLIANT SCARLET IN COLOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-98 THEIR BODIES WERE BARE EXCEPT FOR SKINS FASTENED AROUND THEIR WAISTS AND THEY WORE BRACELETS ON THEIR ANKLES AND WRISTS AND NECKLACES AND GREAT PENDANT EARRINGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-99 TOTO CROUCHED BESIDE HIS MISTRESS AND WAILED AS IF HE DID NOT LIKE THESE STRANGE CREATURES A BIT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-100 SCRAPS BEGAN TO MUTTER SOMETHING ABOUT HOPPITY POPPITY JUMPITY DUMP!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-101 BUT NO ONE PAID ANY ATTENTION TO HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-102 OJO KEPT CLOSE TO THE SCARECROW AND THE SCARECROW KEPT CLOSE TO DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-103 BUT THE LITTLE GIRL TURNED TO THE QUEER CREATURES AND ASKED, WHO ARE YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-104 THEY ANSWERED THIS QUESTION ALL TOGETHER IN A SORT OF CHANTING CHORUS THE WORDS BEING AS FOLLOWS, WE'RE THE JOLLY TOTTENHOTS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-105 WE DO NOT LIKE THE DAY BUT IN THE NIGHT TIS OUR DELIGHT TO GAMBOL SKIP AND PLAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-106 WE HATE THE SUN AND FROM IT RUN THE MOON IS COOL AND CLEAR SO ON THIS SPOT EACH TOTTENHOT WAITS FOR IT TO APPEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-107 WE'RE EV'RY ONE CHOCK FULL OF FUN AND FULL OF MISCHIEF TOO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-108 BUT IF YOU'RE GAY AND WITH US PLAY WE'LL DO NO HARM TO YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-109 GLAD TO MEET YOU TOTTENHOTS SAID THE SCARECROW SOLEMNLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-110 BUT YOU MUSTN'T EXPECT US TO PLAY WITH YOU ALL NIGHT FOR WE'VE TRAVELED ALL DAY AND SOME OF US ARE TIRED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-111 AND WE NEVER GAMBLE ADDED THE PATCHWORK GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-112 IT'S AGAINST THE LAW. THESE REMARKS WERE GREETED WITH SHOUTS OF LAUGHTER BY THE IMPISH CREATURES AND ONE SEIZED THE SCARECROW'S ARM AND WAS ASTONISHED TO FIND THE STRAW MAN WHIRL AROUND SO EASILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-113 SO THE TOTTENHOT RAISED THE SCARECROW HIGH IN THE AIR AND TOSSED HIM OVER THE HEADS OF THE CROWD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-114 SOME ONE CAUGHT HIM AND TOSSED HIM BACK AND SO WITH SHOUTS OF GLEE THEY CONTINUED THROWING THE SCARECROW HERE AND THERE AS IF HE HAD BEEN A BASKET BALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-115 PRESENTLY ANOTHER IMP SEIZED SCRAPS AND BEGAN TO THROW HER ABOUT IN THE SAME WAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-116 THEY FOUND HER A LITTLE HEAVIER THAN THE SCARECROW BUT STILL LIGHT ENOUGH TO BE TOSSED LIKE A SOFA CUSHION AND THEY WERE ENJOYING THE SPORT IMMENSELY WHEN DOROTHY ANGRY AND INDIGNANT AT THE TREATMENT HER FRIENDS WERE RECEIVING RUSHED AMONG THE TOTTENHOTS AND BEGAN SLAPPING AND PUSHING THEM UNTIL SHE HAD RESCUED THE SCARECROW AND THE PATCHWORK GIRL AND HELD THEM CLOSE ON EITHER SIDE OF HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-117 PERHAPS SHE WOULD NOT HAVE ACCOMPLISHED THIS VICTORY SO EASILY HAD NOT TOTO HELPED HER BARKING AND SNAPPING AT THE BARE LEGS OF THE IMPS UNTIL THEY WERE GLAD TO FLEE FROM HIS ATTACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-118 AS FOR OJO SOME OF THE CREATURES HAD ATTEMPTED TO TOSS HIM ALSO BUT FINDING HIS BODY TOO HEAVY THEY THREW HIM TO THE GROUND AND A ROW OF THE IMPS SAT ON HIM AND HELD HIM FROM ASSISTING DOROTHY IN HER BATTLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-119 THE LITTLE BROWN FOLKS WERE MUCH SURPRISED AT BEING ATTACKED BY THE GIRL AND THE DOG AND ONE OR TWO WHO HAD BEEN SLAPPED HARDEST BEGAN TO CRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-120 THEN SUDDENLY THEY GAVE A SHOUT ALL TOGETHER AND DISAPPEARED IN A FLASH INTO THEIR VARIOUS HOUSES THE TOPS OF WHICH CLOSED WITH A SERIES OF POPS THAT SOUNDED LIKE A BUNCH OF FIRECRACKERS BEING EXPLODED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-121 THE ADVENTURERS NOW FOUND THEMSELVES ALONE AND DOROTHY ASKED ANXIOUSLY, IS ANYBODY HURT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-122 NOT ME ANSWERED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-123 THEY HAVE GIVEN MY STRAW A GOOD SHAKING UP AND TAKEN ALL THE LUMPS OUT OF IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-124 I AM NOW IN SPLENDID CONDITION AND AM REALLY OBLIGED TO THE TOTTENHOTS FOR THEIR KIND TREATMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-125 I FEEL MUCH THE SAME WAY SAID SCRAPS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-126 MY COTTON STUFFING HAD SAGGED A GOOD DEAL WITH THE DAY'S WALKING AND THEY'VE LOOSENED IT UP UNTIL I FEEL AS PLUMP AS A SAUSAGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-127 BUT THE PLAY WAS A LITTLE ROUGH AND I'D HAD QUITE ENOUGH OF IT WHEN YOU INTERFERED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-128 SIX OF THEM SAT ON ME SAID OJO BUT AS THEY ARE SO LITTLE THEY DIDN'T HURT ME MUCH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-129 JUST THEN THE ROOF OF THE HOUSE IN FRONT OF THEM OPENED AND A TOTTENHOT STUCK HIS HEAD OUT VERY CAUTIOUSLY AND LOOKED AT THE STRANGERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-130 CAN'T YOU TAKE A JOKE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-131 HE ASKED REPROACHFULLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-132 HAVEN'T YOU ANY FUN IN YOU AT ALL?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-133 IF I HAD SUCH A QUALITY REPLIED THE SCARECROW YOUR PEOPLE WOULD HAVE KNOCKED IT OUT OF ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-134 BUT I DON'T BEAR GRUDGES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-135 I FORGIVE YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-136 SO DO I ADDED SCRAPS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-137 THAT IS IF YOU BEHAVE YOURSELVES AFTER THIS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-138 IT WAS JUST A LITTLE ROUGH HOUSE THAT'S ALL SAID THE TOTTENHOT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-139 BUT THE QUESTION IS NOT IF WE WILL BEHAVE BUT IF YOU WILL BEHAVE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-140 WE CAN'T BE SHUT UP HERE ALL NIGHT BECAUSE THIS IS OUR TIME TO PLAY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-141 NOR DO WE CARE TO COME OUT AND BE CHEWED UP BY A SAVAGE BEAST OR SLAPPED BY AN ANGRY GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-142 THAT SLAPPING HURTS LIKE SIXTY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-143 SOME OF MY FOLKS ARE CRYING ABOUT IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-144 SO HERE'S THE PROPOSITION, YOU LET US ALONE AND WE'LL LET YOU ALONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-145 YOU BEGAN IT DECLARED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-146 WELL YOU ENDED IT SO WE WON'T ARGUE THE MATTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-147 MAY WE COME OUT AGAIN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-148 OR ARE YOU STILL CRUEL AND SLAPPY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-149 TELL YOU WHAT WE'LL DO SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-150 WE'RE ALL TIRED AND WANT TO SLEEP UNTIL MORNING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-151 IF YOU'LL LET US GET INTO YOUR HOUSE AND STAY THERE UNTIL DAYLIGHT YOU CAN PLAY OUTSIDE ALL YOU WANT TO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-152 THAT'S A BARGAIN!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-153 CRIED THE TOTTENHOT EAGERLY AND HE GAVE A QUEER WHISTLE THAT BROUGHT HIS PEOPLE POPPING OUT OF THEIR HOUSES ON ALL SIDES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-154 WHEN THE HOUSE BEFORE THEM WAS VACANT DOROTHY AND OJO LEANED OVER THE HOLE AND LOOKED IN BUT COULD SEE NOTHING BECAUSE IT WAS SO DARK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-155 BUT IF THE TOTTENHOTS SLEPT THERE ALL DAY THE CHILDREN THOUGHT THEY COULD SLEEP THERE AT NIGHT SO OJO LOWERED HIMSELF DOWN AND FOUND IT WAS NOT VERY DEEP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-156 THERE'S A SOFT CUSHION ALL OVER SAID HE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-157 COME ON IN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-158 DOROTHY HANDED TOTO TO THE BOY AND THEN CLIMBED IN HERSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-159 AFTER HER CAME SCRAPS AND THE SCARECROW WHO DID NOT WISH TO SLEEP BUT PREFERRED TO KEEP OUT OF THE WAY OF THE MISCHIEVOUS TOTTENHOTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-160 THERE SEEMED NO FURNITURE IN THE ROUND DEN BUT SOFT CUSHIONS WERE STREWN ABOUT THE FLOOR AND THESE THEY FOUND MADE VERY COMFORTABLE BEDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-19-161 THEY DID NOT CLOSE THE HOLE IN THE ROOF BUT LEFT IT OPEN TO ADMIT AIR.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-25-118 THE WOMAN PROVED TO BE CROSS AND BAD TEMPERED PERHAPS BECAUSE SHE HAD ONLY CAUGHT ONE RED EEL DURING ALL THE DAY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-25-121 THIS PROMISE PLEASED THE WOMAN AND SHE SOON BECAME MORE PLEASANT SAYING THEY COULD STAY THE NIGHT AT HER HOUSE AND BEGIN THEIR VOYAGE ON THE RIVER NEXT MORNING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-25-122 THIS THEY DID SPENDING A PLEASANT EVENING WITH THE QUADLING FAMILY AND BEING ENTERTAINED WITH SUCH HOSPITALITY AS THE POOR PEOPLE WERE ABLE TO OFFER THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-25-123 THE MAN GROANED A GOOD DEAL AND SAID HE HAD OVERWORKED HIMSELF BY CHOPPING THE LOGS BUT THE SCARECROW GAVE HIM TWO MORE TABLETS THAN HE HAD PROMISED WHICH SEEMED TO COMFORT THE LAZY FELLOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-26-01 CHAPTER TWENTY SIX THE TRICK RIVER NEXT MORNING THEY PUSHED THE RAFT INTO THE WATER AND ALL GOT ABOARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-26-02 THE QUADLING MAN HAD TO HOLD THE LOG CRAFT FAST WHILE THEY TOOK THEIR PLACES AND THE FLOW OF THE RIVER WAS SO POWERFUL THAT IT NEARLY TORE THE RAFT FROM HIS HANDS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-27-32 GOOD!

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-01 CHAPTER TWENTY EIGHT THE WONDERFUL WIZARD OF OZ WHEN OJO ENTERED THE ROOM HE RAN QUICKLY TO THE STATUE OF UNC NUNKIE AND KISSED THE MARBLE FACE AFFECTIONATELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-02 I DID MY BEST UNC HE SAID WITH A SOB BUT IT WAS NO USE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-03 THEN HE DREW BACK AND LOOKED AROUND THE ROOM AND THE SIGHT OF THE ASSEMBLED COMPANY QUITE AMAZED HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-04 ASIDE FROM THE MARBLE STATUES OF UNC NUNKIE AND MARGOLOTTE THE GLASS CAT WAS THERE CURLED UP ON A RUG,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-05 AND THE WOOZY WAS THERE SITTING ON ITS SQUARE HIND LEGS AND LOOKING ON THE SCENE WITH SOLEMN INTEREST,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-07 LAST OF ALL DOCTOR PIPT WAS THERE AND THE CROOKED MAGICIAN SAT HUMPED UP IN A CHAIR SEEMING VERY DEJECTED BUT KEEPING HIS EYES FIXED ON THE LIFELESS FORM OF HIS WIFE MARGOLOTTE WHOM HE FONDLY LOVED BUT WHOM HE NOW FEARED WAS LOST TO HIM FOREVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-08 OZMA TOOK A CHAIR WHICH JELLIA JAMB WHEELED FORWARD FOR THE RULER AND BACK OF HER STOOD THE SCARECROW THE TIN WOODMAN AND DOROTHY AS WELL AS THE COWARDLY LION AND THE HUNGRY TIGER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-11 WE HAVE DISCOVERED THAT THE CROOKED MAGICIAN HAS BEEN INDULGING IN HIS MAGICAL ARTS CONTRARY TO LAW AND THEREFORE BY ROYAL EDICT I HEREBY DEPRIVE HIM OF ALL POWER TO WORK MAGIC IN THE FUTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-12 HE IS NO LONGER A CROOKED MAGICIAN BUT A SIMPLE MUNCHKIN,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-13 HE IS NO LONGER EVEN CROOKED BUT A MAN LIKE OTHER MEN.

SCRAPS MAY LIVE IN THE PALACE OR WHEREVER SHE PLEASES AND BE NOBODY'S SERVANT BUT HER OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-23 THAT'S ALL RIGHT SAID SCRAPS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-32 BUT NOW OJO RUSHED UP AND THREW HIS ARMS JOYFULLY ABOUT HIS UNCLE AND THE OLD MAN HUGGED HIS LITTLE NEPHEW TENDERLY AND STROKED HIS HAIR AND WIPED AWAY THE BOY'S TEARS WITH A HANDKERCHIEF FOR OJO WAS CRYING FROM PURE HAPPINESS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-36 ASKED THE TIN WOODMAN AS EVERYONE CROWDED AROUND TO SHAKE OJO'S HAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-37 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-38 AND IT IS TRUE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ2-28-39 REPLIED OJO GRATEFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-01 AUTHOR'S NOTE PERHAPS I SHOULD ADMIT ON THE TITLE PAGE THAT THIS BOOK IS BY L. FRANK BAUM AND HIS CORRESPONDENTS FOR I HAVE USED MANY SUGGESTIONS CONVEYED TO ME IN LETTERS FROM CHILDREN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-02 ONCE ON A TIME I REALLY IMAGINED MYSELF AN AUTHOR OF FAIRY TALES BUT NOW I AM MERELY AN EDITOR OR PRIVATE SECRETARY FOR A HOST OF YOUNGSTERS WHOSE IDEAS I AM REQUESTSED TO WEAVE INTO THE THREAD OF MY STORIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-03 THESE IDEAS ARE OFTEN CLEVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-04 THEY ARE ALSO LOGICAL AND INTERESTING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-05 SO I HAVE USED THEM WHENEVER I COULD FIND AN OPPORTUNITY AND IT IS BUT JUST THAT I ACKNOWLEDGE MY INDEBTEDNESS TO MY LITTLE FRIENDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-06 MY WHAT IMAGINATIONS THESE CHILDREN HAVE DEVELOPED!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-07 SOMETIMES I AM FAIRLY ASTOUNDED BY THEIR DARING AND GENIUS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-08 THERE WILL BE NO LACK OF FAIRY TALE AUTHORS IN THE FUTURE I AM SURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-09 MY READERS HAVE TOLD ME WHAT TO DO WITH DOROTHY AND AUNT EM AND UNCLE HENRY AND I HAVE OBEYED THEIR MANDATES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-10 THEY HAVE ALSO GIVEN ME A VARIETY OF SUBJECTS TO WRITE ABOUT IN THE FUTURE, ENOUGH IN FACT TO KEEP ME BUSY FOR SOME TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-11 I AM VERY PROUD OF THIS ALLIANCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-12 CHILDREN LOVE THESE STORIES BECAUSE CHILDREN HAVE HELPED TO CREATE THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-13 MY READERS KNOW WHAT THEY WANT AND REALIZE THAT I TRY TO PLEASE THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-14 THE RESULT IS VERY SATISFACTORY TO THE PUBLISHERS TO ME AND I AM QUITE SURE TO THE CHILDREN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-15 I HOPE MY DEARS IT WILL BE A LONG TIME BEFORE WE ARE OBLIGED TO DISSOLVE PARTNERSHIP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-16 L. FRANK BAUM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-17 BLUG!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-18 MAJESTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-19 NOMES ARE GOOD FIGHTERS BUT THEY ARE NOT STRONG ENOUGH TO CONQUER THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-20 HIM FLAT UPON THE GROUND WHERE HE LAY MOTIONLESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-01-21 THIS NOME KING WAS NAMED ROQUAT THE RED AND NO ONE LOVED HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-01 CHAPTER TWO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-02 HOW UNCLE HENRY GOT INTO TROUBLE DOROTHY GALE LIVED ON A FARM IN KANSAS WITH HER AUNT EM AND HER UNCLE HENRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-03 IT WAS NOT A BIG FARM NOR A VERY GOOD ONE BECAUSE SOMETIMES THE RAIN DID NOT COME WHEN THE CROPS NEEDED IT AND THEN EVERYTHING WITHERED AND DRIED UP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-04 ONCE A CYCLONE HAD CARRIED AWAY UNCLE HENRY'S HOUSE SO THAT HE WAS OBLIGED TO BUILD ANOTHER,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-05 AND AS HE WAS A POOR MAN HE HAD TO MORTGAGE HIS FARM TO GET THE MONEY TO PAY FOR THE NEW HOUSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-06 THEN HIS HEALTH BECAME BAD AND HE WAS TOO FEEBLE TO WORK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-07 THE DOCTOR ORDERED HIM TO TAKE A SEA VOYAGE AND HE WENT TO AUSTRALIA AND TOOK DOROTHY WITH HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-08 THAT COST A LOT OF MONEY TOO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-09 UNCLE HENRY GREW POORER EVERY YEAR AND THE CROPS RAISED ON THE FARM ONLY BOUGHT FOOD FOR THE FAMILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-10 THEREFORE THE MORTGAGE COULD NOT BE PAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-11 AT LAST THE BANKER WHO HAD LOANED HIM THE MONEY SAID THAT IF HE DID NOT PAY ON A CERTAIN DAY HIS FARM WOULD BE TAKEN AWAY FROM HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-12 THIS WORRIED UNCLE HENRY A GOOD DEAL FOR WITHOUT THE FARM HE WOULD HAVE NO WAY TO EARN A LIVING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-13 HE WAS A GOOD MAN AND WORKED IN THE FIELD AS HARD AS HE COULD,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-14 AND AUNT EM DID ALL THE HOUSEWORK WITH DOROTHY'S HELP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-15 YET THEY DID NOT SEEM TO GET ALONG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-16 THIS LITTLE GIRL DOROTHY WAS LIKE DOZENS OF LITTLE GIRLS YOU KNOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-17 SHE WAS LOVING AND USUALLY SWEET TEMPERED AND HAD A ROUND ROSY FACE AND EARNEST EYES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-18 LIFE WAS A SERIOUS THING TO DOROTHY AND A WONDERFUL THING TOO FOR SHE HAD ENCOUNTERED MORE STRANGE ADVENTURES IN HER SHORT LIFE THAN MANY OTHER GIRLS OF HER AGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-19 AUNT EM ONCE SAID SHE THOUGHT THE FAIRIES MUST HAVE MARKED DOROTHY AT HER BIRTH BECAUSE SHE HAD WANDERED INTO STRANGE PLACES AND HAD ALWAYS BEEN PROTECTED BY SOME UNSEEN POWER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-20 AS FOR UNCLE HENRY HE THOUGHT HIS LITTLE NIECE MERELY A DREAMER AS HER DEAD MOTHER HAD BEEN FOR HE COULD NOT QUITE BELIEVE ALL THE CURIOUS STORIES DOROTHY TOLD THEM OF THE LAND OF OZ WHICH SHE HAD SEVERAL TIMES VISITED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-21 HE DID NOT THINK THAT SHE TRIED TO DECEIVE HER UNCLE AND AUNT BUT HE IMAGINED THAT SHE HAD DREAMED ALL OF THOSE ASTONISHING ADVENTURES AND THAT THE DREAMS HAD BEEN SO REAL TO HER THAT SHE HAD COME TO BELIEVE THEM TRUE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-22 WHATEVER THE EXPLANATION MIGHT BE IT WAS CERTAIN THAT DOROTHY HAD BEEN ABSENT FROM HER KANSAS HOME FOR SEVERAL LONG PERIODS ALWAYS DISAPPEARING UNEXPECTEDLY YET ALWAYS COMING BACK SAFE AND SOUND WITH AMAZING TALES OF WHERE SHE HAD BEEN AND THE UNUSUAL PEOPLE SHE HAD MET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-23 HER UNCLE AND AUNT LISTENED TO HER STORIES EAGERLY AND IN SPITE OF THEIR DOUBTS BEGAN TO FEEL THAT THE LITTLE GIRL HAD GAINED A LOT OF EXPERIENCE AND WISDOM THAT WERE UNACCOUNTABLE IN THIS AGE WHEN FAIRIES ARE SUPPOSED NO LONGER TO EXIST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-24 MOST OF DOROTHY'S STORIES WERE ABOUT THE LAND OF OZ WITH ITS BEAUTIFUL EMERALD CITY AND A LOVELY GIRL RULER NAMED OZMA WHO WAS THE MOST FAITHFUL FRIEND OF THE LITTLE KANSAS GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-25 WHEN DOROTHY TOLD ABOUT THE RICHES OF THIS FAIRY COUNTRY UNCLE HENRY WOULD SIGH FOR HE KNEW THAT A SINGLE ONE OF THE GREAT EMERALDS THAT WERE SO COMMON THERE WOULD PAY ALL HIS DEBTS AND LEAVE HIS FARM FREE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-26 BUT DOROTHY NEVER BROUGHT ANY JEWELS HOME WITH HER SO THEIR POVERTY BECAME GREATER EVERY YEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-27 WHEN THE BANKER TOLD UNCLE HENRY THAT HE MUST PAY THE MONEY IN THIRTY DAYS OR LEAVE THE FARM THE POOR MAN WAS IN DESPAIR AS HE KNEW HE COULD NOT POSSIBLY GET THE MONEY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-28 SO HE TOLD HIS WIFE AUNT EM OF HIS TROUBLE AND SHE FIRST CRIED A LITTLE AND THEN SAID THAT THEY MUST BE BRAVE AND DO THE BEST THEY COULD AND GO AWAY SOMEWHERE AND TRY TO EARN AN HONEST LIVING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-29 BUT THEY WERE GETTING OLD AND FEEBLE AND SHE FEARED THAT THEY COULD NOT TAKE CARE OF DOROTHY AS WELL AS THEY HAD FORMERLY DONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-30 PROBABLY THE LITTLE GIRL WOULD ALSO BE OBLIGED TO GO TO WORK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-31 THEY DID NOT TELL THEIR NIECE THE SAD NEWS FOR SEVERAL DAYS NOT WISHING TO MAKE HER UNHAPPY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-32 BUT ONE MORNING THE LITTLE GIRL FOUND AUNT EM SOFTLY CRYING WHILE UNCLE HENRY TRIED TO COMFORT HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-33 THEN DOROTHY ASKED THEM TO TELL HER WHAT WAS THE MATTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-34 WE MUST GIVE UP THE FARM MY DEAR REPLIED HER UNCLE SADLY AND WANDER AWAY INTO THE WORLD TO WORK FOR OUR LIVING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-35 THE GIRL LISTENED QUITE SERIOUSLY FOR SHE HAD NOT KNOWN BEFORE HOW DESPERATELY POOR THEY WERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-36 WE DON'T MIND FOR OURSELVES SAID HER AUNT STROKING THE LITTLE GIRL'S HEAD TENDERLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-37 BUT WE LOVE YOU AS IF YOU WERE OUR OWN CHILD AND WE ARE HEART BROKEN TO THINK THAT YOU MUST ALSO ENDURE POVERTY AND WORK FOR A LIVING BEFORE YOU HAVE GROWN BIG AND STRONG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-38 WHAT COULD I DO TO EARN MONEY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-39 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-40 YOU MIGHT DO HOUSEWORK FOR SOME ONE DEAR YOU ARE SO HANDY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-41 OR PERHAPS YOU COULD BE A NURSE MAID TO LITTLE CHILDREN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-42 I'M SURE I DON'T KNOW EXACTLY WHAT YOU CAN DO TO EARN MONEY BUT IF YOUR UNCLE AND I ARE ABLE TO SUPPORT YOU WE WILL DO IT WILLINGLY AND SEND YOU TO SCHOOL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-43 WE FEAR THOUGH THAT WE SHALL HAVE MUCH TROUBLE IN EARNING A LIVING FOR OURSELVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-44 NO ONE WANTS TO EMPLOY OLD PEOPLE WHO ARE BROKEN DOWN IN HEALTH AS WE ARE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-45 DOROTHY SMILED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-46 WOULDN'T IT BE FUNNY SHE SAID FOR ME TO DO HOUSEWORK IN KANSAS WHEN I'M A PRINCESS IN THE LAND OF OZ?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-47 A PRINCESS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-48 THEY BOTH EXCLAIMED ASTONISHED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-49 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-50 OZMA MADE ME A PRINCESS SOME TIME AGO AND SHE HAS OFTEN BEGGED ME TO COME AND LIVE ALWAYS IN THE EMERALD CITY SAID THE CHILD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-51 HER UNCLE AND AUNT LOOKED AT HER IN AMAZEMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-52 THEN THE MAN SAID, DO YOU SUPPOSE YOU COULD MANAGE TO RETURN TO YOUR FAIRYLAND MY DEAR?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-53 OH YES REPLIED DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-54 I COULD DO THAT EASILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-55 HOW?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-56 ASKED AUNT EM. OZMA SEES ME EVERY DAY AT FOUR O'CLOCK IN HER MAGIC PICTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-57 SHE CAN SEE ME WHEREVER I AM NO MATTER WHAT I AM DOING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-58 AND AT THAT TIME IF I MAKE A CERTAIN SECRET SIGN SHE WILL SEND FOR ME BY MEANS OF THE MAGIC BELT WHICH I ONCE CAPTURED FROM THE NOME KING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-59 THEN IN THE WINK OF AN EYE I SHALL BE WITH OZMA IN HER PALACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-60 THE ELDER PEOPLE REMAINED SILENT FOR SOME TIME AFTER DOROTHY HAD SPOKEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-61 FINALLY AUNT EM SAID WITH ANOTHER SIGH OF REGRET, IF THAT IS THE CASE DOROTHY PERHAPS YOU'D BETTER GO AND LIVE IN THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-62 IT WILL BREAK OUR HEARTS TO LOSE YOU FROM OUR LIVES BUT YOU WILL BE SO MUCH BETTER OFF WITH YOUR FAIRY FRIENDS THAT IT SEEMS WISEST AND BEST FOR YOU TO GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-63 I'M NOT SO SURE ABOUT THAT REMARKED UNCLE HENRY SHAKING HIS GRAY HEAD DOUBTFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-64 THESE THINGS ALL SEEM REAL TO DOROTHY I KNOW,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-65 BUT I'M AFRAID OUR LITTLE GIRL WON'T FIND HER FAIRYLAND JUST WHAT SHE HAD DREAMED IT TO BE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-66 IT WOULD MAKE ME VERY UNHAPPY TO THINK THAT SHE WAS WANDERING AMONG STRANGERS WHO MIGHT BE UNKIND TO HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-67 DOROTHY LAUGHED MERRILY AT THIS SPEECH AND THEN SHE BECAME VERY SOBER AGAIN FOR SHE COULD SEE HOW ALL THIS TROUBLE WAS WORRYING HER AUNT AND UNCLE AND KNEW THAT UNLESS SHE FOUND A WAY TO HELP THEM THEIR FUTURE LIVES WOULD BE QUITE MISERABLE AND UNHAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-68 SHE KNEW THAT SHE COULD HELP THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-69 SHE HAD THOUGHT OF A WAY ALREADY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-70 YET SHE DID NOT TELL THEM AT ONCE WHAT IT WAS BECAUSE SHE MUST ASK OZMA'S CONSENT BEFORE SHE WOULD BE ABLE TO CARRY OUT HER PLANS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-71 SO SHE ONLY SAID, IF YOU WILL PROMISE NOT TO WORRY A BIT ABOUT ME I'LL GO TO THE LAND OF OZ THIS VERY AFTERNOON.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-72 AND I'LL MAKE A PROMISE TOO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-73 THAT YOU SHALL BOTH SEE ME AGAIN BEFORE THE DAY COMES WHEN YOU MUST LEAVE THIS FARM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-74 THE DAY ISN'T FAR AWAY NOW HER UNCLE SADLY REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-75 I DID NOT TELL YOU OF OUR TROUBLE UNTIL I WAS OBLIGED TO DEAR DOROTHY SO THE EVIL TIME IS NEAR AT HAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-76 BUT IF YOU ARE QUITE SURE YOUR FAIRY FRIENDS WILL GIVE YOU A HOME IT WILL BE BEST FOR YOU TO GO TO THEM AS YOUR AUNT SAYS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-77 THAT WAS WHY DOROTHY WENT TO HER LITTLE ROOM IN THE ATTIC THAT AFTERNOON TAKING WITH HER A SMALL DOG NAMED TOTO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-78 THE DOG HAD CURLY BLACK HAIR AND BIG BROWN EYES AND LOVED DOROTHY VERY DEARLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-79 THE CHILD HAD KISSED HER UNCLE AND AUNT AFFECTIONATELY BEFORE SHE WENT UPSTAIRS AND NOW SHE LOOKED AROUND HER LITTLE ROOM RATHER WISTFULLY GAZING AT THE SIMPLE TRINKETS AND WORN CALICO AND GINGHAM DRESSES AS IF THEY WERE OLD FRIENDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-80 SHE WAS TEMPTED AT FIRST TO MAKE A BUNDLE OF THEM YET SHE KNEW VERY WELL THAT THEY WOULD BE OF NO USE TO HER IN HER FUTURE LIFE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-81 SHE SAT DOWN UPON A BROKEN BACKED CHAIR THE ONLY ONE THE ROOM CONTAINED AND HOLDING TOTO IN HER ARMS WAITED PATIENTLY UNTIL THE CLOCK STRUCK FOUR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-82 THEN SHE MADE THE SECRET SIGNAL THAT HAD BEEN AGREED UPON BETWEEN HER AND OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-83 UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM WAITED DOWNSTAIRS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-84 THEY WERE UNEASY AND A GOOD DEAL EXCITED FOR THIS IS A PRACTICAL HUMDRUM WORLD AND IT SEEMED TO THEM QUITE IMPOSSIBLE THAT THEIR LITTLE NIECE COULD VANISH FROM HER HOME AND TRAVEL INSTANTLY TO FAIRYLAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-85 SO THEY WATCHED THE STAIRS WHICH SEEMED TO BE THE ONLY WAY THAT DOROTHY COULD GET OUT OF THE FARMHOUSE AND THEY WATCHED THEM A LONG TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-86 THEY HEARD THE CLOCK STRIKE FOUR BUT THERE WAS NO SOUND FROM ABOVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-87 HALF PAST FOUR CAME AND NOW THEY WERE TOO IMPATIENT TO WAIT ANY LONGER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-88 SOFTLY THEY CREPT UP THE STAIRS TO THE DOOR OF THE LITTLE GIRL'S ROOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-89 DOROTHY!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-90 DOROTHY!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-91 THEY CALLED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-92 THERE WAS NO ANSWER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-93 THEY OPENED THE DOOR AND LOOKED IN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-02-94 THE ROOM WAS EMPTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-01 CHAPTER THREE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-02 HOW OZMA GRANTED DOROTHY'S REQUEST I SUPPOSE YOU HAVE READ SO MUCH ABOUT THE MAGNIFICENT EMERALD CITY THAT THERE IS LITTLE NEED FOR ME TO DESCRIBE IT HERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-03 IT IS THE CAPITAL CITY OF THE LAND OF OZ WHICH IS JUSTLY CONSIDERED THE MOST ATTRACTIVE AND DELIGHTFUL FAIRYLAND IN ALL THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-04 THE EMERALD CITY IS BUILT ALL OF BEAUTIFUL MARBLES IN WHICH ARE SET A PROFUSION OF EMERALDS EVERY ONE EXQUISITELY CUT AND OF VERY GREAT SIZE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-05 THERE ARE OTHER JEWELS USED IN THE DECORATIONS INSIDE THE HOUSES AND PALACES SUCH AS RUBIES DIAMONDS SAPPHIRES AMETHYSTS AND TURQUOISES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-06 BUT IN THE STREETS AND UPON THE OUTSIDE OF THE BUILDINGS ONLY EMERALDS APPEAR FROM WHICH CIRCUMSTANCE THE PLACE IS NAMED THE EMERALD CITY OF OZ. IT HAS NINE THOUSAND SIX HUNDRED AND FIFTY FOUR BUILDINGS IN WHICH LIVED FIFTY SEVEN THOUSAND THREE HUNDRED AND EIGHTEEN PEOPLE UP TO THE TIME MY STORY OPENS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-07 ALL THE SURROUNDING COUNTRY EXTENDING TO THE BORDERS OF THE DESERT WHICH ENCLOSED IT UPON EVERY SIDE WAS FULL OF PRETTY AND COMFORTABLE FARMHOUSES IN WHICH RESIDED THOSE INHABITANTS OF OZ WHO PREFERRED COUNTRY TO CITY LIFE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-08 ALTOGETHER THERE WERE MORE THAN HALF A MILLION PEOPLE IN THE LAND OF OZ ALTHOUGH SOME OF THEM AS YOU WILL SOON LEARN WERE NOT MADE OF FLESH AND BLOOD AS WE ARE AND EVERY INHABITANT OF THAT FAVORED COUNTRY WAS HAPPY AND PROSPEROUS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-09 NO DISEASE OF ANY SORT WAS EVER KNOWN AMONG THE OZITES AND SO NO ONE EVER DIED UNLESS HE MET WITH AN ACCIDENT THAT PREVENTED HIM FROM LIVING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-10 THIS HAPPENED VERY SELDOM INDEED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-11 THERE WERE NO POOR PEOPLE IN THE LAND OF OZ BECAUSE THERE WAS NO SUCH THING AS MONEY AND ALL PROPERTY OF EVERY SORT BELONGED TO THE RULER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-12 THE PEOPLE WERE HER CHILDREN AND SHE CARED FOR THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-13 EACH PERSON WAS GIVEN FREELY BY HIS NEIGHBORS WHATEVER HE REQUIRED FOR HIS USE WHICH IS AS MUCH AS ANY ONE MAY REASONABLY DESIRE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-14 SOME TILLED THE LANDS AND RAISED GREAT CROPS OF GRAIN WHICH WAS DIVIDED EQUALLY AMONG THE ENTIRE POPULATION SO THAT ALL HAD ENOUGH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-15 THERE WERE MANY TAILORS AND DRESSMAKERS AND SHOEMAKERS AND THE LIKE WHO MADE THINGS THAT ANY WHO DESIRED THEM MIGHT WEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-16 LIKEWISE THERE WERE JEWELERS WHO MADE ORNAMENTS FOR THE PERSON WHICH PLEASED AND BEAUTIFIED THE PEOPLE AND THESE ORNAMENTS ALSO WERE FREE TO THOSE WHO ASKED FOR THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-17 EACH MAN AND WOMAN NO MATTER WHAT HE OR SHE PRODUCED FOR THE GOOD OF THE COMMUNITY WAS SUPPLIED BY THE NEIGHBORS WITH FOOD AND CLOTHING AND A HOUSE AND FURNITURE AND ORNAMENTS AND GAMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-18 IF BY CHANCE THE SUPPLY EVER RAN SHORT MORE WAS TAKEN FROM THE GREAT STOREHOUSES OF THE RULER WHICH WERE AFTERWARD FILLED UP AGAIN WHEN THERE WAS MORE OF ANY ARTICLE THAN THE PEOPLE NEEDED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-19 EVERY ONE WORKED HALF THE TIME AND PLAYED HALF THE TIME AND THE PEOPLE ENJOYED THE WORK AS MUCH AS THEY DID THE PLAY BECAUSE IT IS GOOD TO BE OCCUPIED AND TO HAVE SOMETHING TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-20 THERE WERE NO CRUEL OVERSEERS SET TO WATCH THEM AND NO ONE TO REBUKE THEM OR TO FIND FAULT WITH THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-21 SO EACH ONE WAS PROUD TO DO ALL HE COULD FOR HIS FRIENDS AND NEIGHBORS AND WAS GLAD WHEN THEY WOULD ACCEPT THE THINGS HE PRODUCED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-22 YOU WILL KNOW BY WHAT I HAVE HERE TOLD YOU THAT THE LAND OF OZ WAS A REMARKABLE COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-23 I DO NOT SUPPOSE SUCH AN ARRANGEMENT WOULD BE PRACTICAL WITH US BUT DOROTHY ASSURES ME THAT IT WORKS FINELY WITH THE OZ PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-24 OZ BEING A FAIRY COUNTRY THE PEOPLE WERE OF COURSE FAIRY PEOPLE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-25 BUT THAT DOES NOT MEAN THAT ALL OF THEM WERE VERY UNLIKE THE PEOPLE OF OUR OWN WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-26 THERE WERE ALL SORTS OF QUEER CHARACTERS AMONG THEM BUT NOT A SINGLE ONE WHO WAS EVIL OR WHO POSSESSED A SELFISH OR VIOLENT NATURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-27 THEY WERE PEACEFUL KIND HEARTED LOVING AND MERRY AND EVERY INHABITANT ADORED THE BEAUTIFUL GIRL WHO RULED THEM AND DELIGHTED TO OBEY HER EVERY COMMAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-28 IN SPITE OF ALL I HAVE SAID IN A GENERAL WAY THERE WERE SOME PARTS OF THE LAND OF OZ NOT QUITE SO PLEASANT AS THE FARMING COUNTRY AND THE EMERALD CITY WHICH WAS ITS CENTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-29 FAR AWAY IN THE SOUTH COUNTRY THERE LIVED IN THE MOUNTAINS A BAND OF STRANGE PEOPLE CALLED HAMMER HEADS BECAUSE THEY HAD NO ARMS AND USED THEIR FLAT HEADS TO POUND ANY ONE WHO CAME NEAR THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-30 THEIR NECKS WERE LIKE RUBBER SO THAT THEY COULD SHOOT OUT THEIR HEADS TO QUITE A DISTANCE AND AFTERWARD DRAW THEM BACK AGAIN TO THEIR SHOULDERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-31 THE HAMMER HEADS WERE CALLED THE WILD PEOPLE BUT NEVER HARMED ANY BUT THOSE WHO DISTURBED THEM IN THE MOUNTAINS WHERE THEY LIVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-32 IN SOME OF THE DENSE FORESTS THERE LIVED GREAT BEASTS OF EVERY SORT,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-33 YET THESE WERE FOR THE MOST PART HARMLESS AND EVEN SOCIABLE AND CONVERSED AGREEABLY WITH THOSE WHO VISITED THEIR HAUNTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-34 THE KALIDAHS BEASTS WITH BODIES LIKE BEARS AND HEADS LIKE TIGERS HAD ONCE BEEN FIERCE AND BLOODTHIRSTY BUT EVEN THEY WERE NOW NEARLY ALL TAMED ALTHOUGH AT TIMES ONE OR ANOTHER OF THEM WOULD GET CROSS AND DISAGREEABLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-35 NOT SO TAME WERE THE FIGHTING TREES WHICH HAD A FOREST OF THEIR OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-36 IF ANY ONE APPROACHED THEM THESE CURIOUS TREES WOULD BEND DOWN THEIR BRANCHES TWINE THEM AROUND THE INTRUDERS AND HURL THEM AWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-37 BUT THESE UNPLEASANT THINGS EXISTED ONLY IN A FEW REMOTE PARTS OF THE LAND OF OZ. I SUPPOSE EVERY COUNTRY HAS SOME DRAWBACKS SO EVEN THIS ALMOST PERFECT FAIRYLAND COULD NOT BE QUITE PERFECT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-38 ONCE THERE HAD BEEN WICKED WITCHES IN THE LAND TOO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-39 BUT NOW THESE HAD ALL BEEN DESTROYED,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-40 SO AS I SAID ONLY PEACE AND HAPPINESS REIGNED IN OZ. FOR SOME TIME OZMA HAD RULED OVER THIS FAIR COUNTRY AND NEVER WAS RULER MORE POPULAR OR BELOVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-41 SHE IS SAID TO BE THE MOST BEAUTIFUL GIRL THE WORLD HAS EVER KNOWN AND HER HEART AND MIND ARE AS LOVELY AS HER PERSON.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-42 DOROTHY GALE HAD SEVERAL TIMES VISITED THE EMERALD CITY AND EXPERIENCED ADVENTURES IN THE LAND OF OZ SO THAT SHE AND OZMA HAD NOW BECOME FIRM FRIENDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-43 THE GIRL RULER HAD EVEN MADE DOROTHY A PRINCESS OF OZ AND HAD OFTEN IMPLORED HER TO COME TO OZMA'S STATELY PALACE AND LIVE THERE ALWAYS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-44 BUT DOROTHY HAD BEEN LOYAL TO HER AUNT EM AND UNCLE HENRY WHO HAD CARED FOR HER SINCE SHE WAS A BABY AND SHE HAD REFUSED TO LEAVE THEM BECAUSE SHE KNEW THEY WOULD BE LONELY WITHOUT HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-45 HOWEVER DOROTHY NOW REALIZED THAT THINGS WERE GOING TO BE DIFFERENT WITH HER UNCLE AND AUNT FROM THIS TIME FORTH SO AFTER GIVING THE MATTER DEEP THOUGHT SHE DECIDED TO ASK OZMA TO GRANT HER A VERY GREAT FAVOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-46 A FEW SECONDS AFTER SHE HAD MADE THE SECRET SIGNAL IN HER LITTLE BEDCHAMBER THE KANSAS GIRL WAS SEATED IN A LOVELY ROOM IN OZMA'S PALACE IN THE EMERALD CITY OF OZ. WHEN THE FIRST LOVING KISSES AND EMBRACES HAD BEEN EXCHANGED THE FAIR RULER INQUIRED, WHAT IS THE MATTER DEAR?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-47 I KNOW SOMETHING UNPLEASANT HAS HAPPENED TO YOU FOR YOUR FACE WAS VERY SOBER WHEN I SAW IT IN MY MAGIC PICTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-48 AND WHENEVER YOU SIGNAL ME TO TRANSPORT YOU TO THIS SAFE PLACE WHERE YOU ARE ALWAYS WELCOME I KNOW YOU ARE IN DANGER OR IN TROUBLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-49 DOROTHY SIGHED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-50 THIS TIME OZMA IT ISN'T I SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-51 BUT IT'S WORSE I GUESS FOR UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM ARE IN A HEAP OF TROUBLE AND THERE SEEMS NO WAY FOR THEM TO GET OUT OF IT ANYHOW NOT WHILE THEY LIVE IN KANSAS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-52 TELL ME ABOUT IT DOROTHY SAID OZMA WITH READY SYMPATHY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-56 COURSE HE SPECTED TO PAY BY MAKING MONEY FROM THE FARM,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-57 BUT HE JUST COULDN'T.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-58 AN SO THEY'RE GOING TO TAKE THE FARM AND UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM WON'T HAVE ANY PLACE TO LIVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-59 THEY'RE PRETTY OLD TO DO MUCH HARD WORK OZMA,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-60 SO I'LL HAVE TO WORK FOR THEM UNLESS OZMA HAD BEEN THOUGHTFUL DURING THE STORY BUT NOW SHE SMILED AND PRESSED HER LITTLE FRIEND'S HAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-61 UNLESS WHAT DEAR?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-62 SHE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-03-63 DOROTHY HESITATED BECAUSE HER REQUEST MEANT SO MUCH TO THEM ALL.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-01 CHAPTER FOUR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-02 HOW THE NOME KING PLANNED REVENGE THE REASON MOST PEOPLE ARE BAD IS BECAUSE THEY DO NOT TRY TO BE GOOD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-03 NOW THE NOME KING HAD NEVER TRIED TO BE GOOD SO HE WAS VERY BAD INDEED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-04 HAVING DECIDED TO CONQUER THE LAND OF OZ AND TO DESTROY THE EMERALD CITY AND ENSLAVE ALL ITS PEOPLE KING ROQUAT THE RED KEPT PLANNING WAYS TO DO THIS DREADFUL THING AND THE MORE HE PLANNED THE MORE HE BELIEVED HE WOULD BE ABLE TO ACCOMPLISH IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-05 ABOUT THE TIME DOROTHY WENT TO OZMA THE NOME KING CALLED HIS CHIEF STEWARD TO HIM AND SAID, KALIKO I THINK I SHALL MAKE YOU THE GENERAL OF MY ARMIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-06 I THINK YOU WON'T REPLIED KALIKO POSITIVELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-07 WHY NOT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-08 INQUIRED THE KING REACHING FOR HIS SCEPTER WITH THE BIG SAPPHIRE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-09 BECAUSE I'M YOUR CHIEF STEWARD AND KNOW NOTHING OF WARFARE SAID KALIKO PREPARING TO DODGE IF ANYTHING WERE THROWN AT HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-10 I MANAGE ALL THE AFFAIRS OF YOUR KINGDOM BETTER THAN YOU COULD YOURSELF AND YOU'LL NEVER FIND ANOTHER STEWARD AS GOOD AS I AM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-11 BUT THERE ARE A HUNDRED NOMES BETTER FITTED TO COMMAND YOUR ARMY AND YOUR GENERALS GET THROWN AWAY SO OFTEN THAT I HAVE NO DESIRE TO BE ONE OF THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-12 AH THERE IS SOME TRUTH IN YOUR REMARKS KALIKO REMARKED THE KING DECIDING NOT TO THROW THE SCEPTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-13 SUMMON MY ARMY TO ASSEMBLE IN THE GREAT CAVERN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-14 KALIKO BOWED AND RETIRED AND IN A FEW MINUTES RETURNED TO SAY THAT THE ARMY WAS ASSEMBLED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-15 SO THE KING WENT OUT UPON A BALCONY THAT OVERLOOKED THE GREAT CAVERN WHERE FIFTY THOUSAND NOMES ALL ARMED WITH SWORDS AND PIKES STOOD MARSHALED IN MILITARY ARRAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-16 WHEN THEY WERE NOT REQUIRED AS SOLDIERS ALL THESE NOMES WERE METAL WORKERS AND MINERS AND THEY HAD HAMMERED SO MUCH AT THE FORGES AND DUG SO HARD WITH PICK AND SHOVEL THAT THEY HAD ACQUIRED GREAT MUSCULAR STRENGTH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-17 THEY WERE STRANGELY FORMED CREATURES RATHER ROUND AND NOT VERY TALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-18 THEIR TOES WERE CURLY AND THEIR EARS BROAD AND FLAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-19 IN TIME OF WAR EVERY NOME LEFT HIS FORGE OR MINE AND BECAME PART OF THE GREAT ARMY OF KING ROQUAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-20 THE SOLDIERS WORE ROCK COLORED UNIFORMS AND WERE EXCELLENTLY DRILLED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-21 THE KING LOOKED UPON THIS TREMENDOUS ARMY WHICH STOOD SILENTLY ARRAYED BEFORE HIM AND A CRUEL SMILE CURLED THE CORNERS OF HIS MOUTH FOR HE SAW THAT HIS LEGIONS WERE VERY POWERFUL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-22 THEN HE ADDRESSED THEM FROM THE BALCONY SAYING, I HAVE THROWN AWAY GENERAL BLUG BECAUSE HE DID NOT PLEASE ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-23 SO I WANT ANOTHER GENERAL TO COMMAND THIS ARMY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-24 WHO IS NEXT IN COMMAND?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-25 I AM REPLIED COLONEL CRINKLE A DAPPER LOOKING NOME AS HE STEPPED FORWARD TO SALUTE HIS MONARCH.

WHEN YOU GET THERE I WANT YOU TO CONQUER THE OZ PEOPLE DESTROY THEM AND THEIR CITY AND BRING ALL THEIR GOLD AND SILVER AND PRECIOUS STONES BACK TO MY CAVERN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-27 ALSO YOU ARE TO RECAPTURE MY MAGIC BELT AND RETURN IT TO ME.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-30 FOR IT CAN'T BE DONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-31 OH INDEED!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-32 EXCLAIMED THE KING.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-35 AFTERWARD YOU MAY FEED HIM TO THE SEVEN HEADED DOGS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-63 VERY GOOD INDEED!

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-95 AND THE REASON I WON'T IS BECAUSE WHEN I MARCH I'LL HAVE ALL MY PLANS MADE AND A HOST OF ALLIES TO ASSIST MY NOMES.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-97 ASKED THE KING.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-111 AGAINST OZMA YOU AND YOUR NOMES WOULD HAVE NO SHOW AT ALL.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-120 IT'S ALL VERY SIMPLE AND EASY WHEN YOU KNOW HOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-121 ALONE WE SHOULD BE HELPLESS TO INJURE THE RULER OF OZ BUT WITH THE AID OF THE EVIL POWERS WE CAN SUMMON WE SHALL EASILY SUCCEED.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-124 HE EXCLAIMED HIS EYES SPARKLING WITH JOY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-125 YOU MUST GO AT ONCE AND MAKE ARRANGEMENTS WITH THE EVIL POWERS TO ASSIST US AND MEANTIME I'LL BEGIN TO DIG THE TUNNEL.
