l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-04-127 I'LL START THIS VERY AFTERNOON TO VISIT THE CHIEF OF THE WHIMSIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-01 CHAPTER FIVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-02 HOW DOROTHY BECAME A PRINCESS WHEN THE PEOPLE OF THE EMERALD CITY HEARD THAT DOROTHY HAD RETURNED TO THEM EVERY ONE WAS EAGER TO SEE HER FOR THE LITTLE GIRL WAS A GENERAL FAVORITE IN THE LAND OF OZ. FROM TIME TO TIME SOME OF THE FOLK FROM THE GREAT OUTSIDE WORLD HAD FOUND THEIR WAY INTO THIS FAIRYLAND BUT ALL EXCEPT ONE HAD BEEN COMPANIONS OF DOROTHY AND HAD TURNED OUT TO BE VERY AGREEABLE PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-03 THE EXCEPTION I SPEAK OF WAS THE WONDERFUL WIZARD OF OZ A SLEIGHT OF HAND PERFORMER FROM OMAHA WHO WENT UP IN A BALLOON AND WAS CARRIED BY A CURRENT OF AIR TO THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-04 HIS QUEER AND PUZZLING TRICKS MADE THE PEOPLE OF OZ BELIEVE HIM A GREAT WIZARD FOR A TIME AND HE RULED OVER THEM UNTIL DOROTHY ARRIVED ON HER FIRST VISIT AND SHOWED THE WIZARD TO BE A MERE HUMBUG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-05 HE WAS A GENTLE KIND HEARTED LITTLE MAN AND DOROTHY GREW TO LIKE HIM AFTERWARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-06 WHEN AFTER AN ABSENCE THE WIZARD RETURNED TO THE LAND OF OZ OZMA RECEIVED HIM GRACIOUSLY AND GAVE HIM A HOME IN A PART OF THE PALACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-07 IN ADDITION TO THE WIZARD TWO OTHER PERSONAGES FROM THE OUTSIDE WORLD HAD BEEN ALLOWED TO MAKE THEIR HOME IN THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-08 THE FIRST WAS A QUAINT SHAGGY MAN WHOM OZMA HAD MADE THE GOVERNOR OF THE ROYAL STOREHOUSES AND THE SECOND A YELLOW HEN NAMED BILLINA WHO HAD A FINE HOUSE IN THE GARDENS BACK OF THE PALACE WHERE SHE LOOKED AFTER A LARGE FAMILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-09 BOTH THESE HAD BEEN OLD COMRADES OF DOROTHY SO YOU SEE THE LITTLE GIRL WAS QUITE AN IMPORTANT PERSONAGE IN OZ AND THE PEOPLE THOUGHT SHE HAD BROUGHT THEM GOOD LUCK AND LOVED HER NEXT BEST TO OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-10 DURING HER SEVERAL VISITS THIS LITTLE GIRL HAD BEEN THE MEANS OF DESTROYING TWO WICKED WITCHES WHO OPPRESSED THE PEOPLE AND SHE HAD DISCOVERED A LIVE SCARECROW WHO WAS NOW ONE OF THE MOST POPULAR PERSONAGES IN ALL THE FAIRY COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-11 WITH THE SCARECROW'S HELP SHE HAD RESCUED NICK CHOPPER A TIN WOODMAN WHO HAD RUSTED IN A LONELY FOREST AND THE TIN MAN WAS NOW THE EMPEROR OF THE COUNTRY OF THE WINKIES AND MUCH BELOVED BECAUSE OF HIS KIND HEART.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-12 NO WONDER THE PEOPLE THOUGHT DOROTHY HAD BROUGHT THEM GOOD LUCK!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-13 YET STRANGE AS IT MAY SEEM SHE HAD ACCOMPLISHED ALL THESE WONDERS NOT BECAUSE SHE WAS A FAIRY OR HAD ANY MAGICAL POWERS WHATEVER BUT BECAUSE SHE WAS A SIMPLE SWEET AND TRUE LITTLE GIRL WHO WAS HONEST TO HERSELF AND TO ALL WHOM SHE MET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-14 IN THIS WORLD IN WHICH WE LIVE SIMPLICITY AND KINDNESS ARE THE ONLY MAGIC WANDS THAT WORK WONDERS AND IN THE LAND OF OZ DOROTHY FOUND THESE SAME QUALITIES HAD WON FOR HER THE LOVE AND ADMIRATION OF THE PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-15 INDEED THE LITTLE GIRL HAD MADE MANY WARM FRIENDS IN THE FAIRY COUNTRY AND THE ONLY REAL GRIEF THE OZITES HAD EVER EXPERIENCED WAS WHEN DOROTHY LEFT THEM AND RETURNED TO HER KANSAS HOME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-16 NOW SHE RECEIVED A JOYFUL WELCOME ALTHOUGH NO ONE EXCEPT OZMA KNEW AT FIRST THAT SHE HAD FINALLY COME TO STAY FOR GOOD AND ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-17 THAT EVENING DOROTHY HAD MANY CALLERS AND AMONG THEM WERE SUCH IMPORTANT PEOPLE AS TIKTOK A MACHINE MAN WHO THOUGHT AND SPOKE AND MOVED BY CLOCKWORK,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-18 HER OLD COMPANION THE GENIAL SHAGGY MAN,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-19 JACK PUMPKINHEAD WHOSE BODY WAS BRUSH WOOD AND WHOSE HEAD WAS A RIPE PUMPKIN WITH A FACE CARVED UPON IT,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-20 THE COWARDLY LION AND THE HUNGRY TIGER TWO GREAT BEASTS FROM THE FOREST WHO SERVED PRINCESS OZMA AND PROFESSOR H. M. WOGGLEBUG TE THIS WOGGLEBUG WAS A REMARKABLE CREATURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-21 HE HAD ONCE BEEN A TINY LITTLE BUG CRAWLING AROUND IN A SCHOOL ROOM BUT HE WAS DISCOVERED AND HIGHLY MAGNIFIED SO THAT HE COULD BE SEEN MORE PLAINLY AND WHILE IN THIS MAGNIFIED CONDITION HE HAD ESCAPED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-22 HE HAD ALWAYS REMAINED BIG AND HE DRESSED LIKE A DANDY AND WAS SO FULL OF KNOWLEDGE AND INFORMATION WHICH ARE DISTINCT ACQUIREMENTS THAT HE HAD BEEN MADE A PROFESSOR AND THE HEAD OF THE ROYAL COLLEGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-23 DOROTHY HAD A NICE VISIT WITH THESE OLD FRIENDS AND ALSO TALKED A LONG TIME WITH THE WIZARD WHO WAS LITTLE AND OLD AND WITHERED AND DRIED UP BUT AS MERRY AND ACTIVE AS A CHILD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-24 AFTERWARD SHE WENT TO SEE BILLINA'S FAST GROWING FAMILY OF CHICKS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-25 TOTO DOROTHY'S LITTLE BLACK DOG ALSO MET WITH A CORDIAL RECEPTION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-26 TOTO WAS AN ESPECIAL FRIEND OF THE SHAGGY MAN AND HE KNEW EVERY ONE ELSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-27 BEING THE ONLY DOG IN THE LAND OF OZ HE WAS HIGHLY RESPECTED BY THE PEOPLE WHO BELIEVED ANIMALS ENTITLED TO EVERY CONSIDERATION IF THEY BEHAVED THEMSELVES PROPERLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-28 DOROTHY HAD FOUR LOVELY ROOMS IN THE PALACE WHICH WERE ALWAYS RESERVED FOR HER USE AND WERE CALLED DOROTHY'S ROOMS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-29 THESE CONSISTED OF A BEAUTIFUL SITTING ROOM A DRESSING ROOM A DAINTY BEDCHAMBER AND A BIG MARBLE BATHROOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-30 AND IN THESE ROOMS WERE EVERYTHING THAT HEART COULD DESIRE PLACED THERE WITH LOVING THOUGHTFULNESS BY OZMA FOR HER LITTLE FRIEND'S USE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-31 THE ROYAL DRESSMAKERS HAD THE LITTLE GIRL'S MEASURE SO THEY KEPT THE CLOSETS IN HER DRESSING ROOM FILLED WITH LOVELY DRESSES OF EVERY DESCRIPTION AND SUITABLE FOR EVERY OCCASION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-32 NO WONDER DOROTHY HAD REFRAINED FROM BRINGING WITH HER HER OLD CALICO AND GINGHAM DRESSES!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-33 HERE EVERYTHING THAT WAS DEAR TO A LITTLE GIRL'S HEART WAS SUPPLIED IN PROFUSION AND NOTHING SO RICH AND BEAUTIFUL COULD EVER HAVE BEEN FOUND IN THE BIGGEST DEPARTMENT STORES IN AMERICA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-34 OF COURSE DOROTHY ENJOYED ALL THESE LUXURIES AND THE ONLY REASON SHE HAD HERETOFORE PREFERRED TO LIVE IN KANSAS WAS BECAUSE HER UNCLE AND AUNT LOVED HER AND NEEDED HER WITH THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-35 NOW HOWEVER ALL WAS TO BE CHANGED AND DOROTHY WAS REALLY MORE DELIGHTED TO KNOW THAT HER DEAR RELATIVES WERE TO SHARE IN HER GOOD FORTUNE AND ENJOY THE DELIGHTS OF THE LAND OF OZ THAN SHE WAS TO POSSESS SUCH LUXURY FOR HERSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-36 NEXT MORNING AT OZMA'S REQUEST DOROTHY DRESSED HERSELF IN A PRETTY SKY BLUE GOWN OF RICH SILK TRIMMED WITH REAL PEARLS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-37 THE BUCKLES OF HER SHOES WERE SET WITH PEARLS TOO AND MORE OF THESE PRICELESS GEMS WERE ON A LOVELY CORONET WHICH SHE WORE UPON HER FOREHEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-38 FOR SAID HER FRIEND OZMA FROM THIS TIME FORTH MY DEAR YOU MUST ASSUME YOUR RIGHTFUL RANK AS A PRINCESS OF OZ AND BEING MY CHOSEN COMPANION YOU MUST DRESS IN A WAY BEFITTING THE DIGNITY OF YOUR POSITION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-39 DOROTHY AGREED TO THIS ALTHOUGH SHE KNEW THAT NEITHER GOWNS NOR JEWELS COULD MAKE HER ANYTHING ELSE THAN THE SIMPLE UNAFFECTED LITTLE GIRL SHE HAD ALWAYS BEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-40 AS SOON AS THEY HAD BREAKFASTED THE GIRLS EATING TOGETHER IN OZMA'S PRETTY BOUDOIR THE RULER OF OZ SAID, NOW DEAR FRIEND WE WILL USE THE MAGIC BELT TO TRANSPORT YOUR UNCLE AND AUNT FROM KANSAS TO THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-41 BUT I THINK IT WOULD BE FITTING IN RECEIVING SUCH DISTINGUISHED GUESTS FOR US TO SIT IN MY THRONE ROOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-42 OH THEY'RE NOT VERY STINGUISHED OZMA SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-43 THEY'RE JUST PLAIN PEOPLE LIKE ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-44 BEING YOUR FRIENDS AND RELATIVES PRINCESS DOROTHY THEY ARE CERTAINLY DISTINGUISHED REPLIED THE RULER WITH A SMILE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-45 THEY THEY WON'T HARDLY KNOW WHAT TO MAKE OF ALL YOUR SPLENDID FURNITURE AND THINGS PROTESTED DOROTHY GRAVELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-46 IT MAY SCARE EM TO SEE YOUR GRAND THRONE ROOM AN P'RAPS WE'D BETTER GO INTO THE BACK YARD OZMA WHERE THE CABBAGES GROW AN THE CHICKENS ARE PLAYING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-47 THEN IT WOULD SEEM MORE NATURAL TO UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM. NO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-48 THEY SHALL FIRST SEE ME IN MY THRONE ROOM REPLIED OZMA DECIDEDLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-49 AND WHEN SHE SPOKE IN THAT TONE DOROTHY KNEW IT WAS NOT WISE TO OPPOSE HER FOR OZMA WAS ACCUSTOMED TO HAVING HER OWN WAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-50 SO TOGETHER THEY WENT TO THE THRONE ROOM AN IMMENSE DOMED CHAMBER IN THE CENTER OF THE PALACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-51 HERE STOOD THE ROYAL THRONE MADE OF SOLID GOLD AND ENCRUSTED WITH ENOUGH PRECIOUS STONES TO STOCK A DOZEN JEWELRY STORES IN OUR COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-52 OZMA WHO WAS WEARING THE MAGIC BELT SEATED HERSELF IN THE THRONE AND DOROTHY SAT AT HER FEET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-53 IN THE ROOM WERE ASSEMBLED MANY LADIES AND GENTLEMEN OF THE COURT CLOTHED IN RICH APPAREL AND WEARING FINE JEWELRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-54 TWO IMMENSE ANIMALS SQUATTED ONE ON EACH SIDE OF THE THRONE THE COWARDLY LION AND THE HUNGRY TIGER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-55 IN A BALCONY HIGH UP IN THE DOME AN ORCHESTRA PLAYED SWEET MUSIC AND BENEATH THE DOME TWO ELECTRIC FOUNTAINS SENT SPRAYS OF COLORED PERFUMED WATER SHOOTING UP NEARLY AS HIGH AS THE ARCHED CEILING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-56 ARE YOU READY DOROTHY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-57 ASKED THE RULER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-58 I AM REPLIED DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-59 BUT I DON'T KNOW WHETHER AUNT EM AND UNCLE HENRY ARE READY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-60 THAT WON'T MATTER DECLARED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-61 THE OLD LIFE CAN HAVE VERY LITTLE TO INTEREST THEM AND THE SOONER THEY BEGIN THE NEW LIFE HERE THE HAPPIER THEY WILL BE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-62 HERE THEY COME MY DEAR!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-63 AS SHE SPOKE THERE BEFORE THE THRONE APPEARED UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM WHO FOR A MOMENT STOOD MOTIONLESS GLARING WITH WHITE AND STARTLED FACES AT THE SCENE THAT CONFRONTED THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-64 IF THE LADIES AND GENTLEMEN PRESENT HAD NOT BEEN SO POLITE I AM SURE THEY WOULD HAVE LAUGHED AT THE TWO STRANGERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-65 AUNT EM HAD HER CALICO DRESS SKIRT TUCKED UP AND SHE WORE A FADED BLUE CHECKED APRON.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-67 IN ONE HAND SHE HELD A DISH TOWEL AND IN THE OTHER A CRACKED EARTHENWARE PLATE WHICH SHE HAD BEEN ENGAGED IN WIPING WHEN SO SUDDENLY TRANSPORTED TO THE LAND OF OZ. UNCLE HENRY WHEN THE SUMMONS CAME HAD BEEN OUT IN THE BARN DOIN CHORES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-68 HE WORE A RAGGED AND MUCH SOILED STRAW HAT A CHECKED SHIRT WITHOUT ANY COLLAR AND BLUE OVERALLS TUCKED INTO THE TOPS OF HIS OLD COWHIDE BOOTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-69 BY GUM!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-70 GASPED UNCLE HENRY LOOKING AROUND AS IF BEWILDERED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-71 WELL I SWAN!

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-73 THEN HER EYES FELL UPON DOROTHY AND SHE SAID, D D D DON'T THAT LOOK LIKE OUR LITTLE GIRL OUR DOROTHY HENRY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-74 HI THERE LOOK OUT EM!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-75 EXCLAIMED THE OLD MAN AS AUNT EM ADVANCED A STEP,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-76 TAKE CARE O THE WILD BEASTSES OR YOU'RE A GONER!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-77 BUT NOW DOROTHY SPRANG FORWARD AND EMBRACED AND KISSED HER AUNT AND UNCLE AFFECTIONATELY AFTERWARD TAKING THEIR HANDS IN HER OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-78 DON'T BE AFRAID SHE SAID TO THEM.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-83 AND THIS IS AUNT EM. THEY WANT TO THANK YOU FOR BRINGING THEM HERE FROM KANSAS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-86 BUT THE RULER OF OZ ROSE AND CAME FROM HER THRONE TO GREET HER NEWLY ARRIVED GUESTS AND SHE SMILED AS SWEETLY UPON THEM AS IF THEY HAD BEEN A KING AND QUEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-87 YOU ARE VERY WELCOME HERE WHERE I HAVE BROUGHT YOU FOR PRINCESS DOROTHY'S SAKE SHE SAID GRACIOUSLY AND I HOPE YOU WILL BE QUITE HAPPY IN YOUR NEW HOME.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-89 IT WILL PLEASE ME TO HAVE YOU SHOW THEM EVERY KINDNESS AND HONOR IN YOUR POWER AND TO JOIN ME IN MAKING THEM HAPPY AND CONTENTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-90 HEARING THIS ALL THOSE ASSEMBLED BOWED LOW AND RESPECTFULLY TO THE OLD FARMER AND HIS WIFE WHO BOBBED THEIR OWN HEADS IN RETURN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-91 AND NOW SAID OZMA TO THEM DOROTHY WILL SHOW YOU THE ROOMS PREPARED FOR YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-92 I HOPE YOU WILL LIKE THEM AND SHALL EXPECT YOU TO JOIN ME AT LUNCHEON.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-95 AND IS IT ALL REAL?

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-99 WHY DIDN'T YOU TELL US WHAT YOU WERE GOIN TO DO?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-100 INQUIRED UNCLE HENRY REPROACHFULLY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-116 YOU'RE IN THE FAIRYLAND OF OZ NOW,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-05-117 AN WHAT'S MORE YOU BELONG TO IT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-01 CHAPTER SIX.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-02 HOW GUPH VISITED THE WHIMSIES THE NEW GENERAL OF THE NOME KING'S ARMY KNEW PERFECTLY WELL THAT TO FAIL IN HIS PLANS MEANT DEATH FOR HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-03 YET HE WAS NOT AT ALL ANXIOUS OR WORRIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-04 HE HATED EVERY ONE WHO WAS GOOD AND LONGED TO MAKE ALL WHO WERE HAPPY UNHAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-05 THEREFORE HE HAD ACCEPTED THIS DANGEROUS POSITION AS GENERAL QUITE WILLINGLY FEELING SURE IN HIS EVIL MIND THAT HE WOULD BE ABLE TO DO A LOT OF MISCHIEF AND FINALLY CONQUER THE LAND OF OZ. YET GUPH DETERMINED TO BE CAREFUL AND TO LAY HIS PLANS WELL SO AS NOT TO FAIL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-06 HE ARGUED THAT ONLY CARELESS PEOPLE FAIL IN WHAT THEY ATTEMPT TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-07 THE MOUNTAINS UNDERNEATH WHICH THE NOME KING'S EXTENSIVE CAVERNS WERE LOCATED LAY GROUPED JUST NORTH OF THE LAND OF EV WHICH LAY DIRECTLY ACROSS THE DEADLY DESERT TO THE EAST OF THE LAND OF OZ. AS THE MOUNTAINS WERE ALSO ON THE EDGE OF THE DESERT THE NOME KING FOUND THAT HE HAD ONLY TO TUNNEL UNDERNEATH THE DESERT TO REACH OZMA'S DOMINIONS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-08 HE DID NOT WISH HIS ARMIES TO APPEAR ABOVE GROUND IN THE COUNTRY OF THE WINKIES WHICH WAS THE PART OF THE LAND OF OZ NEAREST TO KING ROQUAT'S OWN COUNTRY AS THEN THE PEOPLE WOULD GIVE THE ALARM AND ENABLE OZMA TO FORTIFY THE EMERALD CITY AND ASSEMBLE AN ARMY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-09 HE WANTED TO TAKE ALL THE OZ PEOPLE BY SURPRISE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-10 SO HE DECIDED TO RUN THE TUNNEL CLEAR THROUGH TO THE EMERALD CITY WHERE HE AND HIS HOSTS COULD BREAK THROUGH THE GROUND WITHOUT WARNING AND CONQUER THE PEOPLE BEFORE THEY HAD TIME TO DEFEND THEMSELVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-11 ROQUAT THE RED BEGAN WORK AT ONCE UPON HIS TUNNEL SETTING A THOUSAND MINERS AT THE TASK AND BUILDING IT HIGH AND BROAD ENOUGH FOR HIS ARMIES TO MARCH THROUGH IT WITH EASE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-12 THE NOMES WERE USED TO MAKING TUNNELS AS ALL THE KINGDOM IN WHICH THEY LIVED WAS UNDER GROUND,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-13 SO THEY MADE RAPID PROGRESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-14 WHILE THIS WORK WAS GOING ON GENERAL GUPH STARTED OUT ALONE TO VISIT THE CHIEF OF THE WHIMSIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-15 THESE WHIMSIES WERE CURIOUS PEOPLE WHO LIVED IN A RETIRED COUNTRY OF THEIR OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-16 THEY HAD LARGE STRONG BODIES BUT HEADS SO SMALL THAT THEY WERE NO BIGGER THAN DOOR KNOBS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-17 OF COURSE SUCH TINY HEADS COULD NOT CONTAIN ANY GREAT AMOUNT OF BRAINS AND THE WHIMSIES WERE SO ASHAMED OF THEIR PERSONAL APPEARANCE AND LACK OF COMMONSENSE THAT THEY WORE BIG HEADS MADE OF PASTEBOARD WHICH THEY FASTENED OVER THEIR OWN LITTLE HEADS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-18 ON THESE PASTEBOARD HEADS THEY SEWED SHEEP'S WOOL FOR HAIR AND THE WOOL WAS COLORED MANY TINTS PINK GREEN AND LAVENDER BEING THE FAVORITE COLORS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-19 THE FACES OF THESE FALSE HEADS WERE PAINTED IN MANY RIDICULOUS WAYS ACCORDING TO THE WHIMS OF THE OWNERS AND THESE BIG BURLY CREATURES LOOKED SO WHIMSICAL AND ABSURD IN THEIR QUEER MASKS THAT THEY WERE CALLED WHIMSIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-20 THEY FOOLISHLY IMAGINED THAT NO ONE WOULD SUSPECT THE LITTLE HEADS THAT WERE INSIDE THE IMITATION ONES NOT KNOWING THAT IT IS FOLLY TO TRY TO APPEAR OTHERWISE THAN AS NATURE HAS MADE US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-21 THE CHIEF OF THE WHIMSIES HAD AS LITTLE WISDOM AS THE OTHERS AND HAD BEEN CHOSEN CHIEF MERELY BECAUSE NONE AMONG THEM WAS ANY WISER OR MORE CAPABLE OF RULING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-22 THE WHIMSIES WERE EVIL SPIRITS AND COULD NOT BE KILLED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-23 THEY WERE HATED AND FEARED BY EVERY ONE AND WERE KNOWN AS TERRIBLE FIGHTERS BECAUSE THEY WERE SO STRONG AND MUSCULAR AND HAD NOT SENSE ENOUGH TO KNOW WHEN THEY WERE DEFEATED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-24 GENERAL GUPH THOUGHT THE WHIMSIES WOULD BE A GREAT HELP TO THE NOMES IN THE CONQUEST OF OZ FOR UNDER HIS LEADERSHIP THEY COULD BE INDUCED TO FIGHT AS LONG SO THEY COULD STAND UP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-25 SO HE TRAVELED TO THEIR COUNTRY AND ASKED TO SEE THE CHIEF WHO LIVED IN A HOUSE THAT HAD A PICTURE OF HIS GROTESQUE FALSE HEAD PAINTED OVER THE DOORWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-26 THE CHIEF'S FALSE HEAD HAD BLUE HAIR A TURNED UP NOSE AND A MOUTH THAT STRETCHED HALF ACROSS THE FACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-27 BIG GREEN EYES HAD BEEN PAINTED UPON IT BUT IN THE CENTER OF THE CHIN WERE TWO SMALL HOLES MADE IN THE PASTEBOARD SO THAT THE CHIEF COULD SEE THROUGH THEM WITH HIS OWN TINY EYES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-28 FOR WHEN THE BIG HEAD WAS FASTENED UPON HIS SHOULDERS THE EYES IN HIS OWN NATURAL HEAD WERE ON A LEVEL WITH THE FALSE CHIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-29 SAID GENERAL GUPH TO THE CHIEF OF THE WHIMSIES, WE NOMES ARE GOING TO CONQUER THE LAND OF OZ AND CAPTURE OUR KING'S MAGIC BELT WHICH THE OZ PEOPLE STOLE FROM HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-30 THEN WE ARE GOING TO PLUNDER AND DESTROY THE WHOLE COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-31 AND WE WANT THE WHIMSIES TO HELP US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-32 WILL THERE BE ANY FIGHTING?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-33 ASKED THE CHIEF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-34 PLENTY REPLIED GUPH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-35 THAT MUST HAVE PLEASED THE CHIEF FOR HE GOT UP AND DANCED AROUND THE ROOM THREE TIMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-36 THEN HE SEATED HIMSELF AGAIN ADJUSTED HIS FALSE HEAD AND SAID, WE HAVE NO QUARREL WITH OZMA OF OZ. BUT YOU WHIMSIES LOVE TO FIGHT AND HERE IS A SPLENDID CHANCE TO DO SO URGED GUPH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-37 WAIT TILL I SING A SONG SAID THE CHIEF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-38 THEN HE LAY BACK IN HIS CHAIR AND SANG A FOOLISH SONG THAT DID NOT SEEM TO THE GENERAL TO MEAN ANYTHING ALTHOUGH HE LISTENED CAREFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-39 WHEN HE HAD FINISHED THE CHIEF WHIMSIE LOOKED AT HIM THROUGH THE HOLES IN HIS CHIN AND ASKED, WHAT REWARD WILL YOU GIVE US IF WE HELP YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-40 THE GENERAL WAS PREPARED FOR THIS QUESTION FOR HE HAD BEEN THINKING THE MATTER OVER ON HIS JOURNEY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-06-41 PEOPLE OFTEN DO A GOOD DEED WITHOUT HOPE OF REWARD BUT FOR AN EVIL DEED THEY ALWAYS DEMAND PAYMENT.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-01 CHAPTER EIGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-02 HOW THE GRAND GALLIPOOT JOINED THE NOMES AFTER LEAVING THE WHIMSIES GUPH CONTINUED ON HIS JOURNEY AND PENETRATED FAR INTO THE NORTHWEST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-03 HE WANTED TO GET TO THE COUNTRY OF THE GROWLEYWOGS AND IN ORDER TO DO THAT HE MUST CROSS THE RIPPLE LAND WHICH WAS A HARD THING TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-04 FOR THE RIPPLE LAND WAS A SUCCESSION OF HILLS AND VALLEYS ALL VERY STEEP AND ROCKY AND THEY CHANGED PLACES CONSTANTLY BY RIPPLING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-05 WHILE GUPH WAS CLIMBING A HILL IT SANK DOWN UNDER HIM AND BECAME A VALLEY AND WHILE HE WAS DESCENDING INTO A VALLEY IT ROSE UP AND CARRIED HIM TO THE TOP OF A HILL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-06 THIS WAS VERY PERPLEXING TO THE TRAVELER AND A STRANGER MIGHT HAVE THOUGHT HE COULD NEVER CROSS THE RIPPLE LAND AT ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-07 BUT GUPH KNEW THAT IF HE KEPT STEADILY ON HE WOULD GET TO THE END AT LAST,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-08 SO HE PAID NO ATTENTION TO THE CHANGING HILLS AND VALLEYS AND PLODDED ALONG AS CALMLY AS IF WALKING UPON THE LEVEL GROUND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-09 THE RESULT OF THIS WISE PERSISTENCE WAS THAT THE GENERAL FINALLY REACHED FIRMER SOIL AND AFTER PENETRATING A DENSE FOREST CAME TO THE DOMINION OF THE GROWLEYWOGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-10 NO SOONER HAD HE CROSSED THE BORDER OF THIS DOMAIN WHEN TWO GUARDS SEIZED HIM AND CARRIED HIM BEFORE THE GRAND GALLIPOOT OF THE GROWLEYWOGS WHO SCOWLED UPON HIM FEROCIOUSLY AND ASKED HIM WHY HE DARED INTRUDE UPON HIS TERRITORY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-11 I'M THE LORD HIGH GENERAL OF THE INVINCIBLE ARMY OF THE NOMES AND MY NAME IS GUPH WAS THE REPLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-12 ALL THE WORLD TREMBLES WHEN THAT NAME IS MENTIONED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-13 THE GROWLEYWOGS GAVE A SHOUT OF JEERING LAUGHTER AT THIS AND ONE OF THEM CAUGHT THE NOME IN HIS STRONG ARMS AND TOSSED HIM HIGH INTO THE AIR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-14 GUPH WAS CONSIDERABLY SHAKEN WHEN HE FELL UPON THE HARD GROUND BUT HE APPEARED TO TAKE NO NOTICE OF THE IMPERTINENCE AND COMPOSED HIMSELF TO SPEAK AGAIN TO THE GRAND GALLIPOOT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-15 MY MASTER KING ROQUAT THE RED HAS SENT ME HERE TO CONFER WITH YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-16 HE WISHES YOUR ASSISTANCE TO CONQUER THE LAND OF OZ. HERE THE GENERAL PAUSED AND THE GRAND GALLIPOOT SCOWLED UPON HIM MORE TERRIBLY THAN EVER AND SAID, GO ON!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-17 THE VOICE OF THE GRAND GALLIPOOT WAS PARTLY A ROAR AND PARTLY A GROWL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-18 HE MUMBLED HIS WORDS BADLY AND GUPH HAD TO LISTEN CAREFULLY IN ORDER TO UNDERSTAND HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-19 THESE GROWLEYWOGS WERE CERTAINLY REMARKABLE CREATURES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-20 THEY WERE OF GIGANTIC SIZE YET WERE ALL BONE AND SKIN AND MUSCLE THERE BEING NO MEAT OR FAT UPON THEIR BODIES AT ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-21 THEIR POWERFUL MUSCLES LAY JUST UNDERNEATH THEIR SKINS LIKE BUNCHES OF TOUGH ROPE AND THE WEAKEST GROWLEYWOG WAS SO STRONG THAT HE COULD PICK UP AN ELEPHANT AND TOSS IT SEVEN MILES AWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-22 IT SEEMS UNFORTUNATE THAT STRONG PEOPLE ARE USUALLY SO DISAGREEABLE AND OVERBEARING THAT NO ONE CARES FOR THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-23 IN FACT TO BE DIFFERENT FROM YOUR FELLOW CREATURES IS ALWAYS A MISFORTUNE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-24 THE GROWLEYWOGS KNEW THAT THEY WERE DISLIKED AND AVOIDED BY EVERY ONE SO THEY HAD BECOME SURLY AND UNSOCIABLE EVEN AMONG THEMSELVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-25 GUPH KNEW THAT THEY HATED ALL PEOPLE INCLUDING THE NOMES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-26 BUT HE HOPED TO WIN THEM OVER NEVERTHELESS AND KNEW THAT IF HE SUCCEEDED THEY WOULD AFFORD HIM VERY POWERFUL ASSISTANCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-27 THE LAND OF OZ IS RULED BY A NAMBY PAMBY GIRL WHO IS DISGUSTINGLY KIND AND GOOD HE CONTINUED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-28 HER PEOPLE ARE ALL HAPPY AND CONTENTED AND HAVE NO CARE OR WORRIES WHATEVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-29 GO ON!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-30 GROWLED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-31 ONCE THE NOME KING ENSLAVED THE ROYAL FAMILY OF EV ANOTHER GOODY GOODY LOT THAT WE DETEST SAID THE GENERAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-32 BUT OZMA INTERFERED ALTHOUGH IT WAS NONE OF HER BUSINESS AND MARCHED HER ARMY AGAINST US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-33 WITH HER WAS A KANSAS GIRL NAMED DOROTHY AND A YELLOW HEN AND THEY MARCHED DIRECTLY INTO THE NOME KING'S CAVERN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-34 THERE THEY LIBERATED OUR SLAVES FROM EV AND STOLE KING ROQUAT'S MAGIC BELT WHICH THEY CARRIED AWAY WITH THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-35 SO NOW OUR KING IS MAKING A TUNNEL UNDER THE DEADLY DESERT SO WE CAN MARCH THROUGH IT TO THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-36 WHEN WE GET THERE WE MEAN TO CONQUER AND DESTROY ALL THE LAND AND RECAPTURE THE MAGIC BELT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-37 AGAIN HE PAUSED AND AGAIN THE GRAND GALLIPOOT GROWLED, GO ON!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-38 GUPH TRIED TO THINK WHAT TO SAY NEXT AND A HAPPY THOUGHT SOON OCCURRED TO HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-39 WE WANT YOU TO HELP US IN THIS CONQUEST HE ANNOUNCED FOR WE NEED THE MIGHTY AID OF THE GROWLEYWOGS IN ORDER TO MAKE SURE THAT WE SHALL NOT BE DEFEATED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-40 YOU ARE THE STRONGEST PEOPLE IN ALL THE WORLD AND YOU HATE GOOD AND HAPPY CREATURES AS MUCH AS WE NOMES DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-41 I AM SURE IT WILL BE A REAL PLEASURE TO YOU TO TEAR DOWN THE BEAUTIFUL EMERALD CITY AND IN RETURN FOR YOUR VALUABLE ASSISTANCE WE WILL ALLOW YOU TO BRING BACK TO YOUR COUNTRY TEN THOUSAND PEOPLE OF OZ TO BE YOUR SLAVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-42 TWENTY THOUSAND!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-43 GROWLED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-44 ALL RIGHT WE PROMISE YOU TWENTY THOUSAND AGREED THE GENERAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-45 THE GALLIPOOT MADE A SIGNAL AND AT ONCE HIS ATTENDANTS PICKED UP GENERAL GUPH AND CARRIED HIM AWAY TO A PRISON WHERE THE JAILER AMUSED HIMSELF BY STICKING PINS IN THE ROUND FAT BODY OF THE OLD NOME TO SEE HIM JUMP AND HEAR HIM YELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-46 BUT WHILE THIS WAS GOING ON THE GRAND GALLIPOOT WAS TALKING WITH HIS COUNSELORS WHO WERE THE MOST IMPORTANT OFFICIALS OF THE GROWLEYWOGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-47 WHEN HE HAD STATED TO THEM THE PROPOSITION OF THE NOME KING HE SAID, MY ADVICE IS TO OFFER TO HELP THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-48 THEN WHEN WE HAVE CONQUERED THE LAND OF OZ WE WILL TAKE NOT ONLY OUR TWENTY THOUSAND PRISONERS BUT ALL THE GOLD AND JEWELS WE WANT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-49 LET US TAKE THE MAGIC BELT TOO SUGGESTED ONE COUNSELOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-50 AND ROB THE NOME KING AND MAKE HIM OUR SLAVE SAID ANOTHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-51 THAT IS A GOOD IDEA DECLARED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-52 I'D LIKE KING ROQUAT FOR MY OWN SLAVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-53 HE COULD BLACK MY BOOTS AND BRING ME MY PORRIDGE EVERY MORNING WHILE I AM IN BED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-54 THERE IS A FAMOUS SCARECROW IN OZ. I'LL TAKE HIM FOR MY SLAVE SAID A COUNSELOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-55 I'LL TAKE TIKTOK THE MACHINE MAN SAID ANOTHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-56 GIVE ME THE TIN WOODMAN SAID A THIRD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-57 THEY WENT ON FOR SOME TIME DIVIDING UP THE PEOPLE AND THE TREASURE OF OZ IN ADVANCE OF THE CONQUEST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-58 FOR THEY HAD NO DOUBT AT ALL THAT THEY WOULD BE ABLE TO DESTROY OZMA'S DOMAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-59 WERE THEY NOT THE STRONGEST PEOPLE IN ALL THE WORLD?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-60 THE DEADLY DESERT HAS KEPT US OUT OF OZ BEFORE REMARKED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT BUT NOW THAT THE NOME KING IS BUILDING A TUNNEL WE SHALL GET INTO THE EMERALD CITY VERY EASILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-61 SO LET US SEND THE LITTLE FAT GENERAL BACK TO HIS KING WITH OUR PROMISE TO ASSIST HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-62 WE WILL NOT SAY THAT WE INTEND TO CONQUER THE NOMES AFTER WE HAVE CONQUERED OZ BUT WE WILL DO SO JUST THE SAME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-63 THIS PLAN BEING AGREED UPON THEY ALL WENT HOME TO DINNER LEAVING GENERAL GUPH STILL IN PRISON.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-64 THE NOME HAD NO IDEA THAT HE HAD SUCCEEDED IN HIS MISSION FOR FINDING HIMSELF IN PRISON HE FEARED THE GROWLEYWOGS INTENDED TO PUT HIM TO DEATH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-65 BY THIS TIME THE JAILER HAD TIRED OF STICKING PINS IN THE GENERAL AND WAS AMUSING HIMSELF BY CAREFULLY PULLING THE NOME'S WHISKERS OUT BY THE ROOTS ONE AT A TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-66 THIS ENJOYMENT WAS INTERRUPTED BY THE GRAND GALLIPOOT SENDING FOR THE PRISONER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-67 WAIT A FEW HOURS BEGGED THE JAILER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-68 I HAVEN'T PULLED OUT A QUARTER OF HIS WHISKERS YET.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-70 PERHAPS YOU'RE RIGHT SIGHED THE JAILER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-71 TAKE THE PRISONER AWAY IF YOU WILL BUT I ADVISE YOU TO KICK HIM AT EVERY STEP HE TAKES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-72 IT WILL BE GOOD FUN FOR HE IS AS SOFT AS A RIPE PEACH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-73 SO GUPH WAS LED AWAY TO THE ROYAL CASTLE WHERE THE GRAND GALLIPOOT TOLD HIM THAT THE GROWLEYWOGS HAD DECIDED TO ASSIST THE NOMES IN CONQUERING THE LAND OF OZ. WHENEVER YOU ARE READY HE ADDED SEND ME WORD AND I WILL MARCH WITH EIGHTEEN THOUSAND OF MY MOST POWERFUL WARRIORS TO YOUR AID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-74 GUPH WAS SO DELIGHTED THAT HE FORGOT ALL THE SMARTING CAUSED BY THE PINS AND THE PULLING OF WHISKERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-75 HE DID NOT EVEN COMPLAIN OF THE TREATMENT HE HAD RECEIVED BUT THANKED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT AND HURRIED AWAY UPON HIS JOURNEY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-76 HE HAD NOW SECURED THE ASSISTANCE OF THE WHIMSIES AND THE GROWLEYWOGS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-77 BUT HIS SUCCESS MADE HIM LONG FOR STILL MORE ALLIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-78 HIS OWN LIFE DEPENDED UPON HIS CONQUERING OZ AND HE SAID TO HIMSELF, I'LL TAKE NO CHANCES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-79 I'LL BE CERTAIN OF SUCCESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-80 THEN WHEN OZ IS DESTROYED PERHAPS I SHALL BE A GREATER MAN THAN OLD ROQUAT AND I CAN THROW HIM AWAY AND BE KING OF THE NOMES MYSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-81 WHY NOT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-82 THE WHIMSIES ARE STRONGER THAN THE NOMES AND THEY ALSO ARE MY FRIENDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-08-83 THERE ARE SOME PEOPLE STILL STRONGER THAN THE GROWLEYWOGS AND IF I CAN BUT INDUCE THEM TO AID ME I SHALL HAVE NOTHING MORE TO FEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-01 CHAPTER NINE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-02 HOW THE WOGGLEBUG TAUGHT ATHLETICS IT DID NOT TAKE DOROTHY LONG TO ESTABLISH HERSELF IN HER NEW HOME FOR SHE KNEW THE PEOPLE AND THE MANNERS AND CUSTOMS OF THE EMERALD CITY JUST AS WELL AS SHE KNEW THE OLD KANSAS FARM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-03 BUT UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM HAD SOME TROUBLE IN GETTING USED TO THE FINERY AND POMP AND CEREMONY OF OZMA'S PALACE AND FELT UNEASY BECAUSE THEY WERE OBLIGED TO BE DRESSED UP ALL THE TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-04 YET EVERY ONE WAS VERY COURTEOUS AND KIND TO THEM AND ENDEAVORED TO MAKE THEM HAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-05 OZMA ESPECIALLY MADE MUCH OF DOROTHY'S RELATIVES FOR HER LITTLE FRIEND'S SAKE AND SHE WELL KNEW THAT THE AWKWARDNESS AND STRANGENESS OF THEIR NEW MODE OF LIFE WOULD ALL WEAR OFF IN TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-06 THE OLD PEOPLE WERE CHIEFLY TROUBLED BY THE FACT THAT THERE WAS NO WORK FOR THEM TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-07 EV'RY DAY IS LIKE SUNDAY NOW DECLARED AUNT EM SOLEMNLY AND I CAN'T SAY I LIKE IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-08 IF THEY'D ONLY LET ME DO UP THE DISHES AFTER MEALS OR EVEN SWEEP AN DUST MY OWN ROOMS I'D BE A DEAL HAPPIER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-09 HENRY DON'T KNOW WHAT TO DO WITH HIMSELF EITHER AND ONCE WHEN HE STOLE OUT AN FED THE CHICKENS BILLINA SCOLDED HIM FOR LETTING EM EAT BETWEEN MEALS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-10 I NEVER KNEW BEFORE WHAT A HARDSHIP IT IS TO BE RICH AND HAVE EVERYTHING YOU WANT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-11 THESE COMPLAINTS BEGAN TO WORRY DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-12 SO SHE HAD A LONG TALK WITH OZMA UPON THE SUBJECT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-13 I SEE I MUST FIND THEM SOMETHING TO DO SAID THE GIRLISH RULER OF OZ SERIOUSLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-14 I HAVE BEEN WATCHING YOUR UNCLE AND AUNT AND I BELIEVE THEY WILL BE MORE CONTENTED IF OCCUPIED WITH SOME LIGHT TASKS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-15 WHILE I AM CONSIDERING THIS MATTER DOROTHY YOU MIGHT MAKE A TRIP WITH THEM THROUGH THE LAND OF OZ VISITING SOME OF THE ODD CORNERS AND INTRODUCING YOUR RELATIVES TO SOME OF OUR CURIOUS PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-16 OH THAT WOULD BE FINE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-17 EXCLAIMED DOROTHY EAGERLY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-20 I WILL MARK OUT A PLAN OF THE TRIP FOR YOU AND HAVE EVERYTHING IN READINESS FOR YOU TO START TO MORROW MORNING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-21 TAKE YOUR TIME DEAR AND BE GONE AS LONG AS YOU WISH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-22 BY THE TIME YOU RETURN I SHALL HAVE FOUND SOME OCCUPATION FOR UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM THAT WILL KEEP THEM FROM BEING RESTLESS AND DISSATISFIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-23 DOROTHY THANKED HER GOOD FRIEND AND KISSED THE LOVELY RULER GRATEFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-24 THEN SHE RAN TO TELL THE JOYFUL NEWS TO HER UNCLE AND AUNT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-25 NEXT MORNING AFTER BREAKFAST EVERYTHING WAS FOUND READY FOR THEIR DEPARTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-26 THE ESCORT INCLUDED OMBY AMBY THE CAPTAIN GENERAL OF OZMA'S ARMY WHICH CONSISTED MERELY OF TWENTY SEVEN OFFICERS BESIDES THE CAPTAIN GENERAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-27 ONCE OMBY AMBY HAD BEEN A PRIVATE SOLDIER THE ONLY PRIVATE IN THE ARMY BUT AS THERE WAS NEVER ANY FIGHTING TO DO OZMA SAW NO NEED OF A PRIVATE SO SHE MADE OMBY AMBY THE HIGHEST OFFICER OF THEM ALL.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-33 THE SAWHORSE WORE WOODEN SHOES TO KEEP HIS WOODEN LEGS FROM WEARING AWAY AND HE WAS STRONG AND SWIFT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-09-34 AS THIS CURIOUS CREATURE WAS OZMA'S OWN FAVORITE STEED AND VERY POPULAR WITH ALL THE PEOPLE OF THE EMERALD CITY DOROTHY KNEW THAT SHE HAD BEEN HIGHLY FAVORED BY BEING PERMITTED TO USE THE SAWHORSE ON HER JOURNEY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-111 HERE WE ARE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-112 CALLED THE CAPTAIN STOPPING BEFORE A COTTAGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-113 THIS HOUSE WAS MADE OF WOOD AND WAS REMARKABLY PRETTY IN DESIGN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-114 IN THE EMERALD CITY IT WOULD HAVE BEEN CONSIDERED A TINY DWELLING INDEED,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-115 BUT IN THE MIDST OF THIS PAPER VILLAGE IT SEEMED IMMENSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-116 REAL FLOWERS WERE IN THE GARDEN AND REAL TREES GREW BESIDE IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-117 UPON THE FRONT DOOR WAS A SIGN READING, MISS CUTTENCLIP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-118 JUST AS THEY REACHED THE PORCH THE FRONT DOOR OPENED AND A LITTLE GIRL STOOD BEFORE THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-119 SHE APPEARED TO BE ABOUT THE SAME AGE AS DOROTHY AND SMILING UPON HER VISITORS SHE SAID SWEETLY, YOU ARE WELCOME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-120 ALL THE PARTY SEEMED RELIEVED TO FIND THAT HERE WAS A REAL GIRL OF FLESH AND BLOOD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-121 SHE WAS VERY DAINTY AND PRETTY AS SHE STOOD THERE WELCOMING THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-122 HER HAIR WAS A GOLDEN BLONDE AND HER EYES TURQUOISE BLUE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-123 SHE HAD ROSY CHEEKS AND LOVELY WHITE TEETH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-124 OVER HER SIMPLE WHITE LAWN DRESS SHE WORE AN APRON WITH PINK AND WHITE CHECKS AND IN ONE HAND SHE HELD A PAIR OF SCISSORS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-125 MAY WE SEE MISS CUTTENCLIP PLEASE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-126 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-127 I AM MISS CUTTENCLIP WAS THE REPLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-128 WON'T YOU COME IN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-129 SHE HELD THE DOOR OPEN WHILE THEY ALL ENTERED A PRETTY SITTING ROOM THAT WAS LITTERED WITH ALL SORTS OF PAPER SOME STIFF SOME THIN AND SOME TISSUE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-130 THE SHEETS AND SCRAPS WERE OF ALL COLORS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-131 UPON A TABLE WERE PAINTS AND BRUSHES WHILE SEVERAL PAIR OF SCISSORS OF DIFFERENT SIZES WERE LYING ABOUT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-132 SIT DOWN PLEASE SAID MISS CUTTENCLIP CLEARING THE PAPER SCRAPS OFF SOME OF THE CHAIRS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-133 IT IS SO LONG SINCE I HAVE HAD ANY VISITORS THAT I AM NOT PROPERLY PREPARED TO RECEIVE THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-134 BUT I'M SURE YOU WILL PARDON MY UNTIDY ROOM FOR THIS IS MY WORKSHOP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-135 DO YOU MAKE ALL THE PAPER DOLLS?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-136 INQUIRED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-137 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-138 I CUT THEM OUT WITH MY SCISSORS AND PAINT THE FACES AND SOME OF THE COSTUMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-139 IT IS VERY PLEASANT WORK AND I AM HAPPY MAKING MY PAPER VILLAGE GROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-140 BUT HOW DO THE PAPER DOLLS HAPPEN TO BE ALIVE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-141 ASKED AUNT EM. THE FIRST DOLLS I MADE WERE NOT ALIVE SAID MISS CUTTENCLIP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-142 I USED TO LIVE NEAR THE CASTLE OF A GREAT SORCERESS NAMED GLINDA THE GOOD AND SHE SAW MY DOLLS AND SAID THEY WERE VERY PRETTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-143 I TOLD HER I THOUGHT I WOULD LIKE THEM BETTER IF THEY WERE ALIVE AND THE NEXT DAY THE SORCERESS BROUGHT ME A LOT OF MAGIC PAPER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-144 IS LIVE PAPER SHE SAID AND ALL THE DOLLS YOU CUT OUT OF IT WILL BE ALIVE AND ABLE TO THINK AND TO TALK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-145 WHEN YOU HAVE USED IT ALL UP COME TO ME AND I WILL GIVE YOU MORE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-146 OF COURSE I WAS DELIGHTED WITH THIS PRESENT CONTINUED MISS CUTTENCLIP AND AT ONCE SET TO WORK AND MADE SEVERAL PAPER DOLLS WHICH AS SOON AS THEY WERE CUT OUT BEGAN TO WALK AROUND AND TALK TO ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-147 BUT THEY WERE SO THIN THAT I FOUND THAT ANY BREEZE WOULD BLOW THEM OVER AND SCATTER THEM DREADFULLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-148 SO GLINDA FOUND THIS LONELY PLACE FOR ME WHERE FEW PEOPLE EVER COME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-149 SHE BUILT THE WALL TO KEEP ANY WIND FROM BLOWING AWAY MY PEOPLE AND TOLD ME I COULD BUILD A PAPER VILLAGE HERE AND BE ITS QUEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-150 THAT IS WHY I CAME HERE AND SETTLED DOWN TO WORK AND STARTED THE VILLAGE YOU NOW SEE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-151 IT WAS MANY YEARS AGO THAT I BUILT THE FIRST HOUSES AND I'VE KEPT PRETTY BUSY AND MADE MY VILLAGE GROW FINELY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-152 AND I NEED NOT TELL YOU THAT I AM VERY HAPPY IN MY WORK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-153 MANY YEARS AGO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-154 EXCLAIMED AUNT EM. WHY HOW OLD ARE YOU CHILD?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-155 I NEVER KEEP TRACK OF THE YEARS SAID MISS CUTTENCLIP LAUGHING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-156 YOU SEE I DON'T GROW UP AT ALL BUT STAY JUST THE SAME AS I WAS WHEN FIRST I CAME HERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-157 PERHAPS I'M OLDER EVEN THAN YOU ARE MADAM,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-158 BUT I COULDN'T SAY FOR SURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-159 THEY LOOKED AT THE LOVELY LITTLE GIRL WONDERINGLY AND THE WIZARD ASKED, WHAT HAPPENS TO YOUR PAPER VILLAGE WHEN IT RAINS?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-160 IT DOES NOT RAIN HERE REPLIED MISS CUTTENCLIP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-161 GLINDA KEEPS ALL THE RAIN STORMS AWAY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-162 SO I NEVER WORRY ABOUT MY DOLLS GETTING WET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-163 BUT NOW IF YOU WILL COME WITH ME IT WILL GIVE ME PLEASURE TO SHOW YOU OVER MY PAPER KINGDOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-164 OF COURSE YOU MUST GO SLOWLY AND CAREFULLY AND AVOID MAKING ANY BREEZE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-165 THEY LEFT THE COTTAGE AND FOLLOWED THEIR GUIDE THROUGH THE VARIOUS STREETS OF THE VILLAGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-166 IT WAS INDEED AN AMAZING PLACE WHEN ONE CONSIDERED THAT IT WAS ALL MADE WITH SCISSORS AND THE VISITORS WERE NOT ONLY GREATLY INTERESTED BUT FULL OF ADMIRATION FOR THE SKILL OF LITTLE MISS CUTTENCLIP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-167 IN ONE PLACE A LARGE GROUP OF ESPECIALLY NICE PAPER DOLLS ASSEMBLED TO GREET THEIR QUEEN WHOM IT WAS EASY TO SEE THEY LOVED EARLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-168 THESE DOLLS MARCHED AND DANCED BEFORE THE VISITORS AND THEN THEY ALL WAVED THEIR PAPER HANDKERCHIEFS AND SANG IN A SWEET CHORUS A SONG CALLED THE FLAG OF OUR NATIVE LAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-169 AT THE CONCLUSION OF THE SONG THEY RAN UP A HANDSOME PAPER FLAG ON A TALL FLAGPOLE AND ALL OF THE PEOPLE OF THE VILLAGE GATHERED AROUND TO CHEER AS LOUDLY AS THEY COULD ALTHOUGH OF COURSE THEIR VOICES WERE NOT ESPECIALLY STRONG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-170 MISS CUTTENCLIP WAS ABOUT TO MAKE HER SUBJECTS A SPEECH IN REPLY TO THIS PATRIOTIC SONG WHEN THE SHAGGY MAN HAPPENED TO SNEEZE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-171 HE WAS A VERY LOUD AND POWERFUL SNEEZER AT ANY TIME AND HE HAD TRIED SO HARD TO HOLD IN THIS SNEEZE THAT WHEN IT SUDDENLY EXPLODED THE RESULT WAS TERRIBLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-172 THE PAPER DOLLS WERE MOWED DOWN BY DOZENS AND FLEW AND FLUTTERED IN WILD CONFUSION IN EVERY DIRECTION TUMBLING THIS WAY AND THAT AND GETTING MORE OR LESS WRINKLED AND BENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-173 A WAIL OF TERROR AND GRIEF CAME FROM THE SCATTERED THRONG AND MISS CUTTENCLIP EXCLAIMED, DEAR ME!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-174 DEAR ME!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-175 AND HURRIED AT ONCE TO THE RESCUE OF HER OVERTURNED PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-176 OH SHAGGY MAN!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-177 HOW COULD YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-178 ASKED DOROTHY REPROACHFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-179 I COULDN'T HELP IT REALLY I COULDN'T PROTESTED THE SHAGGY MAN LOOKING QUITE ASHAMED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-180 AND I HAD NO IDEA IT TOOK SO LITTLE TO UPSET THESE PAPER DOLLS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-181 SO LITTLE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-182 SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-183 WHY IT WAS MOST AS BAD AS A KANSAS CYCLONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-184 AND THEN SHE HELPED MISS CUTTENCLIP RESCUE THE PAPER FOLK AND STAND THEM ON THEIR FEET AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-185 TWO OF THE CARDBOARD HOUSES HAD ALSO TUMBLED OVER AND THE LITTLE QUEEN SAID SHE WOULD HAVE TO REPAIR THEM AND PASTE THEM TOGETHER BEFORE THEY COULD BE LIVED IN AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-186 AND NOW FEARING THEY MIGHT DO MORE DAMAGE TO THE FLIMSY PAPER PEOPLE THEY DECIDED TO GO AWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-187 BUT FIRST THEY THANKED MISS CUTTENCLIP VERY WARMLY FOR HER COURTESY AND KINDNESS TO THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-188 ANY FRIEND OF PRINCESS OZMA IS ALWAYS WELCOME HERE UNLESS HE SNEEZES SAID THE QUEEN WITH A RATHER SEVERE LOOK AT THE SHAGGY MAN WHO HUNG HIS HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-189 I LIKE TO HAVE VISITORS ADMIRE MY WONDERFUL VILLAGE AND I HOPE YOU WILL CALL AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-190 MISS CUTTENCLIP HERSELF LED THEM TO THE DOOR IN THE WALL AND AS THEY PASSED ALONG THE STREET THE PAPER DOLLS PEEPED AT THEM HALF FEARFULLY FROM THE DOORS AND WINDOWS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-10-191 PERHAPS THEY WILL NEVER FORGET THE SHAGGY MAN'S AWFUL SNEEZE AND I AM SURE THEY WERE ALL GLAD TO SEE THE MEAT PEOPLE GO AWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-01 CHAPTER ELEVEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-02 HOW THE GENERAL MET THE FIRST AND FOREMOST ON LEAVING THE GROWLEYWOGS GENERAL GUPH HAD TO RECROSS THE RIPPLE LANDS AND HE DID NOT FIND IT A PLEASANT THING TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-03 PERHAPS HAVING HIS WHISKERS PULLED OUT ONE BY ONE AND BEING USED AS A PIN CUSHION FOR THE INNOCENT AMUSEMENT OF A GOOD NATURED JAILER HAD NOT IMPROVED THE QUALITY OF GUPH'S TEMPER FOR THE OLD NOME RAVED AND RAGED AT THE RECOLLECTION OF THE WRONGS HE HAD SUFFERED AND VOWED TO TAKE VENGEANCE UPON THE GROWLEYWOGS AFTER HE HAD USED THEM FOR HIS PURPOSES AND OZ HAD BEEN CONQUERED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-04 HE WENT ON IN THIS FURIOUS WAY UNTIL HE WAS HALF ACROSS THE RIPPLE LAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-05 THEN HE BECAME SEASICK AND THE REST OF THE WAY THIS NAUGHTY NOME WAS ALMOST AS MISERABLE AS HE DESERVED TO BE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-06 BUT WHEN HE REACHED THE PLAINS AGAIN AND THE GROUND WAS FIRM UNDER HIS FEET HE BEGAN TO FEEL BETTER AND INSTEAD OF GOING BACK HOME HE TURNED DIRECTLY WEST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-07 A SQUIRREL PERCHED IN A TREE SAW HIM TAKE THIS ROAD AND CALLED TO HIM WARNINGLY, LOOK OUT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-08 BUT HE PAID NO ATTENTION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-09 AN EAGLE PAUSED IN ITS FLIGHT THROUGH THE AIR TO LOOK AT HIM WONDERINGLY AND SAY, LOOK OUT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-10 BUT ON HE WENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-11 NO ONE CAN SAY THAT GUPH WAS NOT BRAVE FOR HE HAD DETERMINED TO VISIT THOSE DANGEROUS CREATURES THE PHANFASMS WHO RESIDED UPON THE VERY TOP OF THE DREAD MOUNTAIN OF PHANTASTICO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-12 THE PHANFASMS WERE ERBS AND SO DREADED BY MORTALS AND IMMORTALS ALIKE THAT NO ONE HAD BEEN NEAR THEIR MOUNTAIN HOME FOR SEVERAL THOUSAND YEARS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-13 YET GENERAL GUPH HOPED TO INDUCE THEM TO JOIN IN HIS PROPOSED WARFARE AGAINST THE GOOD AND HAPPY OZ PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-14 GUPH KNEW VERY WELL THAT THE PHANFASMS WOULD BE ALMOST AS DANGEROUS TO THE NOMES AS THEY WOULD TO THE OZITES BUT HE THOUGHT HIMSELF SO CLEVER THAT HE BELIEVED HE COULD MANAGE THESE STRANGE CREATURES AND MAKE THEM OBEY HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-15 AND THERE WAS NO DOUBT AT ALL THAT IF HE COULD ENLIST THE SERVICES OF THE PHANFASMS THEIR TREMENDOUS POWER UNITED TO THE STRENGTH OF THE GROWLEYWOGS AND THE CUNNING OF THE WHIMSIES WOULD DOOM THE LAND OF OZ TO ABSOLUTE DESTRUCTION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-16 SO THE OLD NOME CLIMBED THE FOOTHILLS AND TRUDGED ALONG THE WILD MOUNTAIN PATHS UNTIL HE CAME TO A BIG GULLY THAT ENCIRCLED THE MOUNTAIN OF PHANTASTICO AND MARKED THE BOUNDARY LINE OF THE DOMINION OF THE PHANFASMS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-17 THIS GULLY WAS ABOUT A THIRD OF THE WAY UP THE MOUNTAIN AND IT WAS FILLED TO THE BRIM WITH RED HOT MOLTEN LAVA IN WHICH SWAM FIRE SERPENTS AND POISONOUS SALAMANDERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-18 THE HEAT FROM THIS MASS AND ITS POISONOUS SMELL WERE BOTH SO UNBEARABLE THAT EVEN BIRDS HESITATED TO FLY OVER THE GULLY BUT CIRCLED AROUND IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-19 ALL LIVING THINGS KEPT AWAY FROM THE MOUNTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-20 NOW GUPH HAD HEARD DURING HIS LONG LIFETIME MANY TALES OF THESE DREADED PHANFASMS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-21 SO HE HAD HEARD OF THIS BARRIER OF MELTED LAVA AND ALSO HE HAD BEEN TOLD THAT THERE WAS A NARROW BRIDGE THAT SPANNED IT IN ONE PLACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-22 SO HE WALKED ALONG THE EDGE UNTIL HE FOUND THE BRIDGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-23 IT WAS A SINGLE ARCH OF GRAY STONE AND LYING FLAT UPON THE BRIDGE WAS A SCARLET ALLIGATOR SEEMINGLY FAST ASLEEP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-24 WHEN GUPH STUMBLED OVER THE ROCKS IN APPROACHING THE BRIDGE THE CREATURE OPENED ITS EYES FROM WHICH TINY FLAMES SHOT IN ALL DIRECTIONS AND AFTER LOOKING AT THE INTRUDER VERY WICKEDLY THE SCARLET ALLIGATOR CLOSED ITS EYELIDS AGAIN AND LAY STILL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-25 GUPH SAW THERE WAS NO ROOM FOR HIM TO PASS THE ALLIGATOR ON THE NARROW BRIDGE SO HE CALLED OUT TO IT, GOOD MORNING FRIEND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-26 I DON'T WISH TO HURRY YOU BUT PLEASE TELL ME IF YOU ARE COMING DOWN OR GOING UP?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-27 NEITHER SNAPPED THE ALLIGATOR CLICKING ITS CRUEL JAWS TOGETHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-28 THE GENERAL HESITATED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-29 ARE YOU LIKELY TO STAY THERE LONG?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-30 HE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-31 A FEW HUNDRED YEARS OR SO SAID THE ALLIGATOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-32 GUPH SOFTLY RUBBED THE END OF HIS NOSE AND TRIED TO THINK WHAT TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-33 DO YOU KNOW WHETHER THE FIRST AND FOREMOST PHANFASM OF PHANTASTICO IS AT HOME OR NOT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-34 HE PRESENTLY INQUIRED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-35 I EXPECT HE IS SEEING HE IS ALWAYS AT HOME REPLIED THE ALLIGATOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-36 AH,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-37 WHO IS THAT COMING DOWN THE MOUNTAIN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-38 ASKED THE NOME GAZING UPWARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-39 THE ALLIGATOR TURNED TO LOOK OVER ITS SHOULDER AND AT ONCE GUPH RAN TO THE BRIDGE AND LEAPED OVER THE SENTINEL'S BACK BEFORE IT COULD TURN BACK AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-40 THE SCARLET MONSTER MADE A SNAP AT THE NOME'S LEFT FOOT BUT MISSED IT BY FULLY AN INCH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-41 AH HA!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-42 LAUGHED THE GENERAL WHO WAS NOW ON THE MOUNTAIN PATH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-43 I FOOLED YOU THAT TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-44 SO YOU DID,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-45 AND PERHAPS YOU FOOLED YOURSELF RETORTED THE ALLIGATOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-46 GO UP THE MOUNTAIN IF YOU DARE AND FIND OUT WHAT THE FIRST AND FOREMOST WILL DO TO YOU!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-47 I WILL DECLARED GUPH BOLDLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-48 AND ON HE WENT UP THE PATH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-49 AT FIRST THE SCENE WAS WILD ENOUGH BUT GRADUALLY IT GREW MORE AND MORE AWFUL IN APPEARANCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-50 ALL THE ROCKS HAD THE SHAPES OF FRIGHTFUL BEINGS AND EVEN THE TREE TRUNKS WERE GNARLED AND TWISTED LIKE SERPENTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-51 SUDDENLY THERE APPEARED BEFORE THE NOME A MAN WITH THE HEAD OF AN OWL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-52 HIS BODY WAS HAIRY LIKE THAT OF AN APE AND HIS ONLY CLOTHING WAS A SCARLET SCARF TWISTED AROUND HIS WAIST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-53 HE BORE A HUGE CLUB IN HIS HAND AND HIS ROUND OWL EYES BLINKED FIERCELY UPON THE INTRUDER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-54 WHAT ARE YOU DOING HERE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-55 HE DEMANDED THREATENING GUPH WITH HIS CLUB.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-56 I'VE COME TO SEE THE FIRST AND FOREMOST PHANFASM OF PHANTASTICO REPLIED THE GENERAL WHO DID NOT LIKE THE WAY THIS CREATURE LOOKED AT HIM BUT STILL WAS NOT AFRAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-57 AH,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-58 YOU SHALL SEE HIM!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-59 THE MAN SAID WITH A SNEERING LAUGH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-60 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST SHALL DECIDE UPON THE BEST WAY TO PUNISH YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-61 HE WILL NOT PUNISH ME RETURNED GUPH CALMLY FOR I HAVE COME HERE TO DO HIM AND HIS PEOPLE A RARE FAVOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-62 LEAD ON FELLOW AND TAKE ME DIRECTLY TO YOUR MASTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-63 THE OWL MAN RAISED HIS CLUB WITH A THREATENING GESTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-64 IF YOU TRY TO ESCAPE HE SAID BEWARE BUT HERE THE GENERAL INTERRUPTED HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-65 SPARE YOUR THREATS SAID HE AND DO NOT BE IMPERTINENT OR I WILL HAVE YOU SEVERELY PUNISHED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-66 LEAD ON AND KEEP SILENT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-67 THIS GUPH WAS REALLY A CLEVER RASCAL AND IT SEEMS A PITY HE WAS SO BAD FOR IN A GOOD CAUSE HE MIGHT HAVE ACCOMPLISHED MUCH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-68 HE REALIZED THAT HE HAD PUT HIMSELF INTO A DANGEROUS POSITION BY COMING TO THIS DREADFUL MOUNTAIN BUT HE ALSO KNEW THAT IF HE SHOWED FEAR HE WAS LOST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-69 SO HE ADOPTED A BOLD MANNER AS HIS BEST DEFENSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-70 THE WISDOM OF THIS PLAN WAS SOON EVIDENT FOR THE PHANFASM WITH THE OWL'S HEAD TURNED AND LED THE WAY UP THE MOUNTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-71 AT THE VERY TOP WAS A LEVEL PLAIN UPON WHICH WERE HEAPS OF ROCK THAT AT FIRST GLANCE SEEMED SOLID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-72 BUT ON LOOKING CLOSER GUPH DISCOVERED THAT THESE ROCK HEAPS WERE DWELLINGS FOR EACH HAD AN OPENING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-73 NOT A PERSON WAS TO BE SEEN OUTSIDE THE ROCK HUTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-74 ALL WAS SILENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-75 THE OWL MAN LED THE WAY AMONG THE GROUPS OF DWELLINGS TO ONE STANDING IN THE CENTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-76 IT SEEMED NO BETTER AND NO WORSE THAN ANY OF THE OTHERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-77 OUTSIDE THE ENTRANCE TO THIS ROCK HEAP THE GUIDE GAVE A LOW WAIL THAT SOUNDED LIKE LEE OW AH!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-78 SUDDENLY THERE BOUNDED FROM THE OPENING ANOTHER HAIRY MAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-79 THIS ONE WORE THE HEAD OF A BEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-80 IN HIS HAND HE BORE A BRASS HOOP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-81 HE GLARED AT THE STRANGER IN EVIDENT SURPRISE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-82 WHY HAVE YOU CAPTURED THIS FOOLISH WANDERER AND BROUGHT HIM HERE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-83 HE DEMANDED ADDRESSING THE OWL MAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-84 I DID NOT CAPTURE HIM WAS THE ANSWER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-85 HE PASSED THE SCARLET ALLIGATOR AND CAME HERE OF HIS OWN FREE WILL AND ACCORD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-86 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST LOOKED AT THE GENERAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-87 HAVE YOU TIRED OF LIFE THEN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-88 HE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-89 NO INDEED ANSWERED GUPH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-90 I AM A NOME AND THE CHIEF GENERAL OF KING ROQUAT THE RED'S GREAT ARMY OF NOMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-91 I COME OF A LONG LIVED RACE AND I MAY SAY THAT I EXPECT TO LIVE A LONG TIME YET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-92 SIT DOWN YOU PHANFASMS IF YOU CAN FIND A SEAT IN THIS WILD HAUNT AND LISTEN TO WHAT I HAVE TO SAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-93 WITH ALL HIS KNOWLEDGE AND BRAVERY GENERAL GUPH DID NOT KNOW THAT THE STEADY GLARE FROM THE BEAR EYES WAS READING HIS INMOST THOUGHTS AS SURELY AS IF THEY HAD BEEN PUT INTO WORDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-94 HE DID NOT KNOW THAT THESE DESPISED ROCK HEAPS OF THE PHANFASMS WERE MERELY DECEPTIONS TO HIS OWN EYES NOR COULD HE GUESS THAT HE WAS STANDING IN THE MIDST OF ONE OF THE MOST SPLENDID AND LUXURIOUS CITIES EVER BUILT BY MAGIC POWER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-95 ALL THAT HE SAW WAS A BARREN WASTE OF ROCK HEAPS A HAIRY MAN WITH AN OWL'S HEAD AND ANOTHER WITH A BEAR'S HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-96 THE SORCERY OF THE PHANFASMS PERMITTED HIM TO SEE NO MORE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-97 SUDDENLY THE FIRST AND FOREMOST SWUNG HIS BRASS HOOP AND CAUGHT GUPH AROUND THE NECK WITH IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-98 THE NEXT INSTANT BEFORE THE GENERAL COULD THINK WHAT HAD HAPPENED TO HIM HE WAS DRAGGED INSIDE THE ROCK HUT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-99 HERE HIS EYES STILL BLINDED TO REALITIES HE PERCEIVED ONLY A DIM LIGHT BY WHICH THE HUT SEEMED AS ROUGH AND RUDE INSIDE AS IT WAS OUTSIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-100 YET HE HAD A STRANGE FEELING THAT MANY BRIGHT EYES WERE FASTENED UPON HIM AND THAT HE STOOD IN A VAST AND EXTENSIVE HALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-101 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST NOW LAUGHED GRIMLY AND RELEASED HIS PRISONER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-102 IF YOU HAVE ANYTHING TO SAY THAT IS INTERESTING HE REMARKED SPEAK OUT BEFORE I STRANGLE YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-103 SO GUPH SPOKE OUT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-104 HE TRIED NOT TO PAY ANY ATTENTION TO A STRANGE RUSTLING SOUND THAT HE HEARD AS OF AN UNSEEN MULTITUDE DRAWING NEAR TO LISTEN TO HIS WORDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-105 HIS EYES COULD SEE ONLY THE FIERCE BEAR MAN AND TO HIM HE ADDRESSED HIS SPEECH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-106 FIRST HE TOLD OF HIS PLAN TO CONQUER THE LAND OF OZ AND PLUNDER THE COUNTRY OF ITS RICHES AND ENSLAVE ITS PEOPLE WHO BEING FAIRIES COULD NOT BE KILLED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-107 AFTER RELATING ALL THIS AND TELLING OF THE TUNNEL THE NOME KING WAS BUILDING HE SAID HE HAD COME TO ASK THE FIRST AND FOREMOST TO JOIN THE NOMES WITH HIS BAND OF TERRIBLE WARRIORS AND HELP THEM TO DEFEAT THE OZ PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-108 THE GENERAL SPOKE VERY EARNESTLY AND IMPRESSIVELY BUT WHEN HE HAD FINISHED THE BEAR MAN BEGAN TO LAUGH AS IF MUCH AMUSED AND HIS LAUGHTER SEEMED TO BE ECHOED BY A CHORUS OF MERRIMENT FROM AN UNSEEN MULTITUDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-109 THEN FOR THE FIRST TIME GUPH BEGAN TO FEEL A TRIFLE WORRIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-110 WHO ELSE HAS PROMISED TO HELP YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-111 FINALLY ASKED THE FIRST AND FOREMOST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-112 THE WHIMSIES REPLIED THE GENERAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-113 AGAIN THE BEAR HEADED PHANFASM LAUGHED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-114 ANY OTHERS?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-115 HE INQUIRED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-116 ONLY THE GROWLEYWOGS SAID GUPH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-117 THIS ANSWER SET THE FIRST AND FOREMOST LAUGHING ANEW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-118 WHAT SHARE OF THE SPOILS AM I TO HAVE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-119 WAS THE NEXT QUESTION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-120 ANYTHING YOU LIKE EXCEPT KING ROQUAT'S MAGIC BELT REPLIED GUPH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-121 AT THIS THE PHANFASM SET UP A ROAR OF LAUGHTER WHICH HAD ITS ECHO IN THE UNSEEN CHORUS AND THE BEAR MAN SEEMED SO AMUSED THAT HE ACTUALLY ROLLED UPON THE GROUND AND SHOUTED WITH MERRIMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-122 OH THESE BLIND AND FOOLISH NOMES!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-123 HE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-124 HOW BIG THEY SEEM TO THEMSELVES AND HOW SMALL THEY REALLY ARE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-125 SUDDENLY HE AROSE AND SEIZED GUPH'S NECK WITH ONE HAIRY PAW DRAGGING HIM OUT OF THE HUT INTO THE OPEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-126 HERE HE GAVE A CURIOUS WAILING CRY AND AS IF IN ANSWER FROM ALL THE ROCKY HUTS ON THE MOUNTAIN TOP CAME FLOCKING A HORDE OF PHANFASMS ALL WITH HAIRY BODIES BUT WEARING HEADS OF VARIOUS ANIMALS BIRDS AND REPTILES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-127 ALL WERE FEROCIOUS AND REPULSIVE LOOKING TO THE DECEIVED EYES OF THE NOME AND GUPH COULD NOT REPRESS A SHUDDER OF DISGUST AS HE LOOKED UPON THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-128 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST SLOWLY RAISED HIS ARMS AND IN A TWINKLING HIS HAIRY SKIN FELL FROM HIM AND HE APPEARED BEFORE THE ASTONISHED NOME AS A BEAUTIFUL WOMAN CLOTHED IN A FLOWING GOWN OF PINK GAUZE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-129 IN HER DARK HAIR FLOWERS WERE ENTWINED AND HER FACE WAS NOBLE AND CALM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-130 AT THE SAME INSTANT THE ENTIRE BAND OF PHANFASMS WAS TRANSFORMED INTO A PACK OF HOWLING WOLVES RUNNING HERE AND THERE AS THEY SNARLED AND SHOWED THEIR UGLY YELLOW FANGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-131 THE WOMAN NOW RAISED HER ARMS EVEN AS THE MAN BEAR HAD DONE AND IN A TWINKLING THE WOLVES BECAME CRAWLING LIZARDS WHILE SHE HERSELF CHANGED INTO A HUGE BUTTERFLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-132 GUPH HAD ONLY TIME TO CRY OUT IN FEAR AND TAKE A STEP BACKWARD TO AVOID THE LIZARDS WHEN ANOTHER TRANSFORMATION OCCURRED AND ALL RETURNED INSTANTLY TO THE FORMS THEY HAD ORIGINALLY WORN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-133 THEN THE FIRST AND FOREMOST WHO HAD RESUMED HIS HAIRY BODY AND BEAR HEAD TURNED TO THE NOME AND ASKED, DO YOU STILL DEMAND OUR ASSISTANCE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-134 MORE THAN EVER ANSWERED THE GENERAL FIRMLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-135 THEN TELL ME, WHAT CAN YOU OFFER THE PHANFASMS THAT THEY HAVE NOT ALREADY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-136 INQUIRED THE FIRST AND FOREMOST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-137 GUPH HESITATED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-138 HE REALLY DID NOT KNOW WHAT TO SAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-139 THE NOME KING'S VAUNTED MAGIC BELT SEEMED A POOR THING COMPARED TO THE ASTONISHING MAGICAL POWERS OF THESE PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-140 GOLD JEWELS AND SLAVES THEY MIGHT SECURE IN ANY QUANTITY WITHOUT ESPECIAL EFFORT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-141 HE FELT THAT HE WAS DEALING WITH POWERS GREATLY BEYOND HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-142 THERE WAS BUT ONE ARGUMENT THAT MIGHT INFLUENCE THE PHANFASMS WHO WERE CREATURES OF EVIL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-143 PERMIT ME TO CALL YOUR ATTENTION TO THE EXQUISITE JOY OF MAKING THE HAPPY UNHAPPY SAID HE AT LAST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-144 CONSIDER THE PLEASURE OF DESTROYING INNOCENT AND HARMLESS PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-145 AH!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-146 YOU HAVE ANSWERED ME CRIED THE FIRST AND FOREMOST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-147 FOR THAT REASON ALONE WE WILL AID YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-148 GO HOME AND TELL YOUR BANDY LEGGED KING THAT AS SOON AS HIS TUNNEL IS FINISHED THE PHANFASMS WILL BE WITH HIM AND LEAD HIS LEGIONS TO THE CONQUEST OF OZ. THE DEADLY DESERT ALONE HAS KEPT US FROM DESTROYING OZ LONG AGO AND YOUR UNDERGROUND TUNNEL IS A CLEVER THOUGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-149 GO HOME AND PREPARE FOR OUR COMING!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-150 GUPH WAS VERY GLAD TO BE PERMITTED TO GO WITH THIS PROMISE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-151 THE OWL MAN LED HIM BACK DOWN THE MOUNTAIN PATH AND ORDERED THE SCARLET ALLIGATOR TO CRAWL AWAY AND ALLOW THE NOME TO CROSS THE BRIDGE IN SAFETY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-152 AFTER THE VISITOR HAD GONE A BRILLIANT AND GORGEOUS CITY APPEARED UPON THE MOUNTAIN TOP CLEARLY VISIBLE TO THE EYES OF THE GAILY DRESSED MULTITUDE OF PHANFASMS THAT LIVED THERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-153 AND THE FIRST AND FOREMOST BEAUTIFULLY ARRAYED ADDRESSED THE OTHERS IN THESE WORDS, IT IS TIME WE WENT INTO THE WORLD AND BROUGHT SORROW AND DISMAY TO ITS PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-154 TOO LONG HAVE WE REMAINED FOR OURSELVES UPON THIS MOUNTAIN TOP FOR WHILE WE ARE THUS SECLUDED MANY NATIONS HAVE GROWN HAPPY AND PROSPEROUS AND THE CHIEF JOY OF THE RACE OF PHANFASMS IS TO DESTROY HAPPINESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-155 SO I THINK IT IS LUCKY THAT THIS MESSENGER FROM THE NOMES ARRIVED AMONG US JUST NOW TO REMIND US THAT THE OPPORTUNITY HAS COME FOR US TO MAKE TROUBLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-156 WE WILL USE KING ROQUAT'S TUNNEL TO CONQUER THE LAND OF OZ. THEN WE WILL DESTROY THE WHIMSIES THE GROWLEYWOGS AND THE NOMES AND AFTERWARD GO OUT TO RAVAGE AND ANNOY AND GRIEVE THE WHOLE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-157 THE MULTITUDE OF EVIL PHANFASMS EAGERLY APPLAUDED THIS PLAN WHICH THEY FULLY APPROVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-11-158 I AM TOLD THAT THE ERBS ARE THE MOST POWERFUL AND MERCILESS OF ALL THE EVIL SPIRITS AND THE PHANFASMS OF PHANTASTICO BELONG TO THE RACE OF ERBS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-01 CHAPTER TWELVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-02 HOW THEY MATCHED THE FUDDLES DOROTHY AND HER FELLOW TRAVELERS RODE AWAY FROM THE CUTTENCLIP VILLAGE AND FOLLOWED THE INDISTINCT PATH AS FAR AS THE SIGN POST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-03 HERE THEY TOOK THE MAIN ROAD AGAIN AND PROCEEDED PLEASANTLY THROUGH THE PRETTY FARMING COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-04 WHEN EVENING CAME THEY STOPPED AT A DWELLING AND WERE JOYFULLY WELCOMED AND GIVEN PLENTY TO EAT AND GOOD BEDS FOR THE NIGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-05 EARLY NEXT MORNING HOWEVER THEY WERE UP AND EAGER TO START AND AFTER A GOOD BREAKFAST THEY BADE THEIR HOST GOOD BYE AND CLIMBED INTO THE RED WAGON TO WHICH THE SAWHORSE HAD BEEN HITCHED ALL NIGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-06 BEING MADE OF WOOD THIS HORSE NEVER GOT TIRED NOR CARED TO LIE DOWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-07 DOROTHY WAS NOT QUITE SURE WHETHER HE EVER SLEPT OR NOT BUT IT WAS CERTAIN THAT HE NEVER DID WHEN ANYBODY WAS AROUND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-08 THE WEATHER IS ALWAYS BEAUTIFUL IN OZ AND THIS MORNING THE AIR WAS COOL AND REFRESHING AND THE SUNSHINE BRILLIANT AND DELIGHTFUL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-09 IN ABOUT AN HOUR THEY CAME TO A PLACE WHERE ANOTHER ROAD BRANCHED OFF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-10 THERE WAS A SIGN POST HERE WHICH READ, THIS WAY TO FUDDLECUMJIG OH HERE IS WHERE WE TURN SAID DOROTHY OBSERVING THE SIGN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-11 WHAT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-12 ARE WE GOING TO FUDDLECUMJIG?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-13 ASKED THE CAPTAIN GENERAL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-14 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-15 OZMA THOUGHT WE MIGHT ENJOY THE FUDDLES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-16 THEY ARE SAID TO BE VERY INTERESTING SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-17 NO ONE WOULD SUSPECT IT FROM THEIR NAME SAID AUNT EM. WHO ARE THEY ANYHOW?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-18 MORE PAPER THINGS?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-19 I THINK NOT ANSWERED DOROTHY LAUGHING,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-20 BUT I CAN'T SAY ZACTLY AUNT EM WHAT THEY ARE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-21 WE'LL FIND OUT WHEN WE GET THERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-22 PERHAPS THE WIZARD KNOWS SUGGESTED UNCLE HENRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-23 NO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-24 I'VE NEVER BEEN THERE BEFORE SAID THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-25 BUT I'VE OFTEN HEARD OF FUDDLECUMJIG AND THE FUDDLES WHO ARE SAID TO BE THE MOST PECULIAR PEOPLE IN ALL THE LAND OF OZ. IN WHAT WAY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-26 ASKED THE SHAGGY MAN. I DON'T KNOW I'M SURE SAID THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-27 JUST THEN AS THEY RODE ALONG THE PRETTY GREEN LANE TOWARD FUDDLECUMJIG THEY ESPIED A KANGAROO SITTING BY THE ROADSIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-28 THE POOR ANIMAL HAD ITS FACE COVERED WITH BOTH ITS FRONT PAWS AND WAS CRYING SO BITTERLY THAT THE TEARS COURSED DOWN ITS CHEEKS IN TWO TINY STREAMS AND TRICKLED ACROSS THE ROAD WHERE THEY FORMED A POOL IN A SMALL HOLLOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-29 THE SAWHORSE STOPPED SHORT AT THIS PITIFUL SIGHT AND DOROTHY CRIED OUT WITH READY SYMPATHY, WHAT'S THE MATTER KANGAROO?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-30 BOO HOO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-31 BOO HOO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-32 WAILED THE KANGAROO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-33 I'VE LOST MY MI MI MI OH BOO HOO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-34 BOO HOO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-35 POOR THING SAID THE WIZARD SHE'S LOST HER MISTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-36 IT'S PROBABLY HER HUSBAND AND HE'S DEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-37 NO NO NO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-38 SOBBED THE KANGAROO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-39 IT IT ISN'T THAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-40 I'VE LOST MY MI MI OH BOO BOO HOO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-41 I KNOW SAID THE SHAGGY MAN,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-42 SHE'S LOST HER MIRROR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-43 NO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-44 THE KANGAROO CRIED HARDER THAN EVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-45 IT MUST BE HER MINCE PIE SUGGESTED AUNT EM. OR HER MILK TOAST PROPOSED UNCLE HENRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-46 I'VE LOST MY MI MI MITTENS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-47 SAID THE KANGAROO GETTING IT OUT AT LAST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-48 OH!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-49 CRIED THE YELLOW HEN WITH A CACKLE OF RELIEF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-50 WHY DIDN'T YOU SAY SO BEFORE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-51 BOO HOO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-52 I I COULDN'T ANSWERED THE KANGAROO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-53 BUT SEE HERE SAID DOROTHY YOU DON'T NEED MITTENS IN THIS WARM WEATHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-54 YES INDEED I DO REPLIED THE ANIMAL STOPPING HER SOBS AND REMOVING HER PAWS FROM HER FACE TO LOOK AT THE LITTLE GIRL REPROACHFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-55 MY HANDS WILL GET ALL SUNBURNED AND TANNED WITHOUT MY MITTENS AND I'VE WORN THEM SO LONG THAT I'LL PROBABLY CATCH COLD WITHOUT THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-56 NONSENSE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-57 SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-58 I NEVER HEARD OF ANY KANGAROO WEARING MITTENS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-59 DIDN'T YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-60 ASKED THE ANIMAL AS IF SURPRISED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-61 NEVER!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-62 REPEATED THE GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-63 AND YOU'LL PROBABLY MAKE YOURSELF SICK IF YOU DON'T STOP CRYING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-64 WHERE DO YOU LIVE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-65 ABOUT TWO MILES BEYOND FUDDLECUMJIG WAS THE ANSWER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-66 GRANDMOTHER GNIT MADE ME THE MITTENS AND SHE'S ONE OF THE FUDDLES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-67 WELL YOU'D BETTER GO HOME NOW AND PERHAPS THE OLD LADY WILL MAKE YOU ANOTHER PAIR SUGGESTED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-68 WE'RE ON OUR WAY TO FUDDLECUMJIG AND YOU MAY HOP ALONG BESIDE US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-69 SO THEY RODE ON AND THE KANGAROO HOPPED BESIDE THE RED WAGON AND SEEMED QUICKLY TO HAVE FORGOTTEN HER LOSS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-70 BY AND BY THE WIZARD SAID TO THE ANIMAL, ARE THE FUDDLES NICE PEOPLE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-71 OH VERY NICE ANSWERED THE KANGAROO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-72 THAT IS WHEN THEY'RE PROPERLY PUT TOGETHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-73 BUT THEY GET DREADFULLY SCATTERED AND MIXED UP AT TIMES AND THEN YOU CAN'T DO ANYTHING WITH THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-74 WHAT DO YOU MEAN BY THEIR GETTING SCATTERED?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-75 INQUIRED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-76 WHY THEY'RE MADE IN A GOOD MANY SMALL PIECES EXPLAINED THE KANGAROO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-77 AND WHENEVER ANY STRANGER COMES NEAR THEM THEY HAVE A HABIT OF FALLING APART AND SCATTERING THEMSELVES AROUND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-78 THAT'S WHEN THEY GET SO DREADFULLY MIXED AND IT'S A HARD PUZZLE TO PUT THEM TOGETHER AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-79 WHO USUALLY PUTS THEM TOGETHER?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-80 ASKED OMBY AMBY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-81 ANY ONE WHO IS ABLE TO MATCH THE PIECES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-82 I SOMETIMES PUT GRANDMOTHER GNIT TOGETHER MYSELF BECAUSE I KNOW HER SO WELL I CAN TELL EVERY PIECE THAT BELONGS TO HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-83 THEN WHEN SHE'S ALL MATCHED SHE KNITS FOR ME AND THAT'S HOW SHE MADE MY MITTENS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-84 BUT IT TOOK A GOOD MANY DAYS HARD KNITTING AND I HAD TO PUT GRANDMOTHER TOGETHER A GOOD MANY TIMES BECAUSE EVERY TIME I CAME NEAR SHE'D SCATTER HERSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-85 I SHOULD THINK SHE WOULD GET USED TO YOUR COMING AND NOT BE AFRAID SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-86 IT ISN'T THAT REPLIED THE KANGAROO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-87 THEY'RE NOT A BIT AFRAID WHEN THEY'RE PUT TOGETHER AND USUALLY THEY'RE VERY JOLLY AND PLEASANT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-88 IT'S JUST A HABIT THEY HAVE TO SCATTER THEMSELVES AND IF THEY DIDN'T DO IT THEY WOULDN'T BE FUDDLES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-89 THE TRAVELERS THOUGHT UPON THIS QUITE SERIOUSLY FOR A TIME WHILE THE SAWHORSE CONTINUED TO CARRY THEM RAPIDLY FORWARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-90 THEN AUNT EM REMARKED, I DON'T SEE MUCH USE OUR VISITIN THESE FUDDLES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-91 IF WE FIND THEM SCATTERED ALL WE CAN DO IS TO SWEEP EM UP AND THEN GO ABOUT OUR BUSINESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-92 OH I B'LIEVE WE'D BETTER GO ON REPLIED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-93 I'M GETTING HUNGRY AND WE MUST TRY TO GET SOME LUNCHEON AT FUDDLECUMJIG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-94 PERHAPS THE FOOD WON'T BE SCATTERED AS BADLY AS THE PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-95 YOU'LL FIND PLENTY TO EAT THERE DECLARED THE KANGAROO HOPPING ALONG IN BIG BOUNDS BECAUSE THE SAWHORSE WAS GOING SO FAST,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-96 AND THEY HAVE A FINE COOK TOO IF YOU CAN MANAGE TO PUT HIM TOGETHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-97 THERE'S THE TOWN NOW JUST AHEAD OF US!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-98 THEY LOOKED AHEAD AND SAW A GROUP OF VERY PRETTY HOUSES STANDING IN A GREEN FIELD A LITTLE APART FROM THE MAIN ROAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-99 SOME MUNCHKINS CAME HERE A FEW DAYS AGO AND MATCHED A LOT OF PEOPLE TOGETHER SAID THE KANGAROO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-100 I THINK THEY ARE TOGETHER YET AND IF YOU GO SOFTLY WITHOUT MAKING ANY NOISE PERHAPS THEY WON'T SCATTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-101 LET'S TRY IT SUGGESTED THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-102 SO THEY STOPPED THE SAWHORSE AND GOT OUT OF THE WAGON AND AFTER BIDDING GOOD BYE TO THE KANGAROO WHO HOPPED AWAY HOME THEY ENTERED THE FIELD AND VERY CAUTIOUSLY APPROACHED THE GROUP OF HOUSES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-103 SO SILENTLY DID THEY MOVE THAT SOON THEY SAW THROUGH THE WINDOWS OF THE HOUSES PEOPLE MOVING AROUND WHILE OTHERS WERE PASSING TO AND FRO IN THE YARDS BETWEEN THE BUILDINGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-104 THEY SEEMED MUCH LIKE OTHER PEOPLE FROM A DISTANCE AND APPARENTLY THEY DID NOT NOTICE THE LITTLE PARTY SO QUIETLY APPROACHING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-105 THEY HAD ALMOST REACHED THE NEAREST HOUSE WHEN TOTO SAW A LARGE BEETLE CROSSING THE PATH AND BARKED LOUDLY AT IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-106 INSTANTLY A WILD CLATTER WAS HEARD FROM THE HOUSES AND YARDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-107 DOROTHY THOUGHT IT SOUNDED LIKE A SUDDEN HAILSTORM AND THE VISITORS KNOWING THAT CAUTION WAS NO LONGER NECESSARY HURRIED FORWARD TO SEE WHAT HAD HAPPENED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-108 AFTER THE CLATTER AN INTENSE STILLNESS REIGNED IN THE TOWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-109 THE STRANGERS ENTERED THE FIRST HOUSE THEY CAME TO WHICH WAS ALSO THE LARGEST AND FOUND THE FLOOR STREWN WITH PIECES OF THE PEOPLE WHO LIVED THERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-110 THEY LOOKED MUCH LIKE FRAGMENTS OF WOOD NEATLY PAINTED AND WERE OF ALL SORTS OF CURIOUS AND FANTASTIC SHAPES NO TWO PIECES BEING IN ANY WAY ALIKE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-111 THEY PICKED UP SOME OF THESE PIECES AND LOOKED AT THEM CAREFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-112 ON ONE WHICH DOROTHY HELD WAS AN EYE WHICH LOOKED AT HER PLEASANTLY BUT WITH AN INTERESTED EXPRESSION AS IF IT WONDERED WHAT SHE WAS GOING TO DO WITH IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-113 QUITE NEAR BY SHE DISCOVERED AND PICKED UP A NOSE AND BY MATCHING THE TWO PIECES TOGETHER FOUND THAT THEY WERE PART OF A FACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-114 IF I COULD FIND THE MOUTH SHE SAID THIS FUDDLE MIGHT BE ABLE TO TALK AND TELL US WHAT TO DO NEXT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-115 THEN LET US FIND IT REPLIED THE WIZARD AND SO ALL GOT DOWN ON THEIR HANDS AND KNEES AND BEGAN EXAMINING THE SCATTERED PIECES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-116 I'VE FOUND IT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-117 CRIED THE SHAGGY MAN AND RAN TO DOROTHY WITH A QUEER SHAPED PIECE THAT HAD A MOUTH ON IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-12-118 BUT WHEN THEY TRIED TO FIT IT TO THE EYE AND NOSE THEY FOUND THE PARTS WOULDN'T MATCH TOGETHER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-25 EXCLAIMED BILLINA IN HORROR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-26 BROIL MY CHICKENS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-27 WHY THAT'S WHAT THEY'RE FOR AIN'T IT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-28 ASKED AUNT EM ASTONISHED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-29 NO AUNT NOT IN OZ SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-30 PEOPLE DO NOT EAT CHICKENS HERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-31 YOU SEE BILLINA WAS THE FIRST HEN THAT WAS EVER SEEN IN THIS COUNTRY AND I BROUGHT HER HERE MYSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-32 EVERYBODY LIKED HER AN RESPECTED HER SO THE OZ PEOPLE WOULDN'T ANY MORE EAT HER CHICKENS THAN THEY WOULD EAT BILLINA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-33 WELL I DECLARE GASPED AUNT EM. HOW ABOUT THE EGGS?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-34 OH IF WE HAVE MORE EGGS THAN WE WANT TO HATCH WE ALLOW PEOPLE TO EAT THEM SAID BILLINA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-35 INDEED I AM VERY GLAD THE OZ FOLKS LIKE OUR EGGS FOR OTHERWISE THEY WOULD SPOIL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-36 THIS CERTAINLY IS A QUEER COUNTRY SIGHED AUNT EM. EXCUSE ME CALLED THE SAWHORSE THE PATH HAS ENDED AND I'D LIKE TO KNOW WHICH WAY TO GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-37 THEY LOOKED AROUND AND SURE ENOUGH THERE WAS NO PATH TO BE SEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-38 WELL SAID DOROTHY WE'RE GOING SOUTHWEST AND IT SEEMS JUST AS EASY TO FOLLOW THAT DIRECTION WITHOUT A PATH AS WITH ONE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-39 CERTAINLY ANSWERED THE SAWHORSE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-40 IT IS NOT HARD TO DRAW THE WAGON OVER THE MEADOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-41 I ONLY WANT TO KNOW WHERE TO GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-42 THERE'S A FOREST OVER THERE ACROSS THE PRAIRIE SAID THE WIZARD AND IT LIES IN THE DIRECTION WE ARE GOING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-43 MAKE STRAIGHT FOR THE FOREST SAWHORSE AND YOU'RE BOUND TO GO RIGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-44 SO THE WOODEN ANIMAL TROTTED ON AGAIN AND THE MEADOW GRASS WAS SO SOFT UNDER THE WHEELS THAT IT MADE EASY RIDING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-45 BUT DOROTHY WAS A LITTLE UNEASY AT LOSING THE PATH BECAUSE NOW THERE WAS NOTHING TO GUIDE THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-46 NO HOUSES WERE TO BE SEEN AT ALL SO THEY COULD NOT ASK THEIR WAY OF ANY FARMER,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-47 AND ALTHOUGH THE LAND OF OZ WAS ALWAYS BEAUTIFUL WHEREVER ONE MIGHT GO THIS PART OF THE COUNTRY WAS STRANGE TO ALL THE PARTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-48 PERHAPS WE'RE LOST SUGGESTED AUNT EM AFTER THEY HAD PROCEEDED QUITE A WAY IN SILENCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-49 NEVER MIND SAID THE SHAGGY MAN,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-50 I'VE BEEN LOST MANY A TIME AND SO HAS DOROTHY AND WE'VE ALWAYS BEEN FOUND AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-51 THAT IS THE WORST OF GETTING LOST IN A PLACE WHERE THERE ARE NO HOUSES NEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-52 WE HAD A GOOD DINNER AT THE FUDDLE TOWN SAID UNCLE HENRY AND THAT WILL KEEP US FROM STARVING TO DEATH FOR A LONG TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-53 NO ONE EVER STARVED TO DEATH IN OZ DECLARED DOROTHY POSITIVELY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-54 BUT PEOPLE MAY GET PRETTY HUNGRY SOMETIMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-55 THE WIZARD SAID NOTHING AND HE DID NOT SEEM ESPECIALLY ANXIOUS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-56 THE SAWHORSE WAS TROTTING ALONG BRISKLY YET THE FOREST SEEMED FARTHER AWAY THAN THEY HAD THOUGHT WHEN THEY FIRST SAW IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-57 SO IT WAS NEARLY SUNDOWN WHEN THEY FINALLY CAME TO THE TREES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-58 BUT NOW THEY FOUND THEMSELVES IN A MOST BEAUTIFUL SPOT THE WIDE SPREADING TREES BEING COVERED WITH FLOWERING VINES AND HAVING SOFT MOSSES UNDERNEATH THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-59 THIS WILL BE A GOOD PLACE TO CAMP SAID THE WIZARD AS THE SAWHORSE STOPPED FOR FURTHER INSTRUCTIONS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-60 CAMP!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-61 THEY ALL ECHOED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-62 CERTAINLY ASSERTED THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-63 IT WILL BE DARK BEFORE VERY LONG AND WE CANNOT TRAVEL THROUGH THIS FOREST AT NIGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-64 SO LET US MAKE A CAMP HERE AND HAVE SOME SUPPER AND SLEEP UNTIL DAYLIGHT COMES AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-65 THEY ALL LOOKED AT THE LITTLE MAN IN ASTONISHMENT AND AUNT EM SAID WITH A SNIFF, A PRETTY CAMP WE'LL HAVE I MUST SAY!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-66 I SUPPOSE YOU INTEND US TO SLEEP UNDER THE WAGON.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-67 AND CHEW GRASS FOR OUR SUPPER ADDED THE SHAGGY MAN LAUGHING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-68 BUT DOROTHY SEEMED TO HAVE NO DOUBTS AND WAS QUITE CHEERFUL IT'S LUCKY WE HAVE THE WONDERFUL WIZARD WITH US SHE SAID,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-69 BECAUSE HE CAN DO MOST ANYTHING HE WANTS TO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-70 OH YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-71 I FORGOT WE HAD A WIZARD SAID UNCLE HENRY LOOKING AT THE LITTLE MAN CURIOUSLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-72 THE WIZARD SMILED AND CLIMBED OUT OF THE WAGON AND ALL THE OTHERS FOLLOWED HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-73 IN ORDER TO CAMP SAID HE THE FIRST THING WE NEED IS TENTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-74 WILL SOME ONE PLEASE LEND ME A HANDKERCHIEF?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-75 THE SHAGGY MAN OFFERED HIM ONE AND AUNT EM ANOTHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-76 HE TOOK THEM BOTH AND LAID THEM CAREFULLY UPON THE GRASS NEAR TO THE EDGE OF THE FOREST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-77 THEN HE LAID HIS OWN HANDKERCHIEF DOWN TOO AND STANDING A LITTLE BACK FROM THEM HE WAVED HIS LEFT HAND TOWARD THE HANDKERCHIEFS AND SAID, TENTS OF CANVAS WHITE AS SNOW LET ME SEE HOW FAST YOU GROW!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-78 THEN LO AND BEHOLD!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-79 THE HANDKERCHIEFS BECAME TINY TENTS AND AS THE TRAVELERS LOOKED AT THEM THE TENTS GREW BIGGER AND BIGGER UNTIL IN A FEW MINUTES EACH ONE WAS LARGE ENOUGH TO CONTAIN THE ENTIRE PARTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-80 THIS SAID THE WIZARD POINTING TO THE FIRST TENT IS FOR THE ACCOMMODATION OF THE LADIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-81 DOROTHY YOU AND YOUR AUNT MAY STEP INSIDE AND TAKE OFF YOUR THINGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-82 EVERY ONE RAN TO LOOK INSIDE THE TENT AND THEY SAW TWO PRETTY WHITE BEDS ALL READY FOR DOROTHY AND AUNT EM AND A SILVER ROOST FOR BILLINA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-83 RUGS WERE SPREAD UPON THE GRASSY FLOOR AND SOME CAMP CHAIRS AND A TABLE COMPLETED THE FURNITURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-84 WELL WELL WELL!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-85 THIS BEATS ANYTHING I EVER SAW OR HEARD OF!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-86 EXCLAIMED AUNT EM AND SHE GLANCED AT THE WIZARD ALMOST FEARFULLY AS IF HE MIGHT BE DANGEROUS BECAUSE OF HIS GREAT POWERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-87 OH MISTER WIZARD!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-88 HOW DID YOU MANAGE TO DO IT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-89 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-90 IT'S A TRICK GLINDA THE SORCERESS TAUGHT ME AND IT IS MUCH BETTER MAGIC THAN I USED TO PRACTICE IN OMAHA OR WHEN I FIRST CAME TO OZ HE ANSWERED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-91 WHEN THE GOOD GLINDA FOUND I WAS TO LIVE IN THE EMERALD CITY ALWAYS SHE PROMISED TO HELP ME BECAUSE SHE SAID THE WIZARD OF OZ OUGHT REALLY TO BE A CLEVER WIZARD AND NOT A HUMBUG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-92 SO WE HAVE BEEN MUCH TOGETHER AND I AM LEARNING SO FAST THAT I EXPECT TO BE ABLE TO ACCOMPLISH SOME REALLY WONDERFUL THINGS IN TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-93 YOU'VE DONE IT NOW!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-94 DECLARED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-95 THESE TENTS ARE JUST WONDERFUL!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-96 BUT COME AND SEE THE MEN'S TENT SAID THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-97 SO THEY WENT TO THE SECOND TENT WHICH HAD SHAGGY EDGES BECAUSE IT HAS BEEN MADE FROM THE SHAGGY MAN'S HANDKERCHIEF AND FOUND THAT COMPLETELY FURNISHED ALSO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-98 IT CONTAINED FOUR NEAT BEDS FOR UNCLE HENRY OMBY AMBY THE SHAGGY MAN AND THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-99 ALSO THERE WAS A SOFT RUG FOR TOTO TO LIE UPON.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-100 THE THIRD TENT EXPLAINED THE WIZARD IS OUR DINING ROOM AND KITCHEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-101 THEY VISITED THAT NEXT AND FOUND A TABLE AND DISHES IN THE DINING TENT WITH PLENTY OF THOSE THINGS NECESSARY TO USE IN COOKING.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-103 WHILE HE WAS DOING THIS OMBY AMBY AND THE SHAGGY MAN BROUGHT A SUPPLY OF TWIGS FROM THE FOREST AND THEN THEY BUILT A FIRE UNDERNEATH THE KETTLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-104 NOW DOROTHY SAID THE WIZARD SMILING I EXPECT YOU TO COOK OUR SUPPER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-107 INQUIRED THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-108 I DIDN'T SEE ANYTHING PUT IN AND I'M ALMOST SURE IT WAS EMPTY WHEN YOU BROUGHT IT OUT SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-109 NEVERTHELESS SAID THE LITTLE MAN WINKING SLYLY AT UNCLE HENRY YOU WILL DO WELL TO WATCH OUR SUPPER MY DEAR AND SEE THAT IT DOESN'T BOIL OVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-110 THEN THE MEN TOOK SOME PAILS AND WENT INTO THE FOREST TO SEARCH FOR A SPRING OF WATER AND WHILE THEY WERE GONE AUNT EM SAID TO DOROTHY, I BELIEVE THE WIZARD IS FOOLING US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-111 I SAW THE KETTLE MYSELF AND WHEN HE HUNG IT OVER THE FIRE THERE WASN'T A THING IN IT BUT AIR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-112 DON'T WORRY REMARKED BILLINA CONFIDENTLY AS SHE NESTLED IN THE GRASS BEFORE THE FIRE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-113 YOU'LL FIND SOMETHING IN THE KETTLE WHEN IT'S TAKEN OFF AND IT WON'T BE POOR INNOCENT CHICKENS EITHER.
