l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-119 THE PLATTER WAS FAIRLY HEAPED WITH A FINE STEW SMOKING HOT WITH MANY KINDS OF VEGETABLES AND DUMPLINGS AND A RICH DELICIOUS GRAVY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-120 THE WIZARD TRIUMPHANTLY PLACED THE PLATTER UPON THE TABLE IN THE DINING TENT AND THEN THEY ALL SAT DOWN IN CAMP CHAIRS TO THE FEAST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-121 THERE WERE SEVERAL OTHER DISHES ON THE TABLE ALL CAREFULLY COVERED AND WHEN THE TIME CAME TO REMOVE THESE COVERS THEY FOUND BREAD AND BUTTER CAKES CHEESE PICKLES AND FRUITS INCLUDING SOME OF THE LUSCIOUS STRAWBERRIES OF OZ. NO ONE VENTURED TO ASK A QUESTION AS TO HOW THESE THINGS CAME THERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-122 THEY CONTENTED THEMSELVES BY EATING HEARTILY THE GOOD THINGS PROVIDED AND TOTO AND BILLINA HAD THEIR FULL SHARE YOU MAY BE SURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-123 AFTER THE MEAL WAS OVER AUNT EM WHISPERED TO DOROTHY, THAT MAY HAVE BEEN MAGIC FOOD MY DEAR AND FOR THAT REASON PERHAPS IT WON'T BE VERY NOURISHING,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-125 THEN SHE ADDED IN A LOUDER VOICE, WHO'S GOING TO DO THE DISHES?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-126 NO ONE MADAM ANSWERED THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-127 THE DISHES HAVE DONE THEMSELVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-128 LA SAKES!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-129 EJACULATED THE GOOD LADY HOLDING UP HER HANDS IN AMAZEMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-14-130 FOR SURE ENOUGH WHEN SHE LOOKED AT THE DISHES THEY HAD A MOMENT BEFORE LEFT UPON THE TABLE SHE FOUND THEM ALL WASHED AND DRIED AND PILED UP INTO NEAT STACKS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-01 CHAPTER FIFTEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-02 HOW DOROTHY HAPPENED TO GET LOST IT WAS A BEAUTIFUL EVENING SO THEY DREW THEIR CAMP CHAIRS IN A CIRCLE BEFORE ONE OF THE TENTS AND BEGAN TO TELL STORIES TO AMUSE THEMSELVES AND PASS AWAY THE TIME BEFORE THEY WENT TO BED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-03 PRETTY SOON A ZEBRA WAS SEEN COMING OUT OF THE FOREST AND HE TROTTED STRAIGHT UP TO THEM AND SAID POLITELY, GOOD EVENING PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-04 THE ZEBRA WAS A SLEEK LITTLE ANIMAL AND HAD A SLENDER HEAD A STUBBY MANE AND A PAINT BRUSH TAIL VERY LIKE A DONKEY'S.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-05 HIS NEATLY SHAPED WHITE BODY WAS COVERED WITH REGULAR BARS OF DARK BROWN AND HIS HOOFS WERE DELICATE AS THOSE OF A DEER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-06 GOOD EVENING FRIEND ZEBRA SAID OMBY AMBY IN REPLY TO THE CREATURE'S GREETING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-07 CAN WE DO ANYTHING FOR YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-08 YES ANSWERED THE ZEBRA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-09 I SHOULD LIKE YOU TO SETTLE A DISPUTE THAT HAS LONG BEEN A BOTHER TO ME AS TO WHETHER THERE IS MORE WATER OR LAND IN THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-10 WHO ARE YOU DISPUTING WITH?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-11 ASKED THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-12 WITH A SOFT SHELL CRAB SAID THE ZEBRA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-13 HE LIVES IN A POOL WHERE I GO TO DRINK EVERY DAY AND HE IS A VERY IMPERTINENT CRAB I ASSURE YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-14 I HAVE TOLD HIM MANY TIMES THAT THE LAND IS MUCH GREATER IN EXTENT THAN THE WATER BUT HE WILL NOT BE CONVINCED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-15 EVEN THIS VERY EVENING WHEN I TOLD HIM HE WAS AN INSIGNIFICANT CREATURE WHO LIVED IN A SMALL POOL HE ASSERTED THAT THE WATER WAS GREATER AND MORE IMPORTANT THAN THE LAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-16 SO SEEING YOUR CAMP I DECIDED TO ASK YOU TO SETTLE THE DISPUTE FOR ONCE AND ALL THAT I MAY NOT BE FURTHER ANNOYED BY THIS IGNORANT CRAB.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-17 WHEN THEY HAD LISTENED TO THIS EXPLANATION DOROTHY INQUIRED, WHERE IS THE SOFT SHELL CRAB?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-18 NOT FAR AWAY REPLIED THE ZEBRA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-19 IF YOU WILL AGREE TO JUDGE BETWEEN US I WILL RUN AND GET HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-20 RUN ALONG THEN SAID THE LITTLE GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-21 SO THE ANIMAL PRANCED INTO THE FOREST AND SOON CAME TROTTING BACK TO THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-22 WHEN HE DREW NEAR THEY FOUND A SOFT SHELL CRAB CLINGING FAST TO THE STIFF HAIR OF THE ZEBRA'S HEAD WHERE IT HELD ON BY ONE CLAW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-23 NOW THEN MISTER CRAB SAID THE ZEBRA HERE ARE THE PEOPLE I TOLD YOU ABOUT,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-25 FOR THEY HAVE BEEN TRAVELERS ALL OVER THE WORLD AND KNOW EVERY PART OF IT.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-30 AND I SAID THE WIZARD HAVE BEEN TO EUROPE AND IRELAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-31 SO YOU SEE CONTINUED THE ZEBRA ADDRESSING THE CRAB HERE ARE PEOPLE OF REAL CONSEQUENCE WHO KNOW WHAT THEY ARE TALKING ABOUT.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-44 ALSO THE PINCH OF HIS CLAW IS VERY ANNOYING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-45 SO PRAY TELL HIM THAT THE WORLD CONTAINS MORE LAND THAN WATER AND WHEN HE HAS HEARD YOUR JUDGMENT I WILL CARRY HIM BACK AND DUMP HIM INTO HIS POOL WHERE I HOPE HE WILL BE MORE MODEST IN THE FUTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-46 BUT WE CANNOT TELL HIM THAT SAID DOROTHY GRAVELY BECAUSE IT WOULD NOT BE TRUE.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-54 WHY I CAN RUN FOR DAYS UPON THE LAND AND FIND BUT LITTLE WATER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-59 AND THE JOGGERFYS WILL TELL YOU THAT ALL THE OCEANS PUT TOGETHER ARE BIGGER THAN ALL THE LAND PUT TOGETHER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-64 THE ZEBRA SEEMED MUCH HUMBLED.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-67 THE CRAB BEGAN LAUGHING AGAIN WHICH SO PROVOKED THE ZEBRA THAT HE TRIED TO SHAKE THE LITTLE CREATURE OFF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-68 THIS RESULTED IN MORE EAR PINCHING AND FINALLY DOROTHY TOLD THEM THAT IF THEY COULD NOT BEHAVE THEY MUST GO BACK TO THE FOREST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-69 I'M SORRY I ASKED YOU TO DECIDE THIS QUESTION SAID THE ZEBRA CROSSLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-70 SO LONG AS NEITHER OF US COULD PROVE WE WERE RIGHT WE QUITE ENJOYED THE DISPUTE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-71 BUT NOW I CAN NEVER DRINK AT THAT POOL AGAIN WITHOUT THE SOFT SHELL CRAB LAUGHING AT ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-72 SO I MUST FIND ANOTHER DRINKING PLACE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-73 DO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-74 DO YOU IGNORAMUS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-75 SHOUTED THE CRAB AS LOUDLY AS HIS LITTLE VOICE WOULD CARRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-76 RILE SOME OTHER POOL WITH YOUR CLUMSY HOOFS AND LET YOUR BETTERS ALONE AFTER THIS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-77 THEN THE ZEBRA TROTTED BACK TO THE FOREST BEARING THE CRAB WITH HIM AND DISAPPEARED AMID THE GLOOM OF THE TREES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-78 AND AS IT WAS NOW GETTING DARK THE TRAVELERS SAID GOOD NIGHT TO ONE ANOTHER AND WENT TO BED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-79 DOROTHY AWOKE JUST AS THE LIGHT WAS BEGINNING TO GET STRONG NEXT MORNING AND NOT CARING TO SLEEP ANY LATER SHE QUIETLY GOT OUT OF BED DRESSED HERSELF AND LEFT THE TENT WHERE AUNT EM WAS YET PEACEFULLY SLUMBERING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-80 OUTSIDE SHE NOTICED BILLINA BUSILY PECKING AROUND TO SECURE BUGS OR OTHER FOOD FOR BREAKFAST BUT NONE OF THE MEN IN THE OTHER TENT SEEMED AWAKE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-81 SO THE LITTLE GIRL DECIDED TO TAKE A WALK IN THE WOODS AND TRY TO DISCOVER SOME PATH OR ROAD THAT THEY MIGHT FOLLOW WHEN THEY AGAIN STARTED UPON THEIR JOURNEY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-82 SHE HAD REACHED THE EDGE OF THE FOREST WHEN THE YELLOW HEN CAME FLUTTERING ALONG AND ASKED WHERE SHE WAS GOING.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-87 BILLINA HAD BEEN RATHER SUSPICIOUS OF DOGS AND TOTO HAD HAD AN IDEA THAT IT WAS EVERY DOG'S DUTY TO CHASE A HEN ON SIGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-88 BUT DOROTHY HAD TALKED TO THEM AND SCOLDED THEM FOR NOT BEING AGREEABLE TO ONE ANOTHER UNTIL THEY GREW BETTER ACQUAINTED AND BECAME FRIENDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-89 I WON'T SAY THEY LOVED EACH OTHER DEARLY BUT AT LEAST THEY HAD STOPPED QUARRELING AND NOW MANAGED TO GET ON TOGETHER VERY WELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-90 THE DAY WAS GROWING LIGHTER EVERY MINUTE AND DRIVING THE BLACK SHADOWS OUT OF THE FOREST,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-93 THERE WAS NO PATH HERE EITHER ALTHOUGH SHE ADVANCED QUITE A WAY INTO THE FOREST WINDING HERE AND THERE AMONG THE TREES AND PEERING THROUGH THE BUSHES IN AN ENDEAVOR TO FIND SOME BEATEN TRACK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-94 I THINK WE'D BETTER GO BACK SUGGESTED THE YELLOW HEN AFTER A TIME.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-96 VERY WELL AGREED DOROTHY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-99 SO THE LITTLE GIRL STOPPED SHORT AND LOOKED AROUND HER AND TOTO GLANCED UP INTO HER FACE WITH HIS BRIGHT LITTLE EYES AND WAGGED HIS TAIL AS IF HE KNEW SOMETHING WAS WRONG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-15-100 HE COULDN'T TELL MUCH ABOUT DIRECTION HIMSELF BECAUSE HE HAD SPENT HIS TIME PROWLING AMONG THE BUSHES AND RUNNING HERE AND THERE,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-124 THAT'S THE TROUBLE YOUR MAJESTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-125 SHE HASN'T DONE ANYTHING REPLIED THE CAPTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-126 WHAT DO YOU WANT ME TO DO?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-127 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-128 THIS QUESTION SEEMED TO PUZZLE THEM ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-129 FINALLY A CHAFINGDISH EXCLAIMED IRRITABLY, IF NO ONE CAN THROW ANY LIGHT ON THIS SUBJECT YOU MUST EXCUSE ME IF I GO OUT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-130 AT THIS A BIG KITCHEN FORK PRICKED UP ITS EARS AND SAID IN A TINY VOICE, LET'S HEAR FROM JUDGE SIFTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-131 THAT'S PROPER RETURNED THE KING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-132 SO JUDGE SIFTER TURNED AROUND SLOWLY SEVERAL TIMES AND THEN SAID, WE HAVE NOTHING AGAINST THE GIRL EXCEPT THE STOVE HEARTH UPON WHICH SHE SITS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-133 THEREFORE I ORDER HER INSTANTLY DISCHARGED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-134 DISCHARGED!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-135 CRIED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-136 WHY I NEVER WAS DISCHARGED IN MY LIFE AND I DON'T INTEND TO BE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-137 IF IT'S ALL THE SAME TO YOU I'LL RESIGN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-138 IT'S ALL THE SAME DECLARED THE KING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-139 YOU ARE FREE YOU AND YOUR COMPANIONS AND MAY GO WHEREVER YOU LIKE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-140 THANK YOU SAID THE LITTLE GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-141 BUT HAVEN'T YOU ANYTHING TO EAT IN YOUR KINGDOM?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-142 I'M HUNGRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-143 GO INTO THE WOODS AND PICK BLACKBERRIES ADVISED THE KING LYING DOWN UPON HIS BACK AGAIN AND PREPARING TO GO TO SLEEP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-144 THERE ISN'T A MORSEL TO EAT IN ALL UTENSIA THAT I KNOW OF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-145 SO DOROTHY JUMPED UP AND SAID, COME ON TOTO AND BILLINA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-146 IF WE CAN'T FIND THE CAMP WE MAY FIND SOME BLACKBERRIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-147 THE UTENSILS DREW BACK AND ALLOWED THEM TO PASS WITHOUT PROTEST ALTHOUGH CAPTAIN DIPP MARCHED THE SPOON BRIGADE IN CLOSE ORDER AFTER THEM UNTIL THEY HAD REACHED THE EDGE OF THE CLEARING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-148 THERE THE SPOONS HALTED,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-16-149 BUT DOROTHY AND HER COMPANIONS ENTERED THE FOREST AGAIN AND BEGAN SEARCHING DILIGENTLY FOR A WAY BACK TO THE CAMP THAT THEY MIGHT REJOIN THEIR PARTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-01 CHAPTER SEVENTEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-02 HOW THEY CAME TO BUNBURY WANDERING THROUGH THE WOODS WITHOUT KNOWING WHERE YOU ARE GOING OR WHAT ADVENTURE YOU ARE ABOUT TO MEET NEXT IS NOT AS PLEASANT AS ONE MIGHT THINK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-03 THE WOODS ARE ALWAYS BEAUTIFUL AND IMPRESSIVE AND IF YOU ARE NOT WORRIED OR HUNGRY YOU MAY ENJOY THEM IMMENSELY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-04 BUT DOROTHY WAS WORRIED AND HUNGRY THAT MORNING SO SHE PAID LITTLE ATTENTION TO THE BEAUTIES OF THE FOREST AND HURRIED ALONG AS FAST AS SHE COULD GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-05 SHE TRIED TO KEEP IN ONE DIRECTION AND NOT CIRCLE AROUND BUT SHE WAS NOT AT ALL SURE THAT THE DIRECTION SHE HAD CHOSEN WOULD LEAD HER TO THE CAMP.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-06 BY AND BY TO HER GREAT JOY SHE CAME UPON A PATH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-07 IT RAN TO THE RIGHT AND TO THE LEFT BEING LOST IN THE TREES IN BOTH DIRECTIONS AND JUST BEFORE HER UPON A BIG OAK WERE FASTENED TWO SIGNS WITH ARMS POINTING BOTH WAYS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-08 ONE SIGN READ, TAKE THE OTHER ROAD TO BUNBURY AND THE SECOND SIGN READ, TAKE THE OTHER ROAD TO BUNNYBURY WELL!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-09 BILLINA EYEING THE SIGNS THIS LOOKS AS IF WE WERE GETTING BACK TO CIVILIZATION AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-10 I'M NOT SURE ABOUT THE CIVIL'ZATION DEAR REPLIED THE LITTLE GIRL,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-11 BUT IT LOOKS AS IF WE MIGHT GET SOMEWHERE AND THAT'S A BIG RELIEF ANYHOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-12 WHICH PATH SHALL WE TAKE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-13 INQUIRED THE YELLOW HEN. DOROTHY STARED AT THE SIGNS THOUGHTFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-14 BUNBURY SOUNDS LIKE SOMETHING TO EAT SHE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-15 LET'S GO THERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-16 IT'S ALL THE SAME TO ME REPLIED BILLINA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-17 SHE HAD PICKED UP ENOUGH BUGS AND INSECTS FROM THE MOSS AS SHE WENT ALONG TO SATISFY HER OWN HUNGER BUT THE HEN KNEW DOROTHY COULD NOT EAT BUGS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-18 NOR COULD TOTO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-19 THE PATH TO BUNBURY SEEMED LITTLE TRAVELED BUT IT WAS DISTINCT ENOUGH AND RAN THROUGH THE TREES IN A ZIGZAG COURSE UNTIL IT FINALLY LED THEM TO AN OPEN SPACE FILLED WITH THE QUEEREST HOUSES DOROTHY HAD EVER SEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-20 THEY WERE ALL MADE OF CRACKERS LAID OUT IN TINY SQUARES AND WERE OF MANY PRETTY AND ORNAMENTAL SHAPES HAVING BALCONIES AND PORCHES WITH POSTS OF BREAD STICKS AND ROOFS SHINGLED WITH WAFER CRACKERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-21 THERE WERE WALKS OF BREAD CRUSTS LEADING FROM HOUSE TO HOUSE AND FORMING STREETS AND THE PLACE SEEMED TO HAVE MANY INHABITANTS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-22 WHEN DOROTHY FOLLOWED BY BILLINA AND TOTO ENTERED THE PLACE THEY FOUND PEOPLE WALKING THE STREETS OR ASSEMBLED IN GROUPS TALKING TOGETHER OR SITTING UPON THE PORCHES AND BALCONIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-23 AND WHAT FUNNY PEOPLE THEY WERE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-24 MEN WOMEN AND CHILDREN WERE ALL MADE OF BUNS AND BREAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-25 SOME WERE THIN AND OTHERS FAT,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-26 SOME WERE WHITE SOME LIGHT BROWN AND SOME VERY DARK OF COMPLEXION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-27 A FEW OF THE BUNS WHICH SEEMED TO FORM THE MORE IMPORTANT CLASS OF THE PEOPLE WERE NEATLY FROSTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-28 SOME HAD RAISINS FOR EYES AND CURRANT BUTTONS ON THEIR CLOTHES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-29 OTHERS HAD EYES OF CLOVES AND LEGS OF STICK CINNAMON AND MANY WORE HATS AND BONNETS FROSTED PINK AND GREEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-30 THERE WAS SOMETHING OF A COMMOTION IN BUNBURY WHEN THE STRANGERS SUDDENLY APPEARED AMONG THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-31 WOMEN CAUGHT UP THEIR CHILDREN AND HURRIED INTO THEIR HOUSES SHUTTING THE CRACKER DOORS CAREFULLY BEHIND THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-32 SOME MEN RAN SO HASTILY THAT THEY TUMBLED OVER ONE ANOTHER WHILE OTHERS MORE BRAVE ASSEMBLED IN A GROUP AND FACED THE INTRUDERS DEFIANTLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-33 DOROTHY AT ONCE REALIZED THAT SHE MUST ACT WITH CAUTION IN ORDER NOT TO FRIGHTEN THESE SHY PEOPLE WHO WERE EVIDENTLY UNUSED TO THE PRESENCE OF STRANGERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-34 THERE WAS A DELIGHTFUL FRAGRANT ODOR OF FRESH BREAD IN THE TOWN AND THIS MADE THE LITTLE GIRL MORE HUNGRY THAN EVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-35 SHE TOLD TOTO AND BILLINA TO STAY BACK WHILE SHE SLOWLY ADVANCED TOWARD THE GROUP THAT STOOD SILENTLY AWAITING HER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-36 YOU MUST SCUSE ME FOR COMING UNEXPECTED SHE SAID SOFTLY BUT I REALLY DIDN'T KNOW I WAS COMING HERE UNTIL I ARRIVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-37 I WAS LOST IN THE WOODS YOU KNOW AND I'M AS HUNGRY AS ANYTHING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-38 HUNGRY!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-39 THEY MURMURED IN A HORRIFIED CHORUS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-40 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-41 I HAVEN'T HAD ANYTHING TO EAT SINCE LAST NIGHT'S SUPPER SHE EXCLAIMED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-42 ARE THERE ANY EATABLES IN BUNBURY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-43 THEY LOOKED AT ONE ANOTHER UNDECIDEDLY AND THEN ONE PORTLY BUN MAN WHO SEEMED A PERSON OF CONSEQUENCE STEPPED FORWARD AND SAID, LITTLE GIRL TO BE FRANK WITH YOU WE ARE ALL EATABLES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-44 EVERYTHING IN BUNBURY IS EATABLE TO RAVENOUS HUMAN CREATURES LIKE YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-45 BUT IT IS TO ESCAPE BEING EATEN AND DESTROYED THAT WE HAVE SECLUDED OURSELVES IN THIS OUT OF THE WAY PLACE AND THERE IS NEITHER RIGHT NOR JUSTICE IN YOUR COMING HERE TO FEED UPON US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-46 DOROTHY LOOKED AT HIM LONGINGLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-47 YOU'RE BREAD AREN'T YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-48 ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-49 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-50 BREAD AND BUTTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-51 THE BUTTER IS INSIDE ME SO IT WON'T MELT AND RUN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-52 I DO THE RUNNING MYSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-53 AT THIS JOKE ALL THE OTHERS BURST INTO A CHORUS OF LAUGHTER AND DOROTHY THOUGHT THEY COULDN'T BE MUCH AFRAID IF THEY COULD LAUGH LIKE THAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-54 COULDN'T I EAT SOMETHING BESIDES PEOPLE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-55 SHE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-56 COULDN'T I EAT JUST ONE HOUSE OR A SIDE WALK OR SOMETHING?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-57 I WOULDN'T MIND MUCH WHAT IT WAS YOU KNOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-58 THIS IS NOT A PUBLIC BAKERY CHILD REPLIED THE MAN STERNLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-59 IT'S PRIVATE PROPERTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-60 I KNOW MISTER MISTER MY NAME IS C. BUNN ESQUIRE SAID THE MAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-61 C STANDS FOR CINNAMON AND THIS PLACE IS CALLED AFTER MY FAMILY WHICH IS THE MOST ARISTOCRATIC IN THE TOWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-62 OH I DON'T KNOW ABOUT THAT OBJECTED ANOTHER OF THE QUEER PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-63 THE GRAHAMS AND THE BROWNS AND WHITES ARE ALL EXCELLENT FAMILIES AND THERE IS NONE BETTER OF THEIR KIND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-64 I'M A BOSTON BROWN MYSELF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-65 I ADMIT YOU ARE ALL DESIRABLE CITIZENS SAID MISTER BUNN RATHER STIFFLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-66 BUT THE FACT REMAINS THAT OUR TOWN IS CALLED BUNBURY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-67 SCUSE ME INTERRUPTED DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-68 BUT I'M GETTING HUNGRIER EVERY MINUTE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-69 NOW IF YOU'RE POLITE AND KIND AS I'M SURE YOU OUGHT TO BE YOU'LL LET ME EAT SOMETHING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-70 THERE'S SO MUCH TO EAT HERE THAT YOU WILL NEVER MISS IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-71 THEN A BIG PUFFED UP MAN OF A DELICATE BROWN COLOR STEPPED FORWARD AND SAID, I THINK IT WOULD BE A SHAME TO SEND THIS CHILD AWAY HUNGRY ESPECIALLY AS SHE AGREES TO EAT WHATEVER WE CAN SPARE AND NOT TOUCH OUR PEOPLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-72 SO DO I POP REPLIED A ROLL WHO STOOD NEAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-73 WHAT THEN DO YOU SUGGEST MISTER OVER?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-74 INQUIRED MISTER BUNN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-75 WHY I'LL LET HER EAT MY BACK FENCE IF SHE WANTS TO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-76 IT'S MADE OF WAFFLES AND THEY'RE VERY CRISP AND NICE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-77 SHE MAY ALSO EAT MY WHEELBARROW ADDED A PLEASANT LOOKING MUFFIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-78 IT'S MADE OF NABISCOS WITH A ZUZU WHEEL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-79 VERY GOOD,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-80 VERY GOOD REMARKED MISTER BUNN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-81 THAT IS CERTAINLY VERY KIND OF YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-82 GO WITH POP OVER AND MISTER MUFFIN LITTLE GIRL AND THEY WILL FEED YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-83 THANK YOU VERY MUCH SAID DOROTHY GRATEFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-84 MAY I BRING MY DOG TOTO AND THE YELLOW HEN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-85 THEY'RE HUNGRY TOO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-86 WILL YOU MAKE THEM BEHAVE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-87 ASKED THE MUFFIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-88 OF COURSE PROMISED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-89 THEN COME ALONG SAID POP OVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-90 SO DOROTHY AND BILLINA AND TOTO WALKED UP THE STREET AND THE PEOPLE SEEMED NO LONGER TO BE AT ALL AFRAID OF THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-91 MISTER MUFFIN'S HOUSE CAME FIRST AND AS HIS WHEELBARROW STOOD IN THE FRONT YARD THE LITTLE GIRL ATE THAT FIRST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-92 IT DIDN'T SEEM VERY FRESH BUT SHE WAS SO HUNGRY THAT SHE WAS NOT PARTICULAR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-93 TOTO ATE SOME TOO WHILE BILLINA PICKED UP THE CRUMBS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-94 WHILE THE STRANGERS WERE ENGAGED IN EATING MANY OF THE PEOPLE CAME AND STOOD IN THE STREET CURIOUSLY WATCHING THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-95 DOROTHY NOTICED SIX ROGUISH LOOKING BROWN CHILDREN STANDING ALL IN A ROW AND SHE ASKED, WHO ARE YOU LITTLE ONES?

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-100 YOU MUSN'T SAY SUCH THINGS BILLINA SAID DOROTHY REPROVINGLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-101 NOW LET'S GO INTO POP OVER'S BACK YARD AND GET THE WAFFLES.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-103 THE NEIGHBORS BACK OF US ARE SODA BISCUITS AND I DON'T CARE TO MIX WITH THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-104 BUT I'M HUNGRY YET DECLARED THE GIRL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-105 THAT WHEELBARROW WASN'T VERY BIG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-106 I'VE GOT A SHORTCAKE PIANO BUT NONE OF MY FAMILY CAN PLAY ON IT HE SAID REFLECTIVELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-107 SUPPOSE YOU EAT THAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-108 ALL RIGHT SAID DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-109 I DON'T MIND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-110 ANYTHING TO BE ACCOMMODATING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-111 SO MISTER OVER LED HER INTO THE HOUSE WHERE SHE ATE THE PIANO WHICH WAS OF AN EXCELLENT FLAVOR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-112 IS THERE ANYTHING TO DRINK HERE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-113 SHE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-114 YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-115 I'VE A MILK PUMP AND A WATER PUMP,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-116 WHICH WILL YOU HAVE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-117 HE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-118 I GUESS I'LL TRY EM BOTH SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-119 SO MISTER OVER CALLED TO HIS WIFE WHO BROUGHT INTO THE YARD A PAIL MADE OF SOME KIND OF BAKED DOUGH AND DOROTHY PUMPED THE PAIL FULL OF COOL SWEET MILK AND DRANK IT EAGERLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-120 THE WIFE OF POP OVER WAS SEVERAL SHADES DARKER THAN HER HUSBAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-121 AREN'T YOU OVERDONE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-122 THE LITTLE GIRL ASKED HER.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-126 DOROTHY THANKED THEM FOR THEIR HOSPITALITY AND WENT AWAY.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-129 AND ALL OF US WHO ARE IN GOOD HEALTH ARE WELL BRED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-130 IF YOU ARE NO LONGER HUNGRY WE WILL CALL UPON A FEW OF THE MOST IMPORTANT CITIZENS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-131 TOTO AND BILLINA FOLLOWED BEHIND THEM BEHAVING VERY WELL AND A LITTLE WAY DOWN THE STREET THEY CAME TO A HANDSOME RESIDENCE WHERE AUNT SALLY LUNN LIVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-132 THE OLD LADY WAS GLAD TO MEET THE LITTLE GIRL AND GAVE HER A SLICE OF WHITE BREAD AND BUTTER WHICH HAD BEEN USED AS A DOOR MAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-133 IT WAS ALMOST FRESH AND TASTED BETTER THAN ANYTHING DOROTHY HAD EATEN IN THE TOWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-134 WHERE DO YOU GET THE BUTTER?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-135 SHE INQUIRED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-136 WE DIG IT OUT OF THE GROUND WHICH AS YOU MAY HAVE OBSERVED IS ALL FLOUR AND MEAL REPLIED MISTER BUNN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-137 THERE IS A BUTTER MINE JUST AT THE OPPOSITE SIDE OF THE VILLAGE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-138 THE TREES WHICH YOU SEE HERE ARE ALL DOUGHLEANDERS AND DOUGHDERAS AND IN THE SEASON WE GET QUITE A CROP OF DOUGH NUTS OFF THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-139 I SHOULD THINK THE FLOUR WOULD BLOW AROUND AND GET INTO YOUR EYES SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-140 NO SAID HE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-141 WE ARE BOTHERED WITH CRACKER DUST SOMETIMES BUT NEVER WITH FLOUR.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-142 THEN HE TOOK HER TO SEE JOHNNY CAKE A CHEERFUL OLD GENTLEMAN WHO LIVED NEAR BY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-143 I SUPPOSE YOU'VE HEARD OF ME SAID OLD JOHNNY WITH AN AIR OF PRIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-144 I'M A GREAT FAVORITE ALL OVER THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-145 AREN'T YOU RATHER YELLOW?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-146 ASKED DOROTHY LOOKING AT HIM CRITICALLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-147 MAYBE CHILD.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-149 IF ANYTHING AILED ME I'D WILLINGLY ACKNOWLEDGE THE CORN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-150 JOHNNY'S A TRIFLE STALE SAID MISTER BUNN AS THEY WENT AWAY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-151 BUT HE'S A GOOD MIXER AND NEVER GETS CROSS GRAINED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-152 I WILL NOW TAKE YOU TO CALL UPON SOME OF MY OWN RELATIVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-153 THEY VISITED THE SUGAR BUNNS THE CURRANT BUNNS AND THE SPANISH BUNNS THE LATTER HAVING A DECIDEDLY FOREIGN APPEARANCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-154 THEN THEY SAW THE FRENCH ROLLS WHO WERE VERY POLITE TO THEM AND MADE A BRIEF CALL UPON THE PARKER H. ROLLS WHO SEEMED A BIT PROUD AND OVERBEARING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-155 BUT THEY'RE NOT AS STUCK UP AS THE FROSTED JUMBLES DECLARED MISTER BUNN WHO ARE PEOPLE I REALLY CAN'T ABIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-156 I DON'T LIKE TO BE SUSPICIOUS OR TALK SCANDAL BUT SOMETIMES I THINK THE JUMBLES HAVE TOO MUCH BAKING POWDER IN THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-157 JUST THEN A DREADFUL SCREAM WAS HEARD AND DOROTHY TURNED HASTILY AROUND TO FIND A SCENE OF GREAT EXCITEMENT A LITTLE WAY DOWN THE STREET.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-158 THE PEOPLE WERE CROWDING AROUND TOTO AND THROWING AT HIM EVERYTHING THEY COULD FIND AT HAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-159 THEY PELTED THE LITTLE DOG WITH HARD TACK CRACKERS AND EVEN ARTICLES OF FURNITURE WHICH WERE HARD BAKED AND HEAVY ENOUGH FOR MISSILES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-160 TOTO HOWELED A LITTLE AS THE ASSORTMENT OF BAKE STUFF STRUCK HIM,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-161 BUT HE STOOD STILL WITH HEAD BOWED AND TAIL BETWEEN HIS LEGS UNTIL DOROTHY RAN UP AND INQUIRED WHAT THE MATTER WAS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-162 MATTER!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-163 CRIED A RYE LOAFER INDIGNANTLY WHY THE HORRID BEAST HAS EATEN THREE OF OUR DEAR CRUMPETS AND IS NOW DEVOURING A SALT RISING BISCUIT!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-164 OH TOTO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-165 HOW COULD YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-166 EXCLAIMED DOROTHY MUCH DISTRESSED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-167 TOTO'S MOUTH WAS FULL OF HIS SALT RISING VICTIM,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-168 SO HE ONLY WHINED AND WAGGED HIS TAIL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-169 BUT BILLINA WHO HAD FLOWN TO THE TOP OF A CRACKER HOUSE TO BE IN A SAFE PLACE CALLED OUT, DON'T BLAME HIM DOROTHY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-170 THE CRUMPETS DARED HIM TO DO IT.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-174 MISTER CINNAMON BUNN WHO HAD NOW JOINED THEM.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-183 DOROTHY GAZED AROUND AND SAW THREATENING LOOKS UPON THE FACES OF ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-184 SHE HAD NOT NOTICED ANY OVENS IN THE TOWN BUT THEY MIGHT BE THERE NEVERTHELESS FOR SOME OF THE INHABITANTS SEEMED VERY FRESH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-17-185 SO SHE DECIDED TO GO AND CALLING TO TOTO AND BILLINA TO FOLLOW HER SHE MARCHED UP THE STREET WITH AS MUCH DIGNITY AS POSSIBLE CONSIDERING THAT SHE WAS FOLLOWED BY THE HOOTS AND CRIES OF THE BUNS AND BISCUITS AND OTHER BAKE STUFF.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-01 CHAPTER EIGHTEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-02 HOW OZMA LOOKED INTO THE MAGIC PICTURE PRINCESS OZMA WAS A VERY BUSY LITTLE RULER FOR SHE LOOKED CAREFULLY AFTER THE COMFORT AND WELFARE OF HER PEOPLE AND TRIED TO MAKE THEM HAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-03 IF ANY QUARRELS AROSE SHE DECIDED THEM JUSTLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-04 IF ANY ONE NEEDED COUNSEL OR ADVICE SHE WAS READY AND WILLING TO LISTEN TO THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-05 FOR A DAY OR TWO AFTER DOROTHY AND HER COMPANIONS HAD STARTED ON THEIR TRIP OZMA WAS OCCUPIED WITH THE AFFAIRS OF HER KINGDOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-06 THEN SHE BEGAN TO THINK OF SOME MANNER OF OCCUPATION FOR UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM THAT WOULD BE LIGHT AND EASY AND YET GIVE THE OLD PEOPLE SOMETHING TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-07 SHE SOON DECIDED TO MAKE UNCLE HENRY THE KEEPER OF THE JEWELS FOR SOME ONE REALLY WAS NEEDED TO COUNT AND LOOK AFTER THE BINS AND BARRELS OF EMERALDS DIAMONDS RUBIES AND OTHER PRECIOUS STONES THAT WERE IN THE ROYAL STOREHOUSES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-08 THAT WOULD KEEP UNCLE HENRY BUSY ENOUGH BUT IT WAS HARDER TO FIND SOMETHING FOR AUNT EM TO DO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-09 THE PALACE WAS FULL OF SERVANTS SO THERE WAS NO DETAIL OF HOUSEWORK THAT AUNT EM COULD LOOK AFTER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-10 WHILE OZMA SAT IN HER PRETTY ROOM ENGAGED IN THOUGHT SHE HAPPENED TO GLANCE AT HER MAGIC PICTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-11 THIS WAS ONE OF THE MOST IMPORTANT TREASURES IN ALL THE LAND OF OZ. IT WAS A LARGE PICTURE SET IN A BEAUTIFUL GOLD FRAME AND IT HUNG IN A PROMINENT PLACE UPON A WALL OF OZMA'S PRIVATE ROOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-12 USUALLY THIS PICTURE SEEMED MERELY A COUNTRY SCENE BUT WHENEVER OZMA LOOKED AT IT AND WISHED TO KNOW WHAT ANY OF HER FRIENDS OR ACQUAINTANCES WERE DOING THE MAGIC OF THIS WONDERFUL PICTURE WAS STRAIGHTWAY DISCLOSED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-13 FOR THE COUNTRY SCENE WOULD GRADUALLY FADE AWAY AND IN ITS PLACE WOULD APPEAR THE LIKENESS OF THE PERSON OR PERSONS OZMA MIGHT WISH TO SEE SURROUNDED BY THE ACTUAL SCENES IN WHICH THEY WERE THEN PLACED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-14 IN THIS WAY THE PRINCESS COULD VIEW ANY PART OF THE WORLD SHE WISHED AND WATCH THE ACTIONS OF ANY ONE IN WHOM SHE WAS INTERESTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-15 OZMA HAD OFTEN SEEN DOROTHY IN HER KANSAS HOME BY THIS MEANS AND NOW HAVING A LITTLE LEISURE SHE EXPRESSED A DESIRE TO SEE HER LITTLE FRIEND AGAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-16 IT WAS WHILE THE TRAVELERS WERE AT FUDDLECUMJIG AND OZMA LAUGHED MERRILY AS SHE WATCHED IN THE PICTURE HER FRIENDS TRYING TO MATCH THE PIECES OF GRANDMOTHER GNIT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-17 THEY SEEM HAPPY AND ARE DOUBTLESS HAVING A GOOD TIME THE GIRL RULER SAID TO HERSELF,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-18 AND THEN SHE BEGAN TO THINK OF THE MANY ADVENTURES SHE HERSELF HAD ENCOUNTERED WITH DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-19 THE IMAGE OF HER FRIENDS NOW FADED FROM THE MAGIC PICTURE AND THE OLD LANDSCAPE SLOWLY REAPPEARED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-20 OZMA WAS THINKING OF THE TIME WHEN WITH DOROTHY AND HER ARMY SHE MARCHED TO THE NOME KING'S UNDERGROUND CAVERN BEYOND THE LAND OF EV AND FORCED THE OLD MONARCH TO LIBERATE HIS CAPTIVES WHO BELONGED TO THE ROYAL FAMILY OF EV. THAT WAS THE TIME WHEN THE SCARECROW NEARLY FRIGHTENED THE NOME KING INTO FITS BY THROWING ONE OF BILLINA'S EGGS AT HIM AND DOROTHY HAD CAPTURED KING ROQUAT'S MAGIC BELT AND BROUGHT IT AWAY WITH HER TO THE LAND OF OZ. THE PRETTY PRINCESS SMILED AT THE RECOLLECTION OF THIS ADVENTURE AND THEN SHE WONDERED WHAT HAD BECOME OF THE NOME KING SINCE THEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-21 MERELY BECAUSE SHE WAS CURIOUS AND HAD NOTHING BETTER TO DO OZMA GLANCED AT THE MAGIC PICTURE AND WISHED TO SEE IN IT THE KING OF THE NOMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-22 ROQUAT THE RED WENT EVERY DAY INTO HIS TUNNEL TO SEE HOW THE WORK WAS GETTING ALONG AND TO HURRY HIS WORKMEN AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-23 HE WAS THERE NOW AND OZMA SAW HIM PLAINLY IN THE MAGIC PICTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-24 SHE SAW THE UNDERGROUND TUNNEL REACHING FAR UNDERNEATH THE DEADLY DESERT WHICH SEPARATED THE LAND OF OZ FROM THE MOUNTAINS BENEATH WHICH THE NOME KING HAD HIS EXTENSIVE CAVERNS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-25 SHE SAW THAT THE TUNNEL WAS BEING MADE IN THE DIRECTION OF THE EMERALD CITY AND KNEW AT ONCE IT WAS BEING DUG SO THAT THE ARMY OF NOMES COULD MARCH THROUGH IT AND ATTACK HER OWN BEAUTIFUL AND PEACEFUL COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-26 I SUPPOSE KING ROQUAT IS PLANNING REVENGE AGAINST US SHE SAID MUSINGLY AND THINKS HE CAN SURPRISE US AND MAKE US HIS CAPTIVES AND SLAVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-27 HOW SAD IT IS THAT ANY ONE CAN HAVE SUCH WICKED THOUGHTS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-28 BUT I MUST NOT BLAME KING ROQUAT TOO SEVERELY FOR HE IS A NOME AND HIS NATURE IS NOT SO GENTLE AS MY OWN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-29 THEN SHE DISMISSED FROM HER MIND FURTHER THOUGHT OF THE TUNNEL FOR THAT TIME AND BEGAN TO WONDER IF AUNT EM WOULD NOT BE HAPPY AS ROYAL MENDER OF THE STOCKINGS OF THE RULER OF OZ. OZMA WORE FEW HOLES IN HER STOCKINGS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-30 STILL THEY SOMETIMES NEEDED MENDING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-31 AUNT EM OUGHT TO BE ABLE TO DO THAT VERY NICELY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-32 NEXT DAY THE PRINCESS WATCHED THE TUNNEL AGAIN IN HER MAGIC PICTURE AND EVERY DAY AFTERWARD SHE DEVOTED A FEW MINUTES TO INSPECTING THE WORK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-33 IT WAS NOT ESPECIALLY INTERESTING BUT SHE FELT THAT IT WAS HER DUTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-18-34 SLOWLY BUT SURELY THE BIG ARCHED HOLE CREPT THROUGH THE ROCKS UNDERNEATH THE DEADLY DESERT AND DAY BY DAY IT DREW NEARER AND NEARER TO THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-01 CHAPTER NINETEEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-02 HOW BUNNYBURY WELCOMED THE STRANGERS DOROTHY LEFT BUNBURY THE SAME WAY SHE HAD ENTERED IT AND WHEN THEY WERE IN THE FOREST AGAIN SHE SAID TO BILLINA, I NEVER THOUGHT THAT THINGS GOOD TO EAT COULD BE SO DIS'GREE'BLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-03 OFTEN I'VE EATEN THINGS THAT TASTED GOOD BUT WERE DISAGREEABLE AFTERWARD RETURNED THE YELLOW HEN. I THINK DOROTHY IF EATABLES ARE GOING TO ACT BADLY IT'S BETTER BEFORE THAN AFTER YOU EAT THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-04 P'RAPS YOU'RE RIGHT SAID THE LITTLE GIRL WITH A SIGH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-05 BUT WHAT SHALL WE DO NOW?

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-11 STILL IT WAS A GUIDE AND THE WALKING THROUGH THE FOREST WAS NOT AT ALL DIFFICULT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-12 BEFORE LONG THEY REACHED A HIGH WALL OF SOLID WHITE MARBLE AND THE PATH CAME TO AN END AT THIS WALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-13 AT FIRST DOROTHY THOUGHT THERE WAS NO OPENING AT ALL IN THE MARBLE BUT ON LOOKING CLOSELY SHE DISCOVERED A SMALL SQUARE DOOR ABOUT ON A LEVEL WITH HER HEAD AND UNDERNEATH THIS CLOSED DOOR WAS A BELL PUSH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-14 NEAR THE BELL PUSH A SIGN WAS PAINTED IN NEAT LETTERS UPON THE MARBLE AND THE SIGN READ, NO ADMITTANCE EXCEPT ON BUSINESS THIS DID NOT DISCOURAGE DOROTHY HOWEVER AND SHE RANG THE BELL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-15 PRETTY SOON A BOLT WAS CAUTIOUSLY WITHDRAWN AND THE MARBLE DOOR SWUNG SLOWLY OPEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-16 THEN SHE SAW IT WAS NOT REALLY A DOOR BUT A WINDOW FOR SEVERAL BRASS BARS WERE PLACED ACROSS IT BEING SET FAST IN THE MARBLE AND SO CLOSE TOGETHER THAT THE LITTLE GIRL'S FINGERS MIGHT BARELY GO BETWEEN THEM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-17 BACK OF THE BARS APPEARED THE FACE OF A WHITE RABBIT A VERY SOBER AND SEDATE FACE WITH AN EYE GLASS HELD IN HIS LEFT EYE AND ATTACHED TO A CORD IN HIS BUTTON HOLE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-18 WELL!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-19 WHAT IS IT?

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-22 MY BUSINESS SHE REPLIED IS TO FIND OUT WHERE I AM AND TO NO ONE IS ALLOWED IN BUNNYBURY WITHOUT AN ORDER OR A LETTER OF INTRODUCTION FROM EITHER OZMA OF OZ OR GLINDA THE GOOD ANNOUNCED THE RABBIT,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-52 HERE STOOD THE RABBIT SHE HAD BEEN TALKING WITH AND NOW THAT SHE COULD SEE ALL OF HIM SHE GAZED AT THE CREATURE IN SURPRISE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-53 HE WAS A GOOD SIZED WHITE RABBIT WITH PINK EYES MUCH LIKE ALL OTHER WHITE RABBITS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-54 BUT THE ASTONISHING THING ABOUT HIM WAS THE MANNER IN WHICH HE WAS DRESSED.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-56 HIS VEST WAS ROSE COLORED SATIN WITH TOURMALINE BUTTONS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-58 HIS SHOES WERE OF WHITE PLUSH WITH DIAMOND BUCKLES AND HIS STOCKINGS WERE ROSE SILK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-59 THE RICHNESS AND EVEN MAGNIFICENCE OF THE RABBIT'S CLOTHING MADE DOROTHY STARE AT THE LITTLE CREATURE WONDERINGLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-60 TOTO AND BILLINA HAD FOLLOWED HER INTO THE ROOM AND WHEN HE SAW THEM THE RABBIT RAN TO A TABLE AND SPRANG UPON IT NIMBLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-61 THEN HE LOOKED AT THE THREE THROUGH HIS MONOCLE AND SAID, THESE COMPANIONS PRINCESS CANNOT ENTER BUNNYBURY WITH YOU.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-63 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-64 IN THE FIRST PLACE THEY WOULD FRIGHTEN OUR PEOPLE WHO DISLIKE DOGS ABOVE ALL THINGS ON EARTH,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-66 BUT THEY'RE MY FRIENDS PERSISTED DOROTHY AND GO WHEREVER I GO.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-74 SHE HAD NOT FORGOTTEN HOW TOTO AND BILLINA HAD MISBEHAVED IN BUNBURY AND PERHAPS THE RABBIT WAS WISE TO INSIST ON THEIR STAYING OUTSIDE THE TOWN.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-80 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-81 YOUR SIZE.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-85 NO,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-88 ASKED THE GIRL.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-92 ALL RIGHT THEN,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-93 I'M WILLING SHE ANNOUNCED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-94 THE RABBIT JUMPED FROM THE TABLE AND RAN OR RATHER HOPPED TO THE FURTHER WALL WHERE HE OPENED A DOOR SO TINY THAT EVEN TOTO COULD SCARCELY HAVE CRAWLED THROUGH IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-95 FOLLOW ME HE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-96 NOW ALMOST ANY OTHER LITTLE GIRL WOULD HAVE DECLARED THAT SHE COULD NOT GET THROUGH SO SMALL A DOOR,

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-101 THE HIGH MARBLE WALL EXTENDED ALL AROUND THE PLACE AND SHUT OUT ALL THE REST OF THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-102 AND HERE WERE MARBLE HOUSES OF CURIOUS FORMS MOST OF THEM RESEMBLING OVERTURNED KETTLES BUT WITH DELICATE SLENDER SPIRES AND MINARETS RUNNING FAR UP INTO THE SKY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-103 THE STREETS WERE PAVED WITH WHITE MARBLE AND IN FRONT OF EACH HOUSE WAS A LAWN OF RICH GREEN CLOVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-104 EVERYTHING WAS AS NEAT AS WAX THE GREEN AND WHITE CONTRASTING PRETTILY TOGETHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-105 BUT THE RABBIT PEOPLE WERE AFTER ALL THE MOST AMAZING THINGS DOROTHY SAW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-106 THE STREETS WERE FULL OF THEM AND THEIR COSTUMES WERE SO SPLENDID THAT THE RICH DRESS OF THE KEEPER OF THE WICKET WAS COMMONPLACE WHEN COMPARED WITH THE OTHERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-107 SILKS AND SATINS OF DELICATE HUES SEEMED ALWAYS USED FOR MATERIAL AND NEARLY EVERY COSTUME SPARKLED WITH EXQUISITE GEMS.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-109 THEY WORE BONNETS TOO WITH FEATHERS AND JEWELS IN THEM AND SOME WHEELED BABY CARRIAGES IN WHICH THE GIRL COULD SEE WEE BUNNIES.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-111 AS DOROTHY WAS NO BIGGER IN SIZE THAN THE GROWN UP RABBITS SHE HAD A CHANCE TO OBSERVE THEM CLOSELY BEFORE THEY NOTICED HER PRESENCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-112 THEN THEY DID NOT SEEM AT ALL ALARMED ALTHOUGH THE LITTLE GIRL NATURALLY BECAME THE CENTER OF ATTRACTION AND REGARDED HER WITH GREAT CURIOSITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-113 MAKE WAY!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-19-114 CRIED THE KEEPER OF THE WICKET IN A POMPOUS VOICE,

HE FEELS THAT HE CANNOT BE HAPPY WITHOUT A FARM OF HIS OWN SO OZMA GAVE HIM SOME LAND AND EVERY ONE HELPED HIM BUILD HIS MANSION AND NOW HE IS SETTLED THERE FOR GOOD.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-62 SOME OF THE CHAIRS WERE MADE IN THE SHAPE OF BIG CROWS AND UPHOLSTERED WITH CUSHIONS OF CORN COLORED SILK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-63 THE SECOND STORY CONTAINED A FINE BANQUET ROOM WHERE THE SCARECROW MIGHT ENTERTAIN HIS GUESTS AND THE THREE STORIES ABOVE THAT WERE BED CHAMBERS EXQUISITELY FURNISHED AND DECORATED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-64 FROM THESE ROOMS SAID THE SCARECROW PROUDLY ONE MAY OBTAIN FINE VIEWS OF THE SURROUNDING CORNFIELDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-65 THE CORN I GROW IS ALWAYS HUSKY AND I CALL THE EARS MY REGIMENTS BECAUSE THEY HAVE SO MANY KERNELS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-66 OF COURSE I CANNOT RIDE MY COBS BUT I REALLY DON'T CARE SHUCKS ABOUT THAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-67 TAKEN ALTOGETHER MY FARM WILL STACK UP WITH ANY IN THE NEIGHBORHOOD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-68 THE VISITORS PARTOOK OF SOME LIGHT REFRESHMENT AND THEN HURRIED AWAY TO RESUME THE ROAD TO THE EMERALD CITY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-69 THE SCARECROW FOUND A SEAT IN THE WAGON BETWEEN OMBY AMBY AND THE SHAGGY MAN AND HIS WEIGHT DID NOT ADD MUCH TO THE LOAD BECAUSE HE WAS STUFFED WITH STRAW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-70 YOU WILL NOTICE I HAVE ONE OAT FIELD ON MY PROPERTY HE REMARKED AS THEY DROVE AWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-71 OAT STRAW IS I HAVE FOUND THE BEST OF ALL STRAWS TO RE STUFF MYSELF WITH WHEN MY INTERIOR GETS MUSTY OR OUT OF SHAPE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-72 ARE YOU ABLE TO RE STUFF YOURSELF WITHOUT HELP?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-73 ASKED AUNT EM. I SHOULD THINK THAT AFTER THE STRAW WAS TAKEN OUT OF YOU THERE WOULDN'T BE ANYTHING LEFT BUT YOUR CLOTHES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-74 YOU ARE ALMOST CORRECT MADAM HE ANSWERED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-75 MY SERVANTS DO THE STUFFING UNDER MY DIRECTION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-76 FOR MY HEAD IN WHICH ARE MY EXCELLENT BRAINS IS A BAG TIED AT THE BOTTOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-77 MY FACE IS NEATLY PAINTED UPON ONE SIDE OF THE BAG AS YOU MAY SEE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-78 MY HEAD DOES NOT NEED RE STUFFING AS MY BODY DOES FOR ALL THAT IT REQUIRES IS TO HAVE THE FACE TOUCHED UP WITH FRESH PAINT OCCASIONALLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-79 IT WAS NOT FAR FROM THE SCARECROW'S MANSION TO THE FARM OF JACK PUMPKINHEAD AND WHEN THEY ARRIVED THERE BOTH UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM WERE MUCH IMPRESSED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-80 THE FARM WAS ONE VAST PUMPKIN FIELD AND SOME OF THE PUMPKINS WERE OF ENORMOUS SIZE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-81 IN ONE OF THEM WHICH HAD BEEN NEATLY HOLLOWED OUT JACK HIMSELF LIVED AND HE DECLARED THAT IT WAS A VERY COMFORTABLE RESIDENCE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-82 THE REASON HE GREW SO MANY PUMPKINS WAS IN ORDER THAT HE MIGHT CHANGE HIS HEAD AS OFTEN AS IT BECAME WRINKLED OR THREATENED TO SPOIL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-83 THE PUMPKIN HEADED MAN WELCOMED HIS VISITORS JOYFULLY AND OFFERED THEM SEVERAL DELICIOUS PUMPKIN PIES TO EAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-84 I DON'T INDULGE IN PUMPKIN PIES MYSELF FOR TWO REASONS HE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-85 ONE REASON IS THAT WERE I TO EAT PUMPKINS I WOULD BECOME A CANNIBAL AND THE OTHER REASON IS THAT I NEVER EAT NOT BEING HOLLOW INSIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-86 VERY GOOD REASONS AGREED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-87 THEY TOLD JACK PUMPKINHEAD OF THE DREADFUL NEWS ABOUT THE NOME KING AND HE DECIDED TO GO WITH THEM TO THE EMERALD CITY AND HELP COMFORT OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-88 I HAD EXPECTED TO LIVE HERE IN EASE AND COMFORT FOR MANY CENTURIES SAID JACK DOLEFULLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-89 BUT OF COURSE IF THE NOME KING DESTROYS EVERYTHING IN OZ I SHALL BE DESTROYED TOO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-90 REALLY IT SEEMS TOO BAD DOESN'T IT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-25-91 THEY WERE SOON ON THEIR JOURNEY AGAIN AND SO SWIFTLY DID THE SAWHORSE DRAW THE WAGON OVER THE SMOOTH ROADS THAT BEFORE TWILIGHT FELL THEY HAD REACHED THE ROYAL PALACE IN THE EMERALD CITY AND WERE AT THEIR JOURNEY'S END.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-01 CHAPTER TWENTY SIX.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-02 HOW OZMA REFUSED TO FIGHT FOR HER KINGDOM OZMA WAS IN HER ROSE GARDEN PICKING A BOUQUET WHEN THE PARTY ARRIVED AND SHE GREETED ALL HER OLD AND NEW FRIENDS AS SMILINGLY AND SWEETLY AS EVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-03 DOROTHY'S EYES WERE FULL OF TEARS AS SHE KISSED THE LOVELY RULER OF OZ AND SHE WHISPERED TO HER, OH OZMA OZMA!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-04 I'M SO SORRY!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-05 OZMA SEEMED SURPRISED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-06 SORRY FOR WHAT DOROTHY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-07 SHE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-08 FOR ALL YOUR TROUBLE ABOUT THE NOME KING WAS THE REPLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-09 OZMA LAUGHED WITH GENUINE AMUSEMENT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-10 WHY THAT HAS NOT TROUBLED ME A BIT DEAR PRINCESS SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-11 THEN LOOKING AROUND AT THE SAD FACES OF HER FRIENDS SHE ADDED, HAVE YOU ALL BEEN WORRYING ABOUT THIS TUNNEL?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-12 WE HAVE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-13 THEY EXCLAIMED IN A CHORUS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-14 WELL PERHAPS IT IS MORE SERIOUS THAN I IMAGINED ADMITTED THE FAIR RULER,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-15 BUT I HAVEN'T GIVEN THE MATTER MUCH THOUGHT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-16 AFTER DINNER WE WILL ALL MEET TOGETHER AND TALK IT OVER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-17 SO THEY WENT TO THEIR ROOMS AND PREPARED FOR DINNER AND DOROTHY DRESSED HERSELF IN HER PRETTIEST GOWN AND PUT ON HER CORONET FOR SHE THOUGHT THAT THIS MIGHT BE THE LAST TIME SHE WOULD EVER APPEAR AS A PRINCESS OF OZ. THE SCARECROW THE TIN WOODMAN AND JACK PUMPKINHEAD ALL SAT AT THE DINNER TABLE ALTHOUGH NONE OF THEM WAS MADE SO HE COULD EAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-18 USUALLY THEY SERVED TO ENLIVEN THE MEAL WITH THEIR MERRY TALK BUT TO NIGHT ALL SEEMED STRANGELY SILENT AND UNEASY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-19 AS SOON AS THE DINNER WAS FINISHED OZMA LED THE COMPANY TO HER OWN PRIVATE ROOM IN WHICH HUNG THE MAGIC PICTURE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-20 WHEN THEY HAD SEATED THEMSELVES THE SCARECROW WAS THE FIRST TO SPEAK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-21 IS THE NOME KING'S TUNNEL FINISHED OZMA?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-22 HE ASKED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-23 IT WAS COMPLETED TO DAY SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-24 THEY HAVE BUILT IT RIGHT UNDER MY PALACE GROUNDS AND IT ENDS IN FRONT OF THE FORBIDDEN FOUNTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-25 NOTHING BUT A CRUST OF EARTH REMAINS TO SEPARATE OUR ENEMIES FROM US AND WHEN THEY MARCH HERE THEY WILL EASILY BREAK THROUGH THIS CRUST AND RUSH UPON US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-26 WHO WILL ASSIST THE NOME KING?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-27 INQUIRED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-28 THE WHIMSIES THE GROWLEYWOGS AND THE PHANFASMS SHE REPLIED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-29 I WATCHED TO DAY IN MY MAGIC PICTURE THE MESSENGERS WHOM THE NOME KING SENT TO ALL THESE PEOPLE TO SUMMON THEM TO ASSEMBLE IN HIS GREAT CAVERNS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-30 LET US SEE WHAT THEY ARE DOING NOW SUGGESTED THE TIN WOODMAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-31 SO OZMA WISHED TO SEE THE NOME KING'S CAVERN AND AT ONCE THE LANDSCAPE FADED FROM THE MAGIC PICTURE AND WAS REPLACED BY THE SCENE THEN BEING ENACTED IN THE JEWELED CAVERN OF KING ROQUAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-32 A WILD AND STARTLING SCENE IT WAS WHICH THE OZ PEOPLE BEHELD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-33 BEFORE THE NOME KING STOOD THE CHIEF OF THE WHIMSIES AND THE GRAND GALLIPOOT OF THE GROWLEYWOGS SURROUNDED BY THEIR MOST SKILLFUL GENERALS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-34 VERY FIERCE AND POWERFUL THEY LOOKED SO THAT EVEN THE NOME KING AND GENERAL GUPH WHO STOOD BESIDE HIS MASTER SEEMED A BIT FEARFUL IN THE PRESENCE OF THEIR ALLIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-35 NOW A STILL MORE FORMIDABLE CREATURE ENTERED THE CAVERN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-36 IT WAS THE FIRST AND FOREMOST OF THE PHANFASMS AND HE PROUDLY SAT DOWN IN KING ROQUAT'S OWN THRONE AND DEMANDED THE RIGHT TO LEAD HIS FORCES THROUGH THE TUNNEL IN ADVANCE OF ALL THE OTHERS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-37 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST NOW APPEARED TO ALL EYES IN HIS HAIRY SKIN AND THE BEAR'S HEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-38 WHAT HIS REAL FORM WAS EVEN ROQUAT DID NOT KNOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-39 THROUGH THE ARCHES LEADING INTO THE VAST SERIES OF CAVERNS THAT LAY BEYOND THE THRONE ROOM OF KING ROQUAT COULD BE SEEN RANKS UPON RANKS OF THE INVADERS THOUSANDS OF PHANFASMS GROWLEYWOGS AND WHIMSIES STANDING IN SERRIED LINES WHILE BEHIND THEM WERE MASSED THE THOUSANDS UPON THOUSANDS OF GENERAL GUPH'S OWN ARMY OF NOMES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-40 LISTEN!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-41 WHISPERED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-42 I THINK WE CAN HEAR WHAT THEY ARE SAYING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-43 SO THEY KEPT STILL AND LISTENED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-44 IS ALL READY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-45 DEMANDED THE FIRST AND FOREMOST HAUGHTILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-46 THE TUNNEL IS FINALLY COMPLETED REPLIED GENERAL GUPH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-47 HOW LONG WILL IT TAKE US TO MARCH TO THE EMERALD CITY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-48 ASKED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT OF THE GROWLEYWOGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-49 IF WE START AT MIDNIGHT REPLIED THE NOME KING WE SHALL ARRIVE AT THE EMERALD CITY BY DAYBREAK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-50 THEN WHILE ALL THE OZ PEOPLE ARE SLEEPING WE WILL CAPTURE THEM AND MAKE THEM OUR SLAVES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-51 AFTER THAT WE WILL DESTROY THE CITY ITSELF AND MARCH THROUGH THE LAND OF OZ BURNING AND DEVASTATING AS WE GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-52 GOOD!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-53 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-54 WHEN WE GET THROUGH WITH OZ IT WILL BE A DESERT WILDERNESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-55 OZMA SHALL BE MY SLAVE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-56 SHE SHALL BE MY SLAVE!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-57 SHOUTED THE GRAND GALLIPOOT ANGRILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-58 WE'LL DECIDE THAT BY AND BY SAID KING ROQUAT HASTILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-59 DON'T LET US QUARREL NOW FRIENDS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-60 FIRST LET US CONQUER OZ AND THEN WE WILL DIVIDE THE SPOILS OF WAR IN A SATISFACTORY MANNER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-61 THE FIRST AND FOREMOST SMILED WICKEDLY,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-62 BUT HE ONLY SAID, I AND MY PHANFASMS GO FIRST FOR NOTHING ON EARTH CAN OPPOSE OUR POWER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-63 THEY ALL AGREED TO THAT KNOWING THE PHANFASMS TO BE THE MIGHTIEST OF THE COMBINED FORCES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-64 KING ROQUAT NOW INVITED THEM TO ATTEND A BANQUET HE HAD PREPARED WHERE THEY MIGHT OCCUPY THEMSELVES IN EATING AND DRINKING UNTIL MIDNIGHT ARRIVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-65 AS THEY HAD NOW SEEN AND HEARD ALL OF THE PLOT AGAINST THEM THAT THEY CARED TO OZMA ALLOWED HER MAGIC PICTURE TO FADE AWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-66 THEN SHE TURNED TO HER FRIENDS AND SAID, OUR ENEMIES WILL BE HERE SOONER THAN I EXPECTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-67 WHAT DO YOU ADVISE ME TO DO?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-68 IF YOU HAD ALLOWED ME TO ARM AND DRILL MY WINKIES WE MIGHT HAVE PUT UP A GOOD FIGHT AND DESTROYED MANY OF OUR ENEMIES BEFORE WE WERE CONQUERED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-69 AND SO ARE THE GILLIKINS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-70 BUT I DO NOT WISH TO FIGHT DECLARED OZMA FIRMLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-71 NO ONE HAS THE RIGHT TO DESTROY ANY LIVING CREATURES HOWEVER EVIL THEY MAY BE OR TO HURT THEM OR MAKE THEM UNHAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-72 I WILL NOT FIGHT EVEN TO SAVE MY KINGDOM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-73 THE NOME KING IS NOT SO PARTICULAR REMARKED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-74 HE INTENDS TO DESTROY US ALL AND RUIN OUR BEAUTIFUL COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-75 BECAUSE THE NOME KING INTENDS TO DO EVIL IS NO EXCUSE FOR MY DOING THE SAME REPLIED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-76 SELF PRESERVATION IS THE FIRST LAW OF NATURE QUOTED THE SHAGGY MAN. TRUE SHE SAID READILY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-77 I WOULD LIKE TO DISCOVER A PLAN TO SAVE OURSELVES WITHOUT FIGHTING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-78 THAT SEEMED A HOPELESS TASK TO THEM BUT REALIZING THAT OZMA WAS DETERMINED NOT TO FIGHT THEY TRIED TO THINK OF SOME MEANS THAT MIGHT PROMISE ESCAPE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-79 COULDN'T WE BRIBE OUR ENEMIES BY GIVING THEM A LOT OF EMERALDS AND GOLD?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-80 ASKED JACK PUMPKINHEAD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-81 NO BECAUSE THEY BELIEVE THEY ARE ABLE TO TAKE EVERYTHING WE HAVE REPLIED THE RULER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-82 I HAVE THOUGHT OF SOMETHING SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-83 WHAT IS IT DEAR?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-84 ASKED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-85 LET US USE THE MAGIC BELT TO WISH ALL OF US IN KANSAS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-86 WE WILL PUT SOME EMERALDS IN OUR POCKETS AND CAN SELL THEM IN TOPEKA FOR ENOUGH TO PAY OFF THE MORTGAGE ON UNCLE HENRY'S FARM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-87 THEN WE CAN ALL LIVE TOGETHER AND BE HAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-88 A CLEVER IDEA!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-89 SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-90 KANSAS IS A VERY GOOD COUNTRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-91 I'VE BEEN THERE SAID THE SHAGGY MAN. THAT SEEMS TO ME AN EXCELLENT PLAN APPROVED THE TIN WOODMAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-92 NO!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-93 SAID OZMA DECIDEDLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-94 NEVER WILL I DESERT MY PEOPLE AND LEAVE THEM TO SO CRUEL A FATE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-95 I WILL USE THE MAGIC BELT TO SEND THE REST OF YOU TO KANSAS IF YOU WISH BUT IF MY BELOVED COUNTRY MUST BE DESTROYED AND MY PEOPLE ENSLAVED I WILL REMAIN AND SHARE THEIR FATE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-96 QUITE RIGHT ASSERTED THE SCARECROW SIGHING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-97 I WILL REMAIN WITH YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-98 AND SO WILL I DECLARED THE TIN WOODMAN AND THE SHAGGY MAN AND JACK PUMPKINHEAD IN TURN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-99 TIKTOK THE MACHINE MAN ALSO SAID HE INTENDED TO STAND BY OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-100 FOR SAID HE I SHOULD BE OF NO USE AT ALL IN KAN SAS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-101 FOR MY PART ANNOUNCED DOROTHY GRAVELY IF THE RULER OF OZ MUST NOT DESERT HER PEOPLE A PRINCESS OF OZ HAS NO RIGHT TO RUN AWAY EITHER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-102 I'M WILLING TO BECOME A SLAVE WITH THE REST OF YOU,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-103 SO ALL WE CAN DO WITH THE MAGIC BELT IS TO USE IT TO SEND UNCLE HENRY AND AUNT EM BACK TO KANSAS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-104 I'VE BEEN A SLAVE ALL MY LIFE AUNT EM REPLIED WITH CONSIDERABLE CHEERFULNESS AND SO HAS HENRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-105 I GUESS WE WON'T GO BACK TO KANSAS ANYWAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-106 I'D RATHER TAKE MY CHANCES WITH THE REST OF YOU.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-107 OZMA SMILED UPON THEM ALL GRATEFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-108 THERE IS NO NEED TO DESPAIR JUST YET SHE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-109 I'LL GET UP EARLY TO MORROW MORNING AND BE AT THE FORBIDDEN FOUNTAIN WHEN THE FIERCE WARRIORS BREAK THROUGH THE CRUST OF THE EARTH.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-110 I WILL SPEAK TO THEM PLEASANTLY AND PERHAPS THEY WON'T BE SO VERY BAD AFTER ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-111 WHY DO THEY CALL IT THE FORBIDDEN FOUNTAIN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-112 ASKED DOROTHY THOUGHTFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-113 DON'T YOU KNOW DEAR?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-114 RETURNED OZMA SURPRISED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-115 NO SAID DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-116 OF COURSE I'VE SEEN THE FOUNTAIN IN THE PALACE GROUNDS EVER SINCE I FIRST CAME TO OZ,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-117 AND I'VE READ THE SIGN WHICH SAYS, ALL PERSONS ARE FORBIDDEN TO DRINK AT THIS FOUNTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-118 BUT I NEVER KNEW WHY THEY WERE FORBIDDEN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-119 THE WATER SEEMS CLEAR AND SPARKLING AND IT BUBBLES UP IN A GOLDEN BASIN ALL THE TIME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-120 THAT WATER DECLARED OZMA GRAVELY IS THE MOST DANGEROUS THING IN ALL THE LAND OF OZ. IT IS THE WATER OF OBLIVION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-121 WHAT DOES THAT MEAN?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-122 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-123 WHOEVER DRINKS AT THE FORBIDDEN FOUNTAIN AT ONCE FORGETS EVERYTHING HE HAS EVER KNOWN OZMA ASSERTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-124 IT WOULDN'T BE A BAD WAY TO FORGET OUR TROUBLES SUGGESTED UNCLE HENRY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-125 THAT IS TRUE,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-126 BUT YOU WOULD FORGET EVERYTHING ELSE AND BECOME AS IGNORANT AS A BABY RETURNED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-127 DOES IT MAKE ONE CRAZY?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-128 NO,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-129 IT ONLY MAKES ONE FORGET REPLIED THE GIRL RULER.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-130 IT IS SAID THAT ONCE LONG LONG AGO A WICKED KING RULED OZ AND MADE HIMSELF AND ALL HIS PEOPLE VERY MISERABLE AND UNHAPPY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-131 SO GLINDA THE GOOD SORCERESS PLACED THIS FOUNTAIN HERE AND THE KING DRANK OF ITS WATER AND FORGOT ALL HIS WICKEDNESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-132 HIS MIND BECAME INNOCENT AND VACANT AND WHEN HE LEARNED THE THINGS OF LIFE AGAIN THEY WERE ALL GOOD THINGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-133 BUT THE PEOPLE REMEMBERED HOW WICKED THEIR KING HAD BEEN AND WERE STILL AFRAID OF HIM.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-134 THEREFORE HE MADE THEM ALL DRINK OF THE WATER OF OBLIVION AND FORGET EVERYTHING THEY HAD KNOWN SO THAT THEY BECAME AS SIMPLE AND INNOCENT AS THEIR KING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-135 AFTER THAT THEY ALL GREW WISE TOGETHER AND THEIR WISDOM WAS GOOD SO THAT PEACE AND HAPPINESS REIGNED IN THE LAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-136 BUT FOR FEAR SOME ONE MIGHT DRINK OF THE WATER AGAIN AND IN AN INSTANT FORGET ALL HE HAD LEARNED THE KING PUT THAT SIGN UPON THE FOUNTAIN WHERE IT HAS REMAINED FOR MANY CENTURIES UP TO THIS VERY DAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-137 THEY HAD ALL LISTENED INTENTLY TO OZMA'S STORY AND WHEN SHE FINISHED SPEAKING THERE WAS A LONG PERIOD OF SILENCE WHILE ALL THOUGHT UPON THE CURIOUS MAGICAL POWER OF THE WATER OF OBLIVION.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-138 FINALLY THE SCARECROW'S PAINTED FACE TOOK ON A BROAD SMILE THAT STRETCHED THE CLOTH AS FAR AS IT WOULD GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-139 HOW THANKFUL I AM HE SAID THAT I HAVE SUCH AN EXCELLENT ASSORTMENT OF BRAINS!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-140 I GAVE YOU THE BEST BRAINS I EVER MIXED DECLARED THE WIZARD WITH AN AIR OF PRIDE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-141 YOU DID INDEED!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-142 AGREED THE SCARECROW AND THEY WORK SO SPLENDIDLY THAT THEY HAVE FOUND A WAY TO SAVE OZ TO SAVE US ALL!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-143 I'M GLAD TO HEAR THAT SAID THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-144 WE NEVER NEEDED SAVING MORE THAN WE DO JUST NOW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-145 DO YOU MEAN TO SAY YOU CAN SAVE US FROM THOSE AWFUL PHANFASMS AND GROWLEYWOGS AND WHIMSIES?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-146 ASKED DOROTHY EAGERLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-147 I'M SURE OF IT MY DEAR ASSERTED THE SCARECROW STILL SMILING GENIALLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-148 TELL US HOW!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-149 CRIED THE TIN WOODMAN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-150 NOT NOW SAID THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-151 YOU MAY ALL GO TO BED AND I ADVISE YOU TO FORGET YOUR WORRIES JUST AS COMPLETELY AS IF YOU HAD DRUNK OF THE WATER OF OBLIVION IN THE FORBIDDEN FOUNTAIN.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-26-152 I'M GOING TO STAY HERE AND TELL MY PLAN TO OZMA ALONE BUT IF YOU WILL ALL BE AT THE FORBIDDEN FOUNTAIN AT DAYBREAK YOU'LL SEE HOW EASILY WE WILL SAVE THE KINGDOM WHEN OUR ENEMIES BREAK THROUGH THE CRUST OF EARTH AND COME FROM THE TUNNEL.

l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-13 I SAY WHAT I AM WOUND UP TO SAY ANSWERED TIKTOK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-14 AND YOU ARE RIGHT DECLARED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-15 I MYSELF HAVE BEEN THINKING OF THIS VERY IDEA AND IT SEEMS TO ME THERE ARE ENTIRELY TOO MANY WAYS FOR PEOPLE TO GET TO THE LAND OF OZ. WE USED TO THINK THE DEADLY DESERT THAT SURROUNDS US WAS ENOUGH PROTECTION,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-16 BUT THAT IS NO LONGER THE CASE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-17 THE WIZARD AND DOROTHY HAVE BOTH COME HERE THROUGH THE AIR AND I AM TOLD THE EARTH PEOPLE HAVE INVENTED AIRSHIPS THAT CAN FLY ANYWHERE THEY WISH THEM TO GO.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-18 WHY SOMETIMES THEY DO AND SOMETIMES THEY DON'T ASSERTED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-19 BUT IN TIME THE AIRSHIPS MAY CAUSE US TROUBLE CONTINUED OZMA FOR IF THE EARTH FOLK LEARN HOW TO MANAGE THEM WE WOULD BE OVERRUN WITH VISITORS WHO WOULD RUIN OUR LOVELY SECLUDED FAIRYLAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-20 THAT IS TRUE ENOUGH AGREED THE WIZARD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-21 ALSO THE DESERT FAILS TO PROTECT US IN OTHER WAYS OZMA WENT ON THOUGHTFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-22 JOHNNY DOOIT ONCE MADE A SAND BOAT THAT SAILED ACROSS IT AND THE NOME KING MADE A TUNNEL UNDER IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-23 SO I BELIEVE SOMETHING OUGHT TO BE DONE TO CUT US OFF FROM THE REST OF THE WORLD ENTIRELY SO THAT NO ONE IN THE FUTURE WILL EVER BE ABLE TO INTRUDE UPON US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-24 HOW WILL YOU DO THAT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-25 ASKED THE SCARECROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-26 I DO NOT KNOW,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-27 BUT IN SOME WAY I AM SURE IT CAN BE ACCOMPLISHED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-28 TO MORROW I WILL MAKE A JOURNEY TO THE CASTLE OF GLINDA THE GOOD AND ASK HER ADVICE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-29 MAY I GO WITH YOU?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-30 ASKED DOROTHY EAGERLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-31 OF COURSE MY DEAR PRINCESS,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-32 AND I ALSO INVITE ANY OF OUR FRIENDS HERE WHO WOULD LIKE TO UNDERTAKE THE JOURNEY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-33 THEY ALL DECLARED THEY WISHED TO ACCOMPANY THEIR GIRL RULER FOR THIS WAS INDEED AN IMPORTANT MISSION SINCE THE FUTURE OF THE LAND OF OZ TO A GREAT EXTENT DEPENDED UPON IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-34 SO OZMA GAVE ORDERS TO HER SERVANTS TO PREPARE FOR THE JOURNEY ON THE MORROW.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-35 THAT DAY SHE WATCHED HER MAGIC PICTURE AND WHEN IT SHOWED HER THAT ALL THE NOMES HAD RETURNED THROUGH THE TUNNEL TO THEIR UNDERGROUND CAVERNS OZMA USED THE MAGIC BELT TO CLOSE UP THE TUNNEL SO THAT THE EARTH UNDERNEATH THE DESERT SANDS BECAME AS SOLID AS IT WAS BEFORE THE NOMES BEGAN TO DIG.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-36 EARLY THE FOLLOWING MORNING A GAY CAVALCADE SET OUT TO VISIT THE FAMOUS SORCERESS GLINDA THE GOOD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-37 OZMA AND DOROTHY RODE IN A CHARIOT DRAWN BY THE COWARDLY LION AND THE HUNGRY TIGER WHILE THE SAWHORSE DREW THE RED WAGON IN WHICH RODE THE REST OF THE PARTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-38 WITH HEARTS LIGHT AND FREE FROM CARE THEY TRAVELED MERRILY ALONG THROUGH THE LOVELY AND FASCINATING LAND OF OZ AND IN GOOD SEASON REACHED THE STATELY CASTLE IN WHICH RESIDED THE SORCERESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-39 GLINDA KNEW THAT THEY WERE COMING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-40 I HAVE BEEN READING ABOUT YOU IN MY MAGIC BOOK SHE SAID AS SHE GREETED THEM IN HER GRACIOUS WAY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-41 WHAT IS YOUR MAGIC BOOK LIKE?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-42 INQUIRED AUNT EM CURIOUSLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-43 IT IS A RECORD OF EVERYTHING THAT HAPPENS REPLIED THE SORCERESS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-44 AS SOON AS AN EVENT TAKES PLACE ANYWHERE IN THE WORLD IT IS IMMEDIATELY FOUND PRINTED IN MY MAGIC BOOK.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-45 SO WHEN I READ ITS PAGES I AM WELL INFORMED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-46 DID IT TELL YOU HOW OUR ENEMIES DRANK THE WATER OF BLIVION?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-47 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-48 YES MY DEAR,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-49 IT TOLD ALL ABOUT IT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-50 AND ALSO IT TOLD ME YOU WERE ALL COMING TO MY CASTLE AND WHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-51 THEN SAID OZMA I SUPPOSE YOU KNOW WHAT IS IN MY MIND AND THAT I AM SEEKING A WAY TO PREVENT ANY ONE IN THE FUTURE FROM DISCOVERING THE LAND OF OZ. YES,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-52 I KNOW THAT.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-53 AND WHILE YOU WERE ON YOUR JOURNEY I HAVE THOUGHT OF A WAY TO ACCOMPLISH YOUR DESIRE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-54 FOR IT SEEMS TO ME UNWISE TO ALLOW TOO MANY OUTSIDE PEOPLE TO COME HERE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-55 DOROTHY WITH HER UNCLE AND AUNT HAS NOW RETURNED TO OZ TO LIVE ALWAYS AND THERE IS NO REASON WHY WE SHOULD LEAVE ANY WAY OPEN FOR OTHERS TO TRAVEL UNINVITED TO OUR FAIRYLAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-56 LET US MAKE IT IMPOSSIBLE FOR ANY ONE EVER TO COMMUNICATE WITH US IN ANY WAY AFTER THIS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-57 THEN WE MAY LIVE PEACEFULLY AND CONTENTEDLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-58 YOUR ADVICE IS WISE RETURNED OZMA.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-59 I THANK YOU GLINDA FOR YOUR PROMISE TO ASSIST ME.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-60 BUT HOW CAN YOU DO IT?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-61 ASKED DOROTHY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-62 HOW CAN YOU KEEP EVERY ONE FROM EVER FINDING OZ?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-63 BY MAKING OUR COUNTRY INVISIBLE TO ALL EYES BUT OUR OWN REPLIED THE SORCERESS SMILING.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-64 I HAVE A MAGIC CHARM POWERFUL ENOUGH TO ACCOMPLISH THAT WONDERFUL FEAT AND NOW THAT WE HAVE BEEN WARNED OF OUR DANGER BY THE NOME KING'S INVASION I BELIEVE WE MUST NOT HESITATE TO SEPARATE OURSELVES FOREVER FROM ALL THE REST OF THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-65 I AGREE WITH YOU SAID THE RULER OF OZ. WON'T IT MAKE ANY DIFFERENCE TO US?
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-66 ASKED DOROTHY DOUBTFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-67 NO MY DEAR GLINDA ANSWERED ASSURINGLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-68 WE SHALL STILL BE ABLE TO SEE EACH OTHER AND EVERYTHING IN THE LAND OF OZ. IT WON'T AFFECT US AT ALL,
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-69 BUT THOSE WHO FLY THROUGH THE AIR OVER OUR COUNTRY WILL LOOK DOWN AND SEE NOTHING AT ALL.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-70 THOSE WHO COME TO THE EDGE OF THE DESERT OR TRY TO CROSS IT WILL CATCH NO GLIMPSE OF OZ OR KNOW IN WHAT DIRECTION IT LIES.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-71 NO ONE WILL TRY TO TUNNEL TO US AGAIN BECAUSE WE CANNOT BE SEEN AND THEREFORE CANNOT BE FOUND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-72 IN OTHER WORDS THE LAND OF OZ WILL ENTIRELY DISAPPEAR FROM THE KNOWLEDGE OF THE REST OF THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-73 THAT'S ALL RIGHT SAID DOROTHY CHEERFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-74 YOU MAY MAKE OZ INVIS'BLE AS SOON AS YOU PLEASE FOR ALL I CARE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-75 IT IS ALREADY INVISIBLE GLINDA STATED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-76 I KNEW OZMA'S WISHES AND PERFORMED THE MAGIC SPELL BEFORE YOU ARRIVED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-77 OZMA SEIZED THE HAND OF THE SORCERESS AND PRESSED IT GRATEFULLY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-78 THANK YOU!
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-29-79 SHE SAID.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-01 CHAPTER THIRTY.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-02 HOW THE STORY OF OZ CAME TO AN END THE WRITER OF THESE OZ STORIES HAS RECEIVED A LITTLE NOTE FROM PRINCESS DOROTHY OF OZ WHICH FOR A TIME HAS MADE HIM FEEL RATHER DISCONCERTED.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-03 THE NOTE WAS WRITTEN ON A BROAD WHITE FEATHER FROM A STORK'S WING AND IT SAID, YOU WILL NEVER HEAR ANYTHING MORE ABOUT OZ BECAUSE WE ARE NOW CUT OFF FOREVER FROM ALL THE REST OF THE WORLD.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-04 BUT TOTO AND I WILL ALWAYS LOVE YOU AND ALL THE OTHER CHILDREN WHO LOVE US.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-05 DOROTHY GALE.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-06 THIS SEEMED TO ME TOO BAD AT FIRST FOR OZ IS A VERY INTERESTING FAIRYLAND.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-07 STILL WE HAVE NO RIGHT TO FEEL GRIEVED FOR WE HAVE HAD ENOUGH OF THE HISTORY OF THE LAND OF OZ TO FILL SIX STORY BOOKS AND FROM ITS QUAINT PEOPLE AND THEIR STRANGE ADVENTURES WE HAVE BEEN ABLE TO LEARN MANY USEFUL AND AMUSING THINGS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-08 SO GOOD LUCK TO LITTLE DOROTHY AND HER COMPANIONS.
l._frank_baum_CB-OZ-30-09 MAY THEY LIVE LONG IN THEIR INVISIBLE COUNTRY AND BE VERY HAPPY!
